## DESIGN DECISIONS (review in morning)

### FI-BEL3-B: beholder-escorts-limited — Void Scream fear rider invisible (2026-06-03T12)

- **Context:** 2026-06-03 12:20 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 1st beholder cycle. Seed 494580. TPK R6. Beholder 71/110.

  **Finding:** Void Scream fired R2 and dealt 31+32+27=90 total psychic to 3 PCs (all failed DC16 Wis). Both Bazgar and Marwen were instantly knocked to 0 HP by VS; Sabriel dropped to 17 HP and became the sole survivor from R3 onward. The **fear rider** (frightened for 1 minute) never expressed meaningfully in play: Bazgar was unconscious, Marwen was unconscious, and Sabriel's frightened condition was cleared R3 via save (22 vs DC16). VS's primary design intent per FI-149 is the fear condition that suppresses Bazgar's melee output for 2-3 rounds. This never happened because VS killed Bazgar outright.

  **Root cause:** Marwen rolled initiative 21 (highest) and used Fireball R1, dealing 13 halved damage to beholder. Bazgar then hit for 9. Beholder entered R2 at 80 HP. Void Scream waited 1 full round (correct per tactics — "be patient"), then fired R2 when all 3 PCs were within 30ft. But the 18-roll average × 3 failed PCs produced a one-shot scenario.

  **Human decision:** Should VS be DM-coached to delay until R3+ (after the Multiattack grapple sequence has engaged a PC) so the fear rider has at least 1-2 turns to express? Or is the "VS as two-turn win condition" acceptable for this overwhelming-difficulty slice? Note the distinction: in the full-beholder slice (#4), VS is meant to terrify and weaken before DR finishes; in the limited slice (#3) without DR, VS is doing the killing work instead.

  **Do not auto-fix** (DM coaching question, not a spec bug).

### FI-BEL3-C: beholder-escorts-limited — DD vs FI-125 Tentacle-pressure conflict (2026-06-03T12)

- **Context:** Same run as FI-BEL3-B. Rounds 3-5, Sabriel sole surviving PC at 17 HP cycling Lay on Hands.

  **Finding:** FI-125 specifies: "if Sabriel is < 30 HP and just used LoH on an ally, Tentacle (1 LA) at end of her turn." However, the beholder's default LA priority is Drain Divinity (3 LA) which consumes the entire legendary action budget on Sabriel's end-of-turn trigger. In this run:
  - R3: Sabriel at 17 HP, used LoH. Beholder spent 3 LA on DD (Sabriel saved). 0 LA remaining for Tentacle pressure.
  - R4: Same. Sabriel saved again.
  - R5: Sabriel failed DD, lost L2 slot. 0 LA remaining.
  - R6: No L2 slot target. Beholder correctly switched to VR+TL and killed Sabriel.

  The LoH depletion loop ran 4 full rounds (Sabriel revived Bazgar 3× before LoH hit 0). During this loop the beholder never landed HP pressure on Sabriel via Tentacle. Sabriel stayed at 17 HP throughout R3-R6 despite being the sole PC.

  **Recommendation:** Add tiebreak to beholder tactics: "If Sabriel is the sole surviving PC AND ≤ 30 HP AND her LoH pool is not yet exhausted (> 0), switch to Void Ray (2 LA) + Tentacle (1 LA) split instead of DD (3 LA). DD on a sole survivor with no slot protection is low-marginal-value; VR + TL delivers guaranteed HP pressure per turn."

  **Do not auto-fix** (tactics text change; human should approve the wording and whether it belongs in FI-125 or as a new entry).

### FI-SW25-A: shrine-wedge — low-attrition R2 victory, initiative-order variance (2026-06-03T10)

- **Context:** 2026-06-03 10:17 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 25th cycle. Seed 494578. VICTORY R2. Bazgar 34/49, Marwen 21/32, Sabriel 44/44 untouched.

  **Finding:** This is the lowest-attrition shrine-wedge outcome in 25 cycles. Root cause: Bazgar drew mid-initiative (after both STDs but before Marwen/Sabriel), used Action Surge for 4 attacks, and killed STD-1 outright before it could chain AR. Marwen's Fireball (30 fire, STD-2 FAIL) then left STD-2 at 1 HP, and Sabriel finished. STD-2 never used its stagger-held AR (died R1 before getting a second turn).

  The shrine-wedge slice has now produced outcomes across the full spectrum:
  - R2 easy wins (SW23, SW25 — Bazgar burst + Fireball decisive)
  - R3 party bloodied (SW24: Marwen DOWN; SW21: near-TPK)
  - R4 front-liner collapse (SW22: Bazgar + Sabriel DOWN, Marwen pristine)

  This variance is driven almost entirely by initiative roll. When Bazgar acts before Marwen's Fireball window, his Action Surge removes an STD before AR can chain — easy win. When STDs get two full AR uses (both PCs hit R1 + recharged STD fires again R2), the fight is punishing.

  **Human decision needed:** Is this initiative-variance range acceptable? The slice is *meant* to test resonance recharge + UF, which only matter in R3+ fights. In ~40% of cycles, the fight ends in R2 before those mechanics fire. Options: (a) reduce STD AC from 16 to 15 (no effect — Bazgar hits on 11+ either way), (b) add a 3rd STD to make burst-clearing harder, (c) accept the variance (it's thematically appropriate that an organized burst can overwhelm two derro before they chain resonance).

  **Do not auto-fix** (balance decision).

### FI-SW25-B: shrine-wedge — altar zone fire suppression 25th-cycle confirm (2026-06-03T10)

- **Context:** Same run as FI-SW25-A.

  **Finding:** 25th consecutive cycle in which Marwen's Fireball remained decisive regardless of vulnerability suppression. The altar zone correctly suppresses fire vulnerability, but the base damage (30 fire on a DC14 fail) is already lethal-or-near-lethal against 45 HP STDs without the vulnerability doubling. The mechanical suppression is spec-correct; the design question is whether it creates a meaningful puzzle at the table.

  **Observation:** The "pull-them-away to expose vulnerability" puzzle only matters if (a) players discover the vulnerability (not telegraphed by any .md narration), and (b) the encounter is long enough for positioning to matter. In R2 fights neither condition applies. In R3+ fights (SW21, SW22), the altar zone did matter (Sabriel's smite was notably weaker inside the zone).

  **Recommendation (non-breaking):** Add one line to the Altar Zone box in `shrine-touched-derro.md` (player-facing narration hook): "When a shrine-touched inside the altar zone is struck by fire or radiant, the shrine-runes briefly flare — but the light is absorbed. A perceptive character might notice the dampening (DC 14 Arcana/Religion)." This gives the DM a natural cue to telegraph the suppression without hard-coding a mechanic.

  **Do not auto-fix** (narrative change; human should approve the exact wording).

### MQ-SW25-B: multiattack roller output — combined damage labeled with primary type only (2026-06-03T10)

- **Context:** Observed in Phase B narration; same issue class as prior cycles.

  **Finding:** The multiattack roller output line "dmg 3 slashing (incl +1 necrotic extra_damage)" presents the combined total (2 slashing + 1 necrotic = 3) labeled as "slashing." A DM applying slashing resistance would reduce the full 3 points, including the 1 necrotic. The 🔚-breakdown (shown on the next lines) correctly separates the types, but the summary line invites misreading.

  **Blast radius:** This is in `scripts/dnd_roller.py` (summary-line formatting), not in the DB spec. Out of bot's modification scope.

  **Recommendation:** Change the summary line format from `dmg X slashing (incl +Y necrotic)` to `dmg X total [A slashing + B necrotic]` or similar. The fix belongs in `dnd_roller.py` around the multiattack output block. Human review and fix needed.

### FI-TP21-A: threshold-patrol — CW 0/3 used, 21st-cycle double-block structural confirm (2026-06-03T09)

- **Context:** 2026-06-03 09:18 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 21st cycle. Seed 494577. VICTORY R2.

  **Finding:** Call Weakness went unused for the 21st consecutive threshold-patrol cycle. This cycle reveals the double structural block with unusual clarity: (1) SC-1 rolled initiative 3 — dead last, after both DWs (init 22, 21) and all three PCs. The "already-acted-ally guard" (MQ-12 in the .md checklist) fires against both DWs, since they acted in init slots 22 and 21 before SC's init slot 3. (2) SC-1 is positioned 50 ft behind the DW pair, exceeding CW's 30 ft range. Either block alone would prevent CW from firing; both together make it structurally inaccessible regardless of dice. The .md thoroughly documents both guards, so there is no spec bug.

  **Human decision needed:** Two options:
  - (a) Move SC-1's patrol position to ≤25 ft behind the DW pair (removes the range block; init block may still fire if SC rolls low). Add a note to `encounters.md` or `_overview.md` specifying the patrol gap.
  - (b) Accept that CW is a "shrine/rager combo" ability, not a patrol ability. SC's role in threshold-patrol is barrage + multiattack; CW is intended to matter in the shrine-wedge and tank-wall formations. If this is the intent, no change is needed but the .md tactics could add: "In threshold-patrol setup, expect 0 CW uses; the formation spacing makes it unavailable."

  **Do not auto-fix** (changes encounter narration/positioning).

### MQ-TP21-B: threshold-patrol — SC patrol gap unspecified in encounter files (2026-06-03T09)

- **Context:** Same run.

  **Finding:** The encounter files (encounters.md, _overview.md) do not specify the SC-1 patrol distance behind the DW pair. The current simulation assumption (50 ft, based on "40–60 ft behind the front line" in the derro-shardcaller.md tactics) consistently exceeds CW's 30 ft range. If the patrol gap were 25 ft, CW would be in range and SC's low initiative would become the only block.

  **Recommendation:** Add a line to the threshold-patrol encounter note: "SC-1 patrols 25 ft behind DW-A and DW-B (within CW range)." This is the minimum change to make CW theoretically available in patrol encounters. Whether CW actually fires still depends on SC's initiative roll.

  **Low-risk, but human should confirm patrol geometry with map before updating.**

### FI-EV7-21-A: empty-void — VICTORY anomaly, beholder HP pool question (2026-06-03T08)

- **Context:** 2026-06-03 08:00 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 21st cycle. Seed 494576. VICTORY R5.

  **Finding:** First party victory in 21 empty-void cycles. Root cause was a double-low-probability outcome: DR missed 2/3 attempts (d20=6 and d20=2), and Drain Divinity was resisted 4/4 consecutive times (Sabriel Cha +3 vs DC 16 succeeds on 13+, ~40% per save; P(4 in a row) ≈ 2.6%). With both primary action economies broken, the party's burst damage (Fireball half + Scorching Ray ×2 + 2 Divine Smites + Bazgar 3/5 hits) totaled ~98 damage in 5 rounds — more than the beholder's 110 HP pool.

  **Note:** The simulation error (LoH revived disintegrated Marwen in R4 — see FIX-EV7-21-A) artificially extended the fight by ~1 round. In authentic play the fight outcome is still a likely VICTORY in R5–R6 with 2 PCs.

  **Human review question:** The beholder's 110 HP pool and +6 to-hit DR mean that on bad dice, the party can win before the beholder's action economy matters. Is this acceptable variance, or should HP be raised to 120–130 to force consistent multi-round engagement? The beholder's damage ceiling (10d8 DR, 6d10 VS, legendary VR) is very high — the vulnerability is the to-hit dependency for DR and the DD-saves for legendary actions. HP increase would deepen the fight without changing feel.

  **Human decision needed. Do not auto-fix.**

### FI-EV7-21-C: empty-void — Antireality DD-43 dead-letter vs +7 fighter (2026-06-03T08)

- **Context:** Same run.

  **Finding:** Antireality never fired in this fight. Bazgar's three hits were totals 24, 26, 22 — all above the DD-43 threshold (total ≤ AC+2 = 19). The reaction is structurally blocked against any fighter with ≥+7 to-hit because their hits tend to cluster in the 20–27 range, never in the 18–19 "worth blocking" window. Across 21 cycles, Antireality fires approximately 1-in-5 times Bazgar lands a hit — mostly useless against the primary melee threat.

  **Recommendation:** Consider relaxing DD-43 from "total ≤ AC+2" to "total ≤ AC+4" (i.e., total ≤ 21). This would let Antireality fire on hits of 18–21, which is a meaningful fraction of Bazgar's hits. Without this change the reaction is essentially a "only fires on lucky-but-barely-hits" check.

  **Human decision needed. Do not auto-fix** (changes combat feel).

### FI-SCT-20-D: shardcaller-team — CW 1/9 worst cycle, DD-SCT7-A 20th confirm (2026-06-02T21)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 21:20 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 20th cycle. Seed 494565. Victory R2.

  **Finding:** Only 1 of 9 total CW charges fired this run: SC-B granted CW to SC-C (correct per stagger), but SC-C died before acting (killed by Sabriel's smite in R1 initiative tie). SC-A held 3 charges correctly (would have been wasted on Barrage-firing ally per MQ-64). SC-B had 1 more opportunity in R2 but TR blocked it (bonus-action conflict). 8/9 charges went unused. Across 20 cycles, the pattern is consistent: CW is a 3/day resource that fires 0–3 times total per encounter, average ~2, with many cycles seeing 0–1 actual effect (CW on dead/dying ally, CW on barrage-firing ally correctly held, CW on already-acted ally). The ability's 3/day limit implies it should matter across an encounter, but structurally it never matters that much.

  **Recommendation (escalated from 18th cycle):** Reduce to **1/encounter** (not 3/day). A single high-value CW in the fight's most dangerous round is more thematically correct than 3 charges that mostly misfire or go unused. Alternatively: change to "bonus action + no daily limit" but "once per PC per round" — this would let SCs cycle it freely and increase actual effect without power-spiking.

  **Human decision needed. Do not auto-fix.**

### FI-SCT-20-B: shardcaller-team — Fireball R1-decisive 20th cycle confirm (2026-06-02T21)

- **Context:** Same run as FI-SCT-20-D.

  **Finding:** For the 3rd+ consecutive shardcaller-team cycle, Marwen (init 22, acts first) fires Fireball before any SC acts, crippling all three. In this run: SC-A and SC-C at 3 HP, SC-B at 18 HP. Both sub-10-HP SCs died in R1 without taking a meaningful action. The 3-SC cluster formation is structurally fragile against early-initiative AoE — three targets within a 20-ft radius is an inevitable Fireball cluster.

  **Recommendation:** Two options: (a) add staging note that SCs should not cluster within 20 ft — spread at ≥25 ft apart to deny the simultaneous Fireball. This is a DM staging fix, not a spec fix. (b) Give one SC a reaction or minor defensive ability (e.g., Uncanny Dodge vs one designated AoE per long rest). Option (a) is the lower-lift fix. Add to shardcaller .md under Position: *"Against unknown parties: start spread ≥25 ft apart to deny a single Fireball from hitting all three."*

  **Can be auto-fixed in .md (tactics note only, no balance change). Will fix in this fire.**

### MQ-SCT-20-A: shardcaller-team — initiative tie SC Dex+2 should beat Bazgar/Sabriel (2026-06-02T21)

- **Context:** Same run as FI-SCT-20-D.

  **Finding:** On a 3-way tie at init 5 between Bazgar (Dex -1), Sabriel (Dex +0), and SC-C (Dex +2), 5e rules break ties by Dex modifier — SC-C (+2) acts before Sabriel (+0) before Bazgar (-1). Auth order: SC-C fires (Barrage blocked by stagger, Multiattack vs Marwen), then Sabriel kills SC-C. Sim harness incorrectly ran Bazgar and Sabriel before SC-C. In this run, the auth order gives SC-C one turn of output vs Marwen before dying. 2× Shard-Throw +4 vs AC15: expect ~7 additional piercing on Marwen (from 16/32 → ~9/32 before Sabriel kills SC-C). Party still wins R1-R2, but Marwen is lower.

  **Recommendation:** Add to shardcaller .md: *"Initiative ties: SC Dex +2 typically beats level-5 party members unless they have DEX 14+ (Marwen Dex ~14, tie). On ties, SC acts before Str-heavy PCs."*

  **Auto-fixable (.md coaching note). Will fix in this fire.**

### FI-SRR10-C: solo-rager-rush — Bazgar 1v1 endgame anticlimactic (10th cycle, 2026-06-02T20) solo-rager-rush — Bazgar 1v1 endgame anticlimactic (10th cycle, 2026-06-02T20)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 20:19 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 10th cycle. Seed 494564. Victory R6.

  **Finding:** After Marwen went down R2 and Sabriel went down R3, Bazgar soloed R3 (27/52 HP) through Rounds 4–6. Each round was symmetric chip damage: Bazgar dealing 8–12/round, R3 dealing 6–13/round. Neither was in danger of dying quickly. The encounter ended without drama. The rager's only escalation mechanism (Madness Endurance) provides +1 to attack rolls, which is insufficient to create a "desperate last stand" feel. Berserk requires 2+ enemies in reach and can't fire in a 1v1.

  **Recommendation:** Add a tactics coaching note to derro-rager.md: *"If all allies are dead and only one PC remains: fight to 0 HP per existing text. The 1v1 endgame is a grind by design — the rager's Madness Endurance keeps it competitive but doesn't spike. If the DM wants a more dramatic close, narrate the rager's increasing frenzy but mechanically it just swings until it drops."* This frames the grind as intentional, not a gap.

  **Do not auto-fix balance:** The grind is lore-consistent. Low priority.

### FI-SRR10-D: solo-rager-rush — Taunt DC 12 structurally inert (10th-cycle confirm)

- **Context:** Same run as FI-SRR10-C. 10 cycles of solo-rager-rush data.

  **Finding:** In this run, Taunt generated zero mechanical effect: Bazgar's failed save (vs R1's Taunt) was irrelevant because he was targeting R1 directly; Marwen passed her save; Sabriel failed but went down before making a taunted attack. Across 10 cycles of solo-rager-rush: Taunt's DC 12 is low vs party Cha saves (Bazgar +0, Marwen +1, Sabriel +2). On average ~40% pass rate. Even when it lands, the effect requires the taunted PC to both stay alive AND choose to attack a non-taunting creature — two conditions that frequently don't coexist.

  **Recommendation:** Consider raising Taunt DC to 13. This would shift the Marwen pass rate from ~45% to ~30% and Sabriel's from ~50% to ~40%. Alternatively, add a coaching note that Taunt is most impactful when it forces a caster off a key action — e.g., preventing Fireball requires the wizard to target non-taunting creatures — but since Fireball is a save-based spell unaffected by Taunt, this coaching is already in the .md (FI-31). The root issue is the save DC is borderline too low for level-5 PCs.

  **Human decision needed:** Raising the DC changes balance. Do not auto-fix.

### SIM-SRR10-A: Taunt re-targeting after primary split-target drops — coaching note gap in derro-rager.md

- **Context:** Same run as FI-SRR10-C. When Marwen went down R2, R2's Taunt target expired. Both Bazgar and Sabriel were alive. Simulation skipped R2's Taunt entirely (harness bug), but the .md gives no guidance on reassignment.

  **Finding:** The FI-31 rager-only corollary says "split Taunt across multiple PCs (one rager per target)" but doesn't specify what to do when a split-target drops. MQ-NEW-2 says to skip unconscious/dead targets. These two rules together imply redirect, but to whom? If R2 redirects to Bazgar (who is already taunted by R1), the FI-31 "no stacking" intent is violated. If R2 redirects to Sabriel (R3's assigned target), same problem. If R2 skips, MQ-NEW-2 says "skip entirely" — but that wastes the bonus action.

  **Recommendation:** Add to derro-rager.md Tactics under Taunt: *"If your assigned split-target drops unconscious or dies, redirect Taunt to any living PC not already taunted this round. If all living PCs are already taunted by other ragers this round, skip Taunt per MQ-NEW-2."* This preserves FI-31 while giving clear redirect guidance.

  **Auto-fixable:** This is a tactics coaching note, not a spec error. Can be added to derro-rager.md. **Will add in this fire if human approves; flagging here first since it touches the .md authoring scope.**

### FI-BEL27-A: beholder-escorts-limited — DD at full HP wastes temp HP (27th cycle, 2026-06-02T18)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 18:26 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 27th cycle. Seed 494562. Init: TA(20)→Sabriel(19)→Marwen(17)→beholder(14)=Bazgar(14)→TC(13)→TB(7). TPK R1.

  **Finding:** Drain Divinity (3 LA) fired on Sabriel at the end of her turn. Sabriel failed her Cha save (sv 10 vs DC 16), losing her L3 slot. The beholder gained +6 temp HP (2× slot level). However, beholder was at 110/110 (full HP, no damage taken yet). Temp HP is wasted when at max HP — the slot drain is the only benefit gained. The tactics say "burn LA on DD when clerics/paladins present" but don't note the HP threshold condition. Against a party that opens with burst damage (Fireball, smites), beholder frequently takes damage in R1 before its turn; in this cycle, it went 4th in init so it was undamaged when the LA fired at end-of-Sabriel's-turn.

  **Recommendation:** Add coaching note to beholder.md Tactics under DD priority: *"If beholder is at full HP and the party's total output this round is likely ≤20 dmg (no Fireball yet, no smite hit), DD temp HP will be wasted — the slot drain alone is still valuable. If beholder is already below 100 HP, DD temp HP actively matters. Prioritize DD regardless of HP state when L2+ slots remain, but note the waste at HP cap."*

  **Do not auto-fix:** This is a tactics coaching gap, not a spec error.

### MQ-BEL27-A: VS start-state for slice #3 — 27th-cycle confirmation (MQ-BEL25-B ongoing)

- **Context:** Same run as FI-BEL27-A. VS fired in R1 again — 4th consecutive slice-3 cycle (cycles 24, 25, 26, 27) with VS available at start.

  **Finding:** The cron-prompt slice #3 description says "NO disintegration ray yet" but says nothing about VS. All 27 slice-3 runs have implicitly started with VS available (fresh encounter, no prior use). MQ-BEL25-B first flagged this. The implicit assumption is correct (VS starts available at encounter start — a fresh beholder hasn't fired it), but it should be explicit in the slice definition so the harness doesn't accidentally vary this assumption.

  **Recommendation:** Update cron-prompt slice #3 description to: *"1× beholder-thrulm (NO disintegration ray yet; VS starts AVAILABLE — fresh encounter) + 3× thrall-derro."* Do NOT auto-fix the cron-prompt (human authoring file). Flag for morning review.

### MQ-BEL27-B: Initiative tie at init-20 — creature-vs-lair priority undocumented in beholder.md

- **Context:** Same run as FI-BEL27-A. TA rolled initiative 20 (tying with the lair-action count). Simulation fired lair before TA — incorrect. Lair fires at init 20 "losing ties."

  **Finding:** The beholder.md lair action note states "lair actions trigger on init count 20, LOSING TIES" but doesn't give an example of a creature that also rolled 20. At table, a DM might not immediately catch the tie. The .md is technically correct but silent on the example. In this run, TA's attack was a miss anyway, but the precedent matters.

  **Recommendation:** Add to beholder.md lair action note: *"Example: if a thrall or PC rolls init 20, that creature acts before the lair fires. The lair yields to any creature at exactly init count 20."*

  **Low priority:** Can be added next .md authoring session; no combat outcome impact in this cycle.

### MQ-TW26-A: tank-wall — CW range root cause is positioning, not initiative (26th cycle, 2026-06-02T17)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 17:21 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 26th cycle. Seed 494561. Init: Sabriel(20)→SC(16)→Rager(15)→Marwen(10)→Bazgar(9). VICTORY R2. 0 bugs auto-fixed. Phase A 29/29 clean, 94th consecutive.

  **New finding:** This cycle had the init window open (SC 16 > Rager 15), but CW was still unreachable. Root cause: SC starts 50 ft from party entry point; Rager starts 10 ft from party. SC-to-Rager distance = ~40 ft, which exceeds CW's 30 ft range. Initiative order is irrelevant — even when SC acts before Rager, CW cannot reach Rager at standard starting positions. Prior cycles attributed lockout to "SC acts after Rager in init" — this is a secondary cause. The primary cause is **starting distance**.

  **Recommendation:** Either (a) reduce SC's default starting distance to 30–35 ft from party (i.e., ≤30 ft from Rager) so CW is in range R1, or (b) raise CW range from 30 ft to 60 ft. Option (a) has the side effect of making SC more vulnerable to melee front-loading; option (b) makes CW a more prominent encounter feature. Human design call — do NOT auto-fix. Cross-ref DD-41, DD-TW-19-1, FI-TW20-A (20+ cycles of CW lockout).

### MQ-TW26-B: tank-wall — Taunt-vs-save-caster coaching gap (26th cycle, 2026-06-02T17)

- **Context:** Same run as MQ-TW26-A above.

  **Finding:** Rager's Taunt bonus action targets the "squishiest non-engaged target (caster or rogue)" per .md tactics. In this cycle, that was Marwen. Marwen failed her Cha save (11 vs DC 12), granting her disadvantage on attacks vs non-Rager targets. However, Marwen's entire combat contribution was Fireball (DC 15 Dex save — unaffected by Taunt per FI-31). Taunt consumed the bonus action slot and produced zero effect. 26th-cycle confirm of FI-31.

  **Recommendation:** Add to Rager's Taunt tactic bullet: *"Exception: if the caster's primary weapon is a save-based AOE (Fireball, Shatter, Thunder Wave), Taunt targeting them is mechanically null — redirect to the fighter or martial who uses attack rolls instead (Bazgar). Taunt's disadvantage applies only to attack rolls, not saving throws."* Low-risk coaching note, no spec change.

### FI-NEW-EV7-A/B + MQ-EV7-A/B: empty-void 1st-cycle — DR disintegrates before initiative; DD monopolizes solo LA; DR mechanic undocumented (2026-06-02T14)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 14:21 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 1st cycle. Seed 494558. Initiative: Beholder(25) → Sabriel(16) → Bazgar(11). Marwen disintegrated in surprise round. Outcome: TPK R4. Beholder 48/110. LR 3/3 unused. 1 bug auto-fixed (FIX-EV7-A DR mechanic note in .md checklist). Phase A 29/29 clean, 91st consecutive.

  **FI-NEW-EV7-A — DR disintegrates Marwen before initiative in surprise round:** DR is a to-hit attack (+6 to hit, 10d8 force, no save). vs Marwen AC 15 = 60% hit rate. Full 10d8 averages 44.5 force — any hit kills Marwen (32 HP). In this run, DR hit (22 vs AC 15) in the surprise round and disintegrated Marwen before she rolled initiative. One player watches their character die permanently before their first action. beholder-thrulm.md covers the LoH-after-DR ruling but not the "disintegrated before initiative" communication moment. **Recommendation:** Add to tactics surprise-round guidance: *"If DR disintegrates a PC in the surprise round (before that PC has acted), communicate the outcome immediately — name the mechanic (DR to-hit attack, no save, permanent death at 0 HP), and let the player choose how to narrate their character's final moment before the fight resolves. Do not proceed silently."*

  **FI-NEW-EV7-B — Drain Divinity monopolizes LA in solo fights:** 3 of 3 LA budgets consumed by Drain Divinity (one per round, 3 LA each). Sabriel's CHA save (+3 vs DC 16 ≈ 35% pass rate) passed twice — 2 of 3 DD rounds contributed nothing. In a solo beholder fight, the LA pattern is: one DD per budget cycle, either a significant drain or a complete blank. No split-budget options (Void Ray 2 + Tentacle 1) are exercised unless DD fails. The monotone pattern makes legendary actions feel binary rather than tactical. **Recommendation:** Add to legendary priority rule: *"After DD has failed (target saved) twice in a row against the same target, skip it — switch to Void Ray (2 LA) + Tentacle Lash (1 LA) for one round. The beholder reads the odds and pivots. Resume DD if a different slot-holder becomes targetable."*

  **MQ-EV7-A — DR to-hit vs standard 5e Dex save:** DB spec uses `single_attack` with `to_hit_bonus: 6` for DR (attack roll, no save). Standard 5e beholder DR is DC 16 Dex save. The design choice (attack roll) makes DR ~60% vs Marwen AC 15 vs ~70% fail-rate on a Dex save — slightly less lethal but more predictable. beholder-thrulm.md's checklist never stated the mechanic. **Fix applied this fire (FIX-EV7-A):** Added "DR is a ranged ATTACK ROLL (+6 to hit), NOT a Dex saving throw — full 10d8 force on hit, no half-damage" to start-of-turn checklist item 1. No DB change needed.

  **MQ-EV7-B — Sim methodology: parallel dice vs DB output:** The playtest sim dispatches DB calls for narrative but uses Python `random` rolls to track HP outcomes. These diverge (DB's DR to-hit 13 in R1 was a miss vs Marwen AC 15, but sim applied damage from its own rolls). Qualitative findings are sound (TPK confirmed), but per-round HP numbers are approximations. Future sim iterations should parse the DB's to-hit from the output string and compare to target AC before applying sim damage. Low priority.

### FI-SCT-19-A: shardcaller-team 19th-cycle — CW double-grant hold-clause missing (2026-06-02T13)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 13:21 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 19th cycle. Seed 494557. Initiative: Bazgar(17) → SC-B(14) → SC-A(11) → Sabriel(8) → Marwen(6) → SC-C(3). Outcome: VICTORY R2. Bazgar 37/49, Marwen 16/32 (2 L3 slots spent on dual Fireballs), Sabriel 44/44 untouched. CW charges used: 2 of 9 (both wasted). 0 bugs auto-fixed. Phase A 29/29 clean, 90th consecutive.

  **FI-SCT-19-A (new) — CW double-grant: missing hold-rule when only one future actor exists:** SC-B (init 14) correctly CW'd SC-C (init 3 — only future actor, HP 33 > 20). SC-A (init 11) then also CW'd SC-C, since no other eligible future actor existed. Two CW charges consumed; advantage is not stackable per checklist item 4 ("Toggle, not stackable") — the second grant was pure waste. The checklist rule "don't double-buff the same ally" has no fallback clause for the scenario where only one future actor exists and it already has CW. SC-C then missed both throws (adv 9,9 → 13; +4 → 8 vs AC 15). **Recommendation:** Add to CW checklist after "don't double-buff the same ally": *"If the only eligible future actor already has CW advantage this turn, hold the charge — advantage is already set, re-granting is wasted. Use the bonus action for Tactical Retreat if threatened, or carry the charge to the next round when a different ally may be alive and eligible."*

### FI-SR9-A/B + SIM-SR9-A: solo-rager-rush 9th-cycle — Sabriel AC19 invulnerable; Berserk column gap; Taunt tracking burden (2026-06-02T12)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 12:16 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 9th cycle. Seed 494556. Initiative: R2(20)→R1(19)→R3(17)→Bazgar(14)→Sabriel(13)→Marwen(11). Outcome: VICTORY R8 — Sabriel 44/44 untouched (both Bazgar/Marwen down). 0 bugs auto-fixed. Phase A 29/29 clean, 89th consecutive.

  **FI-SR9-A (NEW) — Sabriel AC19 functionally invulnerable to rager multiattack:** Rager +4 vs AC19 = 30% hit rate unmodified, ~35% with Madness Endurance. R3 spent 4 rounds vs Sabriel in a 1v1 after Bazgar fell — landed 1 of 8 attacks. In rager-only encounters, once the squishy PCs (Marwen, Bazgar) are down, the last rager is often stuck in a slow-death loop against Sabriel. The .md has no coaching about high-AC PC matchups. **Recommendation:** Add to rager tactics: *"Against AC17+ targets, Taunt's disadvantage-on-others clause is your highest-value bonus action — if the rager is in a 1v1 against an armored PC, Taunt still fires to deny any potential allied-NPC attack benefits, and may compound a fear/prone condition already active. The rager doesn't retreat; but if AC17+ is the only target, Berserk all-in is correct."*

  **FI-SR9-B (MQ-SR8-C 9th-cycle confirm) — Berserk column geometry:** R3 never met the 2+ PCs in reach condition for all 8 rounds. Column/alcove approach geometry routes the 3rd rager to a single-file gap → 1 PC in reach → Berserk permanently unavailable. 9 cycles confirm this as a structural pattern. **Recommendation:** Add .md note: *"In tight corridors or column-alcove formations, the flanking rager typically reaches only 1 PC. Berserk eligibility for that rager is near-zero — Multiattack + Taunt is correct. The Berserk ability pays off primarily when the ragers converge in an open chamber (e.g. the main vault)."*

  **SIM-SR9-A (MQ-SR8-A 9th confirm) — Taunt tracking burden:** Sabriel was taunted 6 of 8 rounds but sim did not enforce disadvantage on her attacks vs non-taunting ragers. The single-turn duration requires the DM to mark affected PCs each round. **Recommendation:** Add DM shorthand to .md checklist: *"Taunt tracking: place a chip/token on the taunted PC's miniature each time they fail the save. Remove it at the end of their next turn. Their attacks against any creature except the taunting rager are at disadvantage while marked."*

### FI-TP0-A/B/C + MQ-TP0-B: threshold-patrol 20th-cycle — Fireball 1-round wipe; CW invisible; SC retreat boundary; Fireball geometry (2026-06-02T15)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 15:19 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 20th cycle. Seed 494559. Initiative: Bazgar(17) → DW-A(12) → DW-B(11) → Sabriel(8) → SC(5) → Marwen(5). Outcome: VICTORY R1. Bazgar 40/49, Marwen 32/32 (never targeted), Sabriel 38/44. CW 3/3 unused. 0 bugs auto-fixed. Phase A 29/29 clean, 92nd consecutive. Fireball 35 fire, all three NPCs failed DC 14 save.

  **FI-TP0-A (20th-cycle pattern confirm) — Patrol too fragile vs L5 Fireball:** All three patrol NPCs (27-33 HP, Dex +2) die in R1 if Marwen gets late-to-mid initiative and targets them before the SC can act. Even at average Fireball (8d6≈28), DW-A at 14 HP post-Bazgar-hit and DW-B at 27 HP and SC at 12 HP post-Sabriel-smite all die to full-fail damage. The patrol has no Fireball mitigation: no resistance, no scatter geometry, no cover. This is the 20th consecutive threshold-patrol cycle; the Fireball-wipe resolution has occurred in most of them. **Recommendation (log for human):** Add terrain complexity to force geometry: e.g., the SC starts around a corner (out of Fireball range unless Marwen moves into melee threat), or one DW is in a side alcove. Alternatively, bump DW HP to 35 (d8+4 HD, removes the "already-injured DW dies to half-damage" path).

  **FI-TP0-B (structural confirm) — CW mechanic entirely invisible in short fights:** SC went last in initiative (rolled 5, tied with Marwen). By the time SC acted, it had already taken 21 damage from Sabriel and was on the retreat threshold — Barrage was the only viable action. CW charges (3/3) were never spent. In all 20 threshold-patrol cycles, CW has been mechanically demonstrated in only 3 (the 23rd, 3rd, and 1st cycles — in the 3rd it was collected but inconsequential). CW requires ≥2 rounds to showcase. **Recommendation:** The patrol slice needs structural durability (see FI-TP0-A) as the prerequisite for CW ever mattering. Alternatively, add thrall-derro to the slice composition as HP padding without complicating the patrol's tactical identity.

  **FI-TP0-C — SC at exactly "below 12 HP" retreat boundary post-Sabriel smite:** After Sabriel's two attacks in R1 (21 total damage), SC was at exactly 12/33 HP. The .md retreat trigger is "Below 12 HP." The boundary is inclusive-exclusive ambiguous — 12 HP means the trigger does NOT fire (below = ≤11). SC correctly fired Barrage rather than retreating. This boundary is consistently reached by a R1 Sabriel smite. **Recommendation:** Add parenthetical to the retreat trigger: *"Below 12 HP (i.e., ≤11 HP triggers retreat; exactly 12 HP does NOT — still fires Barrage from cover)."*

  **MQ-TP0-B — Fireball geometry: SC at 40 ft may be outside the blast radius:** The simulation placed all three patrol NPCs in the same Fireball (35 fire, DC 14 save) because the corridor geometry was modeled as colinear. However, if Marwen stands 10 ft from the DWs and centers the Fireball on the DWs, the SC at 40 ft back is 30 ft from the Fireball center — 10 ft outside the 20 ft blast radius. This simulation may have incorrectly included SC. **Recommendation:** Add to patrol overview: *"SC starts 40 ft behind DW-A/B (first pillar, hard cover). A Fireball centered on the DW positions does NOT reach SC. To catch SC, Marwen must aim the origin point ~20 ft ahead of the DWs (i.e., toward SC) — which risks excluding the DWs if the 20-ft radius doesn't backwash. DMs should adjudicate this explicitly at table; don't assume SC is automatically in the blast."*

### FI-FC4-A/B/C/D + MQ-FC4-A/B/C: final-confrontation 26th-cycle — killing blow source; 2-round resource bleed; VS never fires; BM Trip wasted; stagger state bug; death-save TPK edge; DD-wasted-same-kill (2026-06-02T11)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 11:23 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 26th cycle. Seed 494555. Initiative: Marwen(21) → BEHOLDER(17)=Sabriel(17) → ST-1(16) → T4(14) → T2(11) → Bazgar(7) → ST-2(6) → T1(5) → T3(3). Outcome: TPK R2. Beholder 102/110. All thralls dead R1 (Fireball 29 fire). Both STs 31/45. Marwen down to ST-1 AR R1; Bazgar down to VR R2; Sabriel at 0 HP from DR half R2. 0 bugs auto-fixed. Phase A 29/29 clean, 88th consecutive.

  **FI-FC4-A — Killing blow comes from shrine-touched, not beholder:** Marwen was killed by ST-1's Ancient Resonance (necrotic + psychic, R1) after being softened by DR half-damage. The slice-4 design goal was "see WHICH ability lands the killing blow and whether the death feels earned." The beholder's marquee kill was a SAVE result on DR. In this trajectory the beholder never lands a killing blow — a side-mob finishes the wizard. At table this may be fine (the overwhelming force of the encounter as a whole registers), but it's worth asking: should the final confrontation ensure the beholder gets direct credit for at least one kill, e.g. by having VS or a second DR available? **Recommendation:** Consider DM coaching note — "In slice-4, if DR saves on Marwen and AR threatens to steal the kill, hold the beholder's R1 legendary actions until after AR has resolved, then spend VR (2 LA) to finish."

  **FI-FC4-B — 2-round TPK with most PC resources untouched:** Sabriel's LoH (25 HP, never used), 2 L2 smite slots, and Marwen's L2×3 + L1×4 slots all survived. The party never got to mount a meaningful last stand or make resource decisions. This is structurally correct for slice-4 (overwhelming by design), but feels hollow. **Recommendation:** Add DM guidance in the slice-4 briefing: "Run this slice after the party has experienced at least one previous beholder slice (slice-3 or slice-7). Slice-4 cold is fast and one-sided. Prior exposure to DR/VS/Drain Divinity makes the TPK feel earned rather than arbitrary."

  **FI-FC4-C — Void Scream never fires in 2-round slice:** VS starts unavailable and has Recharge 6 (16.7%/round). In 2 rounds it rolled 1 then 3 — never recharged. VS's fear rider is described as the beholder's most durable tactical tool (FI-149), yet in the most extreme encounter slice it's invisible. **Recommendation:** Design decision — should slice-4 start with VS available? The briefing says "FULL" (all abilities) but doesn't specify VS start state. If VS starts available in slice-4, it can fire R1 or R2 and demonstrate the fear rider before the TPK. Currently VS is only reliably demonstrated in multi-round slices.

  **FI-FC4-D — Battlemaster Trip Attack wasted every round:** Bazgar's primary BM maneuver is immunized by MQ-82 (beholder hover). He landed 8 damage total (1 hit in 2 rounds), making his martial identity irrelevant. The tactics note this, but the player experience is: "I built around Trip Attack and the beholder is immune." **Recommendation:** Add a player-advisory sentence to the slice-4 or COMBAT-CHEAT-SHEET: "Fighter players: if using a prone/control Battlemaster build, be aware the beholder is hover-immune to prone. Precision Attack, Goading Attack, or Riposte are your useful maneuvers here."

  **MQ-FC4-A — AR stagger rule requires pre-round marking; sim violated it:** Stagger check is supposed to happen before any turns in a round. In the sim code, the check was re-evaluated at ST-2's turn (after ST-1 consumed AR), making `both_ar_alive` False and bypassing the hold. Both STs fired AR R1 as a result — double-cone necrotic was a significant contributor to the R1 Marwen kill. The spec is correct; the sim code was wrong. At real table, the DM MUST place a physical "AR-HOLD" marker on the lower-initiative shrine-touched's initiative card at the top of each round before any turns resolve. If this is forgotten, double-AR fires and likely kills a PC in round 1. No DB fix needed. **Recommendation:** Add one sentence to shrine-touched-derro.md tactics: "DM tip: at the start of each round, physically mark the lower-initiative shrine-touched as AR-hold before any turns begin — this check cannot wait until that creature's turn."

  **MQ-FC4-B — Sabriel at 0 HP from DR save: narrative TPK edge case:** A DR save reduces to half damage, which can bring a PC to exactly 0 HP without disintegration. Sabriel ended R2 at 0 HP — technically making death saves, not dead. With Bazgar down and Marwen down and no one to stabilize her, it's functionally a TPK. **Recommendation:** Add one sentence to beholder-thrulm.md lair/tactics: "Practical TPK: once all 3 PCs are at 0 HP or DOWN (regardless of disintegration state), declare combat over — do not run death save rounds with no healer and the full encounter force active."

  **MQ-FC4-C — Drain Divinity 3 LA spent on PC who dies same round:** DD was used at the end of Marwen's turn (3 LA), draining her L3 slot. Marwen was killed by ST-1's AR later in the same round. The drained slot generated +6 beholder temp HP that was immediately at-cap (beholder was full). 3 LA for +6 meaningless temp HP is a poor trade compared to VR (2 LA) + TL (1 LA) on surviving PCs. The existing DD priority rules (FI-128) don't address "target is about to die to an allied NPC this round." No auto-fix possible (requires initiative prediction), but note for DM: when ST-1 has AR available and Marwen is softened by DR, reconsider whether DD is worth 3 LA — split into VR+TL instead.

### FI-BEL26-B / MQ-BEL25-B / MQ-BEL26-A: beholder-escorts-limited — compel-wasted-same-turn-kill; VS slice-3 start-state; lair-action-no-live-PCs (2026-06-02T10)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 10:19 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 25th cycle. Seed 494554. Initiative: beholder(23) → Bazgar(21) → [lair-20] → TB(19) → TA(18) → Sabriel(10) → Marwen(9) → TC(7). Outcome: TPK R2. Beholder untouched 110/110. VS R1 decisive (Bazgar fail, Sabriel fail → 9/49 and 4/44). Phase A 29/29 clean, 87th consecutive. 1 bug auto-fixed (MQ-BEL25-A live-thrall guard).

  **FI-BEL26-B (new) — compel wasted on same-turn kill:** Beholder issued `compel_thrall` (bonus action on beholder's R2 turn) directing TB to attack Marwen. On the same beholder R2 turn, TL2-redirect killed Marwen (TL1 → Sabriel 0 HP, TL2 → Marwen 0 HP). By the time TB's turn arrived (init 19), Marwen was already down, making the compel meaningless. The MQ-BEL25-A fix (added this run) covers the *all-thralls-dead* case; this is a subtler *target-just-died-to-beholder's-own-attack* pattern. **Recommendation:** Add a coaching sentence to the compel_thrall tactics bullet: *"Prefer `shrine_drift` over `compel_thrall` on turns when the beholder's own multiattack is likely to kill all remaining PC targets — the compel command has no meaningful target by the time the thrall acts."* Human review: is this edge case worth a coaching note or is it sufficiently covered by the existing "do NOT compel toward a PC who is already focused on a thrall" language?

  **MQ-BEL25-B (25th-cycle open) — VS slice-3 start-state undocumented:** All 25 beholder-escorts-limited runs treat VS as available (recharged) at combat start. The briefing's slice description says "NO disintegration ray yet" but is silent on VS start state. In 25 cycles, VS has fired R1 in every run where it was available. **Recommendation:** Add to `combat-runner/.testbot/thrulm-cron-prompt.md` slice #3 description: *"Beholder starts with VS available (recharged); DR locked. This is by design — tests legendary economy and lair action pressure without the one-shot disintegration ace."*

  **MQ-BEL26-A (new) — lair action with no live PCs:** VE lair action fired at count 20 R2 when all PCs were already at 0 HP. No live targets for the save. The beholder .md lair action section does not address this edge case. **Recommendation:** Add one sentence: *"If all enemies are unconscious (0 HP) at count 20, skip the lair action — it has no live target."* Very low priority; no mechanical impact.

### FI-SW24-A / MQ-SW24-A / MQ-SW24-B: shrine-wedge — double-AR R2 caster-pressure 24th-cycle; Driven-Escape cone validity post-move; OBR fires between multiattack hits (2026-06-02T16)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 16:20 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 24th cycle. Seed 494560. Initiative: Bazgar(19) → STD-A(15)=Marwen(15) → STD-B(13) → Sabriel(6). Outcome: VICTORY R3. Bazgar 29/49, Marwen -2/32 DOWN, Sabriel 29/44. Resources spent: 1× Fireball L3, 1× Divine Smite, 1× Second Wind. Both STDs destroyed. 0 bugs auto-fixed. Phase A 29/29 clean, 93rd consecutive.

  **FI-SW24-A (24th-cycle caster-pressure confirm) — double-AR R2 kills Marwen again:** In R2, STD-A recharged AR (rolled 5) and fired with 3 PCs in cone (correct — per tactics, 3 targets means AR wins regardless of UF). STD-B simultaneously triggered the stagger exemption (below 20 HP after Bazgar's crit + OBR self-damage) and fired recklessly after Driven Escape. Both ARs landed on Marwen in the same round: STD-A AR 18 dmg (Marwen failed Dex save) + STD-B AR 15 dmg (Marwen failed Dex save), totalling 33 combined damage across the two rounds R1–R2. Marwen's 32 HP is insufficient to survive two failed AR saves in back-to-back rounds. This is the 24th consecutive shrine-wedge cycle confirming the structural wizard-pressure pattern. **Human note:** The pattern is functioning as designed (STDs are pressure tools), but the inevitability of wizard kill in R1–R2 under unfavorable saves may warrant a DM coaching note about positioning (Marwen off-axis from both STDs eliminates the double-cone scenario). No spec change recommended.

  **MQ-SW24-A (new) — Driven Escape cone validity after repositioning:** STD-B used Driven Escape (bonus action, 30 ft toward altar, no OA) and then fired reckless Ancient Resonance. After moving away from Bazgar, the spatial validity of the 15-ft cone vs 2+ targets is uncertain. In the simulation, both Bazgar and Sabriel remained in cone — but if the party disperses, only 1 target may be in cone post-move. The tactics say "fires AR recklessly if AR is available and 2+ targets are in cone" — the "in cone" check must be evaluated AFTER the Driven Escape movement lands, not before. **Recommendation:** Add a DM coaching note to the below-20-HP tactics bullet: *"After Driven Escape, re-evaluate cone coverage from new position before committing to reckless AR. If only 1 target is in the 15-ft cone post-move, use Multiattack instead."* Low-risk documentation note, no DB or spec change.

  **MQ-SW24-B (confirm of MQ-SW23-A) — OBR fires between multiattack hits:** In R3, Bazgar's Extra Attack hit STD-A twice (attack 1: 6+7=13 dmg, attack 2: 9 dmg, total 22). At the moment of hit 1, STD-A was at 20 HP → 7 HP (alive). OBR should have fired between hit 1 and hit 2 (reaction triggers on damage taken while alive). The simulation did not enforce this. Per 5e RAW: a reaction fires immediately after the trigger and can interrupt a sequence of attacks. If OBR fires after hit 1 (STD-A at 7 HP), it swings at Bazgar (+4 to hit), potentially landing before hit 2 kills STD-A. **Recommendation:** Add one sentence to the OBR trigger section in shrine-touched-derro.md: *"In a multiattack, OBR may fire between the first and second attack if the first hit doesn't kill — check immediately after each melee hit in a multiattack sequence."* Confirms and extends MQ-SW23-A (which addressed only the killing-blow case); together they fully specify OBR timing.

### MQ-SW23-A / DD-SW23-A / DD-SW23-B: shrine-wedge — OBR killing-blow edge case; altar-zone invisibility; OBR schema gap (2026-06-02T08)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 08:22 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 23rd cycle. Seed 494552. Initiative: STD-B(21) → Marwen(19) → STD-A(17) → Sabriel(6) → Bazgar(3). Outcome: VICTORY R2. Bazgar 14/49 critical, Marwen 17/32, Sabriel 25/44. Resources spent: 1× Fireball L3, 2× Divine Smite (L2 est.), 2× Healing Word. Both STDs destroyed. 1 bug auto-fixed (AR narration duplicate DM note removed). Phase A 29/29 clean, 85th consecutive.

  **MQ-SW23-A (new) — OBR killing-blow edge case:** In both R1 (Sabriel kills STD-A: 18 HP → -1 HP) and R2 (Sabriel kills STD-B: 6 HP → -19 HP), the killing hit did not trigger Oath-Breaking Retaliation. The OBR .md trigger says "fires immediately when the shrine-touched takes damage" but doesn't address whether a fatal hit triggers it. 5e RAW: if a hit drops a creature to 0 HP, it is incapacitated immediately and cannot use reactions. Consequently, OBR should NOT fire on a killing blow — the shrine-touched is dead before the reaction fires. The .md is currently silent on this edge case. **Recommend:** Add a note to the OBR trigger section in shrine-touched-derro.md: *"OBR does not fire if the triggering hit drops the shrine-touched to 0 HP (the creature is incapacitated before it can react)."* Low-risk documentation change only.

  **DD-SW23-A (new) — Altar-zone vulnerability suppression invisible to party:** Fire and radiant vulnerability suppression is a powerful mechanical gate that punishes the party's two highest-damage tools (Fireball, Divine Smite) without a visible in-fiction cue. Marwen's 3rd-level Fireball hit for 27/29 (normal) instead of 54/58 (doubled). Sabriel's two smites each lost ~8 expected radiant damage. The first Fireball lands and "feels weak" without explanation. A DM running this encounter for a real table should consider whether to pre-announce the suppression (as a Perception/Arcana check on first approach, or a visible aura around the altar) or reveal it naturally through play. Current .md has the Altar Zone box in the STD sheet (visible to the DM), but nothing in the chamber description or _overview.md. **Recommend:** Add a DM-coaching line to `_overview.md` Altar section or COMBAT-CHEAT-SHEET.md: *"Shrine ambient power: Altar Zone suppresses fire/radiant vulnerability (any shrine-touched within 60 ft takes normal damage from both types). PCs discover this when Fireball or Smite deals unexpectedly normal damage — this is intentional, not a bug."* Human decision whether to also add a visible in-world tell.

  **DD-SW23-B (new) — OBR reaction_kind:"buff" schema gap:** Oath-Breaking Retaliation is a to-hit counter-attack reaction but is stored with `reaction_kind: "buff"` to satisfy the validator (which requires `attacker_save` for `"damage"` kind, inapplicable here). This means `roll_combat_action("shrine-touched-derro", "oath_breaking_retaliation")` outputs effect text only — the DM must manually roll the +4 attack and 1d8+1 / 1d8 necrotic. The runner doesn't auto-roll OBR. A `to_hit` reaction kind (with fields: `to_hit_bonus`, `damage`, optional `self_damage`) would let OBR auto-roll. **Options:** (1) Add `reaction_kind: "to_hit"` to `scripts/combat_actions_db.py` validator and renderer — spec change + code change; (2) Keep as-is and add a DM note in the OBR .md text: *"DM must manually roll: +4 to-hit vs attacker AC; on hit 1d8+1 slashing + 1d8 necrotic; self takes 1d4 psychic regardless."* The current narration output already says this — option 2 is already effectively in place. Human decision whether a code change for option 1 is worth the effort.

  *Cross-ref:* SIM-SW23-A stagger inversion is a simulation error, not a spec bug — no action on NPC specs.

### FI-TP4-A / FI-TP4-C / MQ-TP4-A: threshold-patrol — CW 4th-lockout cycle; DW targeting-AC coaching gap; Tactical Drilling convergence ambiguity (2026-06-02T07)

- **Context:** 2026-06-02 07:18 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 4th cycle. Seed 494551. Initiative: DW-B(21) > Marwen(18) > DW-A(15) > Bazgar(13) > SC(10) > Sabriel(10). Outcome: VICTORY R2. Shatter ×2 (Marwen, 2× L2 slots) + 1 smite (Sabriel) cleared all three NPCs. Party exits at Bazgar 44/49, Marwen 26/32, Sabriel 35/44. Phase A 29/29 clean, seed 494551, 84th consecutive.

  **FI-TP4-A (4th-cycle CW lockout confirm):** Call Weakness was unused across both rounds. When both DWs roll higher initiative than the SC (DW-B 21, DW-A 15, SC 10), every DW acts before the SC in every round. In R1, DW-A dies to Bazgar's burst; DW-B is at 14 HP (≤20 guard → hold). In R2, Marwen Shatters DW-B before SC acts (DW-B dead). CW correctly held both rounds per existing rules — this is correct behavior, not a spec bug. Pattern summary across 4 cycles: CW fires in 1/4 runs (3rd cycle: deferred R2, DW-B died before SC's turn — still wasted). CW is structurally dead weight in this patrol slice. **Human recommendation:** Add a prose note to the threshold-patrol scenario description in `_overview.md` or the SC .md: *"Call Weakness is an encounter-scale ability, not guaranteed to fire in every slice. In threshold-patrol, if both DWs roll higher initiative than the SC, CW will likely not fire — this is expected and correct behavior. No action needed."* Not a spec change.

  **FI-TP4-C (new — DW vs Sabriel AC 19 target mismatch):** DW-B attacked Sabriel (AC 19) in both rounds: 4/4 attacks missed (to-hit +2 vs AC 19 = 20% per attack, missing all 4 is 41% probability — plausible but revealing). The DW .md says "focus-fire: anyone visibly casting or healing" and "target the closest melee threat" — Sabriel is a divine martial in full heavy armor, the worst target for +2 hand axes. The .md currently has no AC-priority guidance. **Recommendation:** Add to DW tactics: *"When multiple PCs are in melee range, prefer the lowest-AC target — DW hand axes (+2) are ineffective against AC 17+ without Tactical Drilling advantage. Prioritize Marwen (AC 15) or Bazgar (AC 18) over Sabriel (AC 19) when all are reachable."* Low-risk coaching note; no DB change.

  **MQ-TP4-A (new — Tactical Drilling convergence-vs-split ambiguity):** 5e Pack Tactics: a creature gets advantage when "an ally is within 5 feet of the creature it is attacking." The DW .md implies both DWs converge on the same target in R1 ("in formation: Multiattack on the closest melee threat that has an ally in reach"). But a DM reading this could split the DWs (one on Bazgar, one on Sabriel) and incorrectly assume both get Drilling because they're adjacent to each other. They do not — each DW only gets advantage if an ally is within 5 ft of *the DW's specific target*. **Recommendation:** Clarify tactic text: *"In formation, BOTH DWs attack the SAME creature — this places an ally within 5 ft of the shared target, granting Tactical Drilling advantage to both. Splitting targets in R1 means neither DW has an ally adjacent to their target → no advantage for either."* Low-risk clarification.

  *Human sign-off required before editing deep-watch-derro.md. FI-TP4-B (DW-B split-target no-Drilling: 4th-cycle confirm) is a corollary of MQ-TP4-A — same fix addresses both.*

### DD-SCT7-A / DD-SCT7-B: shardcaller-team — CW 3/day non-binding 18th-cycle; back-line clustering vulnerability (2026-06-01T20)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 20:22 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 18th cycle. Seed 494540. VICTORY R4 — Bazgar 35/49, Marwen 1/32, Sabriel 33/44. All 3 SCs eliminated.

  **DD-SCT7-A — CW 3/day limit is non-binding (18th-cycle confirm):** Across 18 shardcaller-team playtest runs, the 3/day CW limit has never been the constraining resource. In this run only 4/9 total CW charges fired across 4 rounds. The typical fight ends in R3-R4, long before charges matter. The resource gate appears on paper (3/day sounds significant) but has zero impact on any fight outcome. **Design options:** (1) Reduce to 2/day or 1/encounter to clarify the scarcity; (2) Keep at 3/day as an "unconstrained" design choice that simplifies tracking (DM never has to watch charges closely — it just always works); (3) Add a condition that limits CW more meaningfully (e.g., once per round, not per day). Human decision required — no auto-fix.

  **DD-SCT7-B — SC back-line clustering punished by area spells:** All three SCs cluster in the back line (40-60 ft from party, ~5-10 ft apart per formation tactics). Any party wizard with an area spell (Shatter, Thunderwave, Fireball) can hit both surviving SCs with one cast, as demonstrated in R3 (Shatter: both SC-B and SC-C failed Con saves, full 10 thunder each — decisive turning point). The tactics section has no spread guidance for when a spellcaster is identified. **Recommendation:** Add a bullet to SC Tactics: *"vs. identified spellcaster: spread to 20+ ft separation once area spells have been observed. Do not cluster when a wizard is alive and un-disabled."* Low-risk tactical note — no DB change needed.

### FI-SR8-A / MQ-SR8-C: solo-rager-rush — Berserk late-fire pattern 8th-cycle; spatial reach ambiguity in alcove-ambush (2026-06-01T19)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 19:16 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 8th cycle. Seed 494539. INDETERMINATE R3 (proj. VICTORY R4).

  **FI-SR8-A (8th-cycle confirm):** Berserk never fires in R1 or R2 when ragers burst from separate alcoves — by the time they consolidate into melee positions with 2+ PCs adjacent, the fight is in R3. The recharge mechanic (5–6) was never exercised because Berserk wasn't *used* until all three fired simultaneously in R3. In prior TPK cycles (FI-SRR18-D), Berserk fires R1–R2 when the party clusters. The variance is tactical geometry. **Recommendation:** Add a coaching bullet to the rager Tactics section: *"Berserk optimal R1 if ragers open within 5 ft of two PCs — position this ambush formation to make Berserk available on turn 1."* This is documentation only, no DB change.

  **MQ-SR8-C (new):** The Berserk DB spec says "One Greataxe attack vs EACH enemy creature in reach." In a split-alcove ambush (R1 left, R2 right, R3 rear), each rager is physically separated. Does R1 (from left alcove) have all three PCs in reach at initiative start? The .md doesn't specify spatial assumptions for the alcove-ambush formation. The DM might legitimately rule that R1 only has Bazgar in reach (5 ft corridor), making Berserk a single-attack wasted as a recharge-cost action. **Recommendation:** Add a sentence to the Berserk prereq description in the rager .md: *"'In reach' means within this rager's melee range at the moment of its turn — PCs in other corridors are not in reach even if visible."* This prevents Berserk from accidentally becoming a 3-target sweep when only 1 target is adjacent.

  **Human sign-off required** before editing derro-rager.md or DB.

### FI-FC25-B / MQ-FC25-A / MQ-FC25-B: final-confrontation — disintegration-announcement gap; compel_thrall all-melee case; void_eruption dice gap (2026-06-01T18)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 18:22 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 25th cycle. Seed 494538. Initiative: Beholder(28) → T1(20) → T3/STD-B(19) → Bazgar(15) → T4(14) → T2(11) → STD-A(9) → Sabriel(6) → Marwen(4). Outcome: TPK R2. DR disintegrated Marwen R1 (22 vs AC15, 50 force); VS wiped Bazgar + Sabriel R2 (32 psychic, all fail). Auth party output ~26 HP to beholder; beholder at 84/110 at TPK. SIM-FC25-B: sim incorrectly allowed LoH on disintegrated Marwen; auth Fireball did not fire; all 4 thralls missed R1 auth (dispatch to-hits 17/4/9/7 vs AC18).

  **FI-FC25-B (NEW) — disintegration-announcement gap:** When Marwen is disintegrated at beholder init 28 before she acts (init 4), the table's first impulse is for Sabriel to use Lay on Hands on her. The .md prohibits this ("no body to touch") but the prohibition is embedded in a paragraph under Chamber Hazards, not in the Tactics section. In 25 final-confrontation cycles, disintegration now happens in the overwhelming majority (Marwen always has lowest init in the party; beholder rolls d20+8). The DM should pre-announce the disintegration rule before the fight begins. Recommend: add a callout box at the top of the beholder-thrulm.md Tactics section: `> **⚠️ PRE-FIGHT DM NOTE:** Disintegration Ray reduces a creature to 0 HP → dust. Lay on Hands requires touch — disintegrated targets cannot be revived. Announce this before Round 1. At this party level, expect Marwen to be the target and to die before acting.` Low-risk documentation change.

  **MQ-FC25-A (NEW) — compel_thrall value collapses in all-melee case:** With Marwen disintegrated R1, all remaining PCs are melee/high-AC. .md says "directing thralls at the divine martial is a near-wasted command." With the caster gone, both viable targets (Bazgar AC18, Sabriel AC19) have hit rates of ~25–30% for the thralls (+4 to-hit). Beholder .md step-4 says "aim at lowest-AC PC (typically Marwen, AC 15)" — but Marwen is dust. There is no guidance for the all-melee-PC case. Recommend: add note "if primary caster (Marwen) is out of combat, skip compel_thrall — use shrine_drift instead to maintain altitude and reposition out of melee reach." Low-risk, only changes bonus-action choice in an already-won fight.

  **MQ-FC25-B (NEW) — void_eruption damage dice not in .md lair section:** DB spec is 2d10 force (avg 11). The .md lair-actions entry describes VE as dealing force damage but doesn't list dice. A DM running without the dispatcher needs to look up the DB spec mid-fight. Low-risk: add "(2d10 force, DC 16 Dex half)" to the .md lair actions bullet for void_eruption.

  *Cross-ref:* MQ-FC25-C confirms MQ-BEL25-A (compel_thrall live-thrall guard, no change since MQ-BEL25-A filed 17:14 UTC). FI-FC25-D is 25th cycle confirm of FI-FC16-C/FI-FC24-A (VS-R2 kill-shot structural pattern — no new action needed beyond prior DESIGN DECISIONS).

### MQ-BEL25-A / MQ-BEL25-B / FI-BEL25-B: beholder-escorts-limited — compel_thrall dead-thrall gap; slice-3 VS start-state undocumented; lair-finisher 24th-cycle confirm (2026-06-01T17)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 17:14 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 24th cycle. Seed 494537. Initiative: TB(20) → TC(13) → TA(11) → beholder(10) → Bazgar(6) → Marwen(5) → Sabriel(4). Outcome: TPK R3. VS fired R1 (started recharged), Sabriel frightened + 34 psychic. Party output ~52 HP auth to beholder before dying. No DR used.

  **MQ-BEL25-A — compel_thrall live-thrall guard missing:** The beholder-thrulm.md step-4 checklist lists "shrine_drift OR compel_thrall" as bonus action options but doesn't state that `compel_thrall` requires a living charmed thrall in range. When all thralls die (e.g., Fireball R1), the DM has no explicit cue to switch to shrine_drift. Recommend: add parenthetical to step 4: *(compel_thrall requires a living thrall in range; if none, use shrine_drift instead)*.

  **MQ-BEL25-B — slice #3 VS start-state undocumented:** Briefing says "NO disintegration ray yet" for slice #3 but is silent on Void Scream availability. Sim assumed VS starts recharged (it fired R1 for 36 psychic, frightening Sabriel to 10/44). If VS was intended to also start unavailable, the slice plays dramatically differently — beholder can only multiattack R1, giving the party a full-damage opening round. Recommend documenting explicit VS start state (recharged / unavailable) per-slice in thrulm-rotation.json.

  **FI-BEL25-B — lair init-20 finisher pattern, 24th-cycle beholder confirm:** VE at init 20 R2 killed Sabriel (10 HP → 0 via 13 force), R3 killed Marwen (2-7 HP → 0 via 11 force). Pattern: any PC ending a round below ~14 HP near the altar dies to the next init-20 lair action before they can act again. This is mechanically sound but may frustrate players who have no stated option to exit the blast zone. No .md coaching note currently tells the DM "injured PCs should move 20+ ft from altar to avoid lair execution." Recommend adding a DM-coaching line to the beholder tactics section or the _overview.md's lair-action description.

### FI-TW24-A / FI-TW24-C / MQ-TW24-A: tank-wall — CW init-dependency 24th-cycle confirm; Taunt misses fast-init casters; SC starting distance question (2026-06-01T16)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 16:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 24th cycle. Seed 494536. Initiative: Marwen(20) → Rager(19) → Sabriel(12) → SC(12) → Bazgar(6). Outcome: VICTORY R3.

  **FI-TW24-A — CW range-locked, 24th-cycle confirm (counter-example to TW23 first-ever collection):** Rager init 19 > SC init 12 → Rager charged to melee before SC acted. SC-to-Rager gap: ~55 ft throughout. CW's 30-ft range exceeded from turn 1 — all 3 charges unused. TW23 was the *only* cycle (of 24) where CW fired on the Rager, and that required SC init 19 > Rager init 11 creating a clean window before the charge. With uniform d20, that window is ~50% of cycles. The DD-41 range note in the .md documents this correctly; the issue is whether ~50% CW utility is acceptable for the slice's "tests CW+Taunt pairing" description.

  **MQ-TW24-A — SC starting distance:** Current layout: Rager 20 ft from party, SC 60 ft (40 ft behind Rager). CW fires only when SC acts before Rager charges (init window). If SC started at 35–40 ft from party (15–20 ft behind Rager), CW would remain in range even after the Rager charges to melee (gap ≤ 30 ft). Recommend: test with SC starting at 40 ft. Trade-off: SC becomes easier for PCs to close on. Human review needed.

  **FI-TW24-C — Taunt initiative-dependency:** When caster acts before Rager (Marwen init 20 > Rager 19 this cycle), Taunt fires *after* the caster has already spent her best action. R1 Taunt was irrelevant (Sleet Storm already cast). The .md note already says "save-based-spell wizard is functionally immune," but this cycle adds: *even attack-roll-spell casters are unaffected if they act before the Rager fires Taunt.* No fix to spec — this is inherent to init ordering. Coaching note candidate: "If caster acts before Rager in init, Rager should prioritize frontliner on R1 to guarantee Taunt pressure on R2 before caster acts again."

  **Options for human review on MQ-TW24-A:**
  1. Reduce SC starting distance to 40 ft — CW stays in range when Rager charges to 5 ft (gap = 35 ft ≤ 30 ft... actually still out by 5). Reduce to 30 ft? Gap would be ~25 ft — CW fires. Risk: SC easier to reach.
  2. Accept current layout — DD-41 note explains the mechanics, ~50% fire rate is fine for CR 2 vs level 5.
  3. Extend CW range to 60 ft — lets the back-line coordinator function across the vault. This is a spec change requiring `combat_action_upsert`.

### FI-TP-3-A / MQ-TP-3-A: threshold-patrol — CW inconsequential 3rd-cycle; DW-B R1 melee-gap coaching note (2026-06-01T14)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 14:18 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 3rd cycle. Seed 494534. Initiative: Marwen(22) → DW-A(19) → Bazgar(10) → DW-B(7) → Sabriel(5) → SC(5). Outcome: VICTORY R2.

  **FI-TP-3-A — CW advantage collected R2 but inconsequential (3rd-cycle confirm):** SC fired CW on DW-B (already-acted, HP 27 > 20 — MQ-12 guard not triggered). DW-B collected advantage R2 atk 1: rolled [14, ?]+2=16 vs AC 15 — a hit without advantage anyway. CW did not flip a miss to a hit; outcome unchanged. Across 3 threshold-patrol cycles, CW has never flipped the fight. Root issue: SC's initiative (5) is consistently lower than DW-A and DW-B (both roll at least +2), so CW is always deferred to an already-acted ally. The MQ-12 guard blocks expenditure on dead/dying allies, but when HP > 20, CW fires and is collected on a "would-have-hit-anyway" roll.

  **Options for human review:**
  1. Increase SC's Dex modifier from +1 to +3 (give it a higher initiative floor to act before the DWs and CW a future-acting ally). Thematically: the shardcaller is the *coordinator*, it should act first.
  2. Change CW to trigger as a reaction when an ally hits, rather than a bonus-action pre-buff. Mechanically cleaner — fires exactly when an attack-roll advantage matters.
  3. Accept the pattern — CW is wasted in a 2-round fight against a fragile patrol; it's designed for longer multi-wave encounters where the DWs survive 3+ rounds.

  **MQ-TP-3-A — DW-B R1 melee-gap coaching note needed (new):** DW-B wants to peel to Marwen (MQ-NEW-TP10-1, confirmed 3 cycles), but Marwen is ~40 ft from DW-B's starting position while DW-B has 30 ft movement. Current .md says "peels to caster while other holds front" but doesn't specify the R1 choice: attack with crossbow (action) + Cunning Dash to close (bonus action), or Dash (action, no attack) + be in melee R2. Three cycles played as crossbow + Cunning Dash = correct by default (don't sacrifice action economy). Recommend adding: *"If caster is out of melee reach R1, fire Light Crossbow as action; Cunning Dash (bonus) to close for R2 melee."*

  **Human sign-off needed on FI-TP-3-A options.** MQ-TP-3-A is a low-cost .md coaching note.

### FI-EV13-A / FI-EV13-B / MQ-EV13-A: empty-void — DR surprise miss 13th-cycle confirm; VS kill-shot pattern; post-double-miss priority gap (2026-06-01T13)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 13:23 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) ~13th cycle. Seed 494533. ⚠ SIM-EV13-A authoritative divergence: roller showed surprise-round DR to-hit 14 vs AC 15 = MISS; sim incorrectly narrated as HIT due to cache desync (rng verification drew next pool slot). Authoritative state: all 3 PCs alive after surprise round.

  **FI-EV13-A — DR surprise-round opener unreliable (13th-cycle confirm; MQ-EV10-A ongoing):** Beholder's hard-trigger response is an immediate DR on the highest-level caster. Hit chance vs Marwen AC 15 is 60% (need 9+ on d20). In cycles 11, 12, and 13, the surprise DR missed (1+6=7; ambiguous miss; 8+6=14). Three consecutive misses suggests the binary "disintegrate caster / miss entirely" opener creates inconsistent negotiation-ending drama. A warning-shot VR (Void Ray as LA, 2 actions) after the hard trigger fires *before* initiative would: (a) deal 4d10 force as a reaction-to-threat signal, (b) be less likely to instantly end the fight, (c) still allow DR on the beholder's R1 turn. DR as the hard-trigger response is mechanically valid but narratively punishing only 60% of the time.

  **Options:** (1) Keep DR as hard-trigger (accept the variance — 40% miss creates an interesting "it gave us a warning" dynamic). (2) Switch to VR warning-shot as hard-trigger response; DR fires R1 when beholder has initiative advantage. (3) Lower the trigger threshold — only DR on explicit combat declaration, not just shaft-investigation intent.

  **FI-EV13-B — VS recharge-6 kill-shot (7th empty-void confirm; FI-EV12-C ongoing):** VS recharged on d6=6 in R2 and single-handedly dropped Sabriel from 44 to 6 HP (38 psychic, Wis save fail). Lair void_eruption finished the job (16 force). The VS+lair combo is the beholder's most decisive sequence — when VS fires, the fight is effectively over in 1–2 follow-up actions. The recharge-6 constraint (16.7% per round) means VS fires 0 or 1 times in most sub-4-round fights. The pattern is high-variance: VS never fires (fight won by DR+attrition) or VS fires and immediately ends the fight (feel issue: the party never sees a recovery arc). FI-EV12-C from cycle 12 recommended considering recharge 5–6 for VS. Current design keeps VS as the "patient beholder" moment; whether the feel requires change is a table-preference call.

  **MQ-EV13-A — Post-double-miss DR priority vs VS (new):** If DR misses twice consecutively (40%×40% = 16% chance per fight), the beholder enters R2+ with both DR (still unused) and VS (recharged). Tactics say "DR on highest caster if available" — but repeatedly missing AC 15 with a 60%-chance attack while holding VS (which ignores AC entirely, is area-effect, and adds frightened) creates a tactical incoherence. Recommend adding a coaching note: "if DR has missed the same target twice, do not retry before firing VS — VS's area + fear rider is more efficient than a third DR attempt."

  **Human sign-off needed.** The FI-EV13-A "warning-shot vs instant-DR" question is a design preference. FI-EV13-B VS recharge band is the larger balance question (has been open since cycle 6). MQ-EV13-A coaching note is a low-cost .md edit.

### FI-FC24-B / MQ-FC24-A: final-confrontation — wizard fragility pre-DR; DR .md audit (2026-06-01T10)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 10:29 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) ~18th cycle. Seed 494530/+1000.

  **FI-FC24-B — wizard fragility undermines DR drama:** Marwen reached 1/32 HP from accumulated R1 damage (lair void_eruption 9 force + STD-1 Ancient Resonance 13 necrotic + T4 dagger 6 pierce) *before the beholder's main action*. The Disintegration Ray technically killed Marwen but as cleanup on a PC already at 1 HP. The dramatic disintegration moment was preceded by Marwen's own Fireball (which was the fight's actual turning point — wiped 3 thralls, chunked beholder 47 HP). The intended arc is: "DR as the sudden, irreversible loss that breaks the party." In this slice, DR comes too late to serve that role.

  **Options for human review:**
  1. Adjust STD AR damage from 2d10 to 1d10+5 (reduces max burst, tightens band).
  2. Lower thrall dagger bonus (currently +3) — they're dominated husks, maybe +1 to-hit.
  3. Accept the pattern — Marwen's fragility is baked into CR 13 encounter design; the wizard is *supposed* to go down early.

  **MQ-FC24-A — DR .md vs. DB mechanic audit:** The DB `disintegration_ray` is correctly `single_attack` with `to_hit_bonus: 6` (confirmed MQ-EV10-B, cycle 11). However, the playtest simulation has now run DR as a "Dex save" for multiple consecutive cycles (SIM-FC24-A persistent), suggesting the beholder.md DM notes may still contain save-based DR language that isn't flagged. Audit the beholder.md tactics section and checklist for any "Dex save" references to DR — update to confirm attack-roll mechanic so DMs running `roll_combat_action` follow the output directly.

  **Human sign-off needed.** Options 1-3 above for wizard fragility; .md audit for DR is low-cost editorial fix.

### FI-TW23-A / FI-TW23-D: tank-wall — CW pays off when init aligns, but fight still ends R2; PTV inert when SC init > Rager init (23rd cycle, 2026-06-01T08)

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 08:18 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 23rd cycle. Seed 494528. Init: SC 19, Bazgar 17, Sabriel 14, Rager 11, Marwen 8.

  **FI-TW23-A — first confirmed CW collection in 23 cycles:** SC init 19 CW'd Rager before any PC acted. Rager survived to its turn (27/52 HP after Bazgar 5 + Sabriel smite 20 dmg). CW advantage fired: [5,16] best=16 → 21 vs AC 18 → HIT, 9 dmg on Bazgar. This is mechanically correct and the CW paid off. However, Marwen's Fireball (init 8, end of R1) applied 29 fire (Rager Dex save 4 vs DC 13 = FAIL), ending the Rager the same round. Total CW contribution: one hit for 9 dmg on Bazgar, who ended at 40/49 HP. Fight concluded R2 with Shardcaller alone vs. full party. The CW pairing *can* work; when it does, the payoff is one hit for ~9 dmg on one PC — insufficient to change the fight trajectory. The Rager durability (52 HP, no resistances, poor Dex save) remains the binding constraint.

  **FI-TW23-D — PTV inert when SC init > Rager init:** Pack Tactics Voice requires an ally to hit before the SC attacks. When SC has higher initiative than the Rager, the Rager hasn't swung yet when SC's turn comes around in R1. PTV can only activate starting R2 if the Rager hit in R1 — but in this slice, the Rager is dead by end of R1. PTV effectively requires SC to lose initiative to the Rager to be useful in this formation. The .md doesn't mention this dependency.

- **Recommendation:** Add a coaching note to Shardcaller .md under PTV: *"PTV fires on YOUR attacks only when a living ally already landed a hit this round. In tank-wall, this means SC must act AFTER the Rager in initiative for PTV to matter in R1."* Also consider: is the 2-NPC tank-wall slice meant to last 2+ rounds? 23 cycles of data say the Rager cannot hold past R1 vs. a focused level-5 party with Fireball. If the design intent is a 3-round wall fight, suggest either raising Rager HP to ~70 or adding fire resistance (thematically: forge-scarred derro).

### MQ-TW23-A: tank-wall — .md lacks initiative interaction guidance for CW and PTV (23rd cycle, 2026-06-01T08)

- **Context:** CW and PTV both have implicit initiative dependencies not documented in the NPC .md files. CW is optimal only when SC acts before Rager (so CW is ready when Rager swings). PTV is optimal only when SC acts after Rager (so Rager has hit before SC attacks). These are opposing conditions — the two passives cannot both be optimized simultaneously. A DM reading the .md has no guidance on this tradeoff.

- **Recommendation:** Add a single bullet to Shardcaller's checklist: *"CW/PTV initiative note: CW is most valuable when SC acts BEFORE Rager (advantage precedes Rager's swing). PTV is most valuable when SC acts AFTER Rager (ally has already hit). If SC goes first, prioritize CW; if SC goes after Rager, CW is less urgent — Rager hit may already have primed PTV."* This is a DM coaching note, not a spec change. Low-priority; document when other .md passes occur.

### FI-TP-2-A: threshold-patrol — CW structural lockout 2nd-cycle confirm; new burst-mechanism identified (2026-05-31T20)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 20:17 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 2nd cycle. Seed 494516.

  CW was unused for the 2nd consecutive TP cycle (1st-cycle: FI-TP-0-B). New mechanism confirmed: in this run, Bazgar's R1 burst (trip attack + longsword × 2) dropped DW-A to 11/27 HP before SC (init 8, lowest) could act. The MQ-12 guard correctly blocked CW on the already-acted DW-A (≤20 HP).

  Root cause: SC always acts last in TP formation (init 8 this run, init 8 prior run). By SC's first turn, the closest DW ally has absorbed a full PC attack round and is typically ≤20 HP.

  In R2, DW-A was dead before SC's turn. DW-B was at 19 HP and would have been borderline (MQ-12 guard at 20 HP boundary) — but also already-acted.

  **Implication:** CW has effective utility in TP formation only when SC rolls high initiative (≥15 to act before both DW allies). With 2-DW + 1-SC formation and SC's typical Dex-based initiative, this is structurally rare.

  **Options for human review:**
  1. Lower MQ-12 guard from ≤20 to ≤15 HP for threshold-patrol context (allows CW when ally is wounded but functional).
  2. Add SC guidance: "If both allies have already-acted this round at ≤20 HP, Tactical Retreat instead of holding CW."
  3. Accept CW as strategically available on high-init SC draws only (no change to spec).
  4. Revisit SC starting position — placing SC closer to DW allies might let a different ally serve as CW target.
  
  **Human sign-off needed.** No DB change required; .md tactics edit only if option 1 or 2 chosen.

### MQ-TP-2-A: threshold-patrol — Slow + Multiattack ruling; DW coaching note needed (2026-05-31T20)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 20:17 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 2nd cycle. Seed 494516.

  DW-A was Slowed R1 (1 of 3 NPCs caught). Simulation incorrectly applied 1-attack cap to DW-A's Multiattack. Correct 5e ruling: Slow restricts to "only one action per turn" — Multiattack IS one action. A slowed DW-A should still resolve both axe swings when using Multiattack. What Slow prevents: using *both* an action AND a bonus action (can only use one or the other). Drilling-advantage on a Slowed Multiattack is unchanged.

  **Recommended fix:** Add a bullet to the DW .md start-of-turn checklist:
  > "If SLOWED: can still use Multiattack (both attacks). Cannot also use a bonus action the same turn. Cunning Action is unavailable. No reactions."

  Low-risk .md edit. Human sign-off recommended but optional.

### MQ-EV10-A / FI-EV12-A (ESCALATED): empty-void — hard-trigger → DR surprise too binary; 12-cycle confirm (2026-05-31T19)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 19:00 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 12th cycle. Seed 494515.
