  MQ-EV10-A has been raised each cycle since the 10th. This cycle is the 12th confirm. Summary: when the party's hard-threat (explicit lower-shaft investigation statement) triggers the surprise round, the beholder fires Disintegration Ray. DR outcome splits the fight into two degenerate results:
  - DR hits Marwen (55% vs AC 15): permanent death before combat formally begins. Fight over in R1-2.
  - DR misses (45%): fight extends, feels anticlimactic — the beholder's opening was a whiff.

  12-cycle data suggests neither outcome feels satisfying. The miss (this cycle, nat 1 surprise round) undercuts tension; the hit (most prior cycles) is permanently-punishing before the party reacts.

  **Recommendation:** Change the hard-trigger response:
  - **Step 1 (hard threat):** Beholder fires a **Void Ray** (2 legendary actions, DC 16 Dex, 4d10 force) as a *warning shot* rather than DR. No surprise round — roll initiative immediately.
  - **DR** becomes available as a first-round action once initiative is established.
  - Second entry after dismissal remains "hostile on sight = DR in surprise" (per existing .md note).
  
  This gives: threat-response → initiative → real fight. DR stays lethal and scary but fires when the party can react. LoH/smites/positioning all matter.

  **Human sign-off required.** Changes negotiation trigger spec in beholder.md. Moderate complexity. Recommend testing in slice #7 cycle 13 before committing.

### FI-EV12-C (NEW): empty-void — VS recharge-6 creates binary outcomes; consider recharge 5-6 (2026-05-31T19)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 19:00 UTC, slice #7 12th cycle. Seed 494515.

  12-cycle data: VS fired in 5 of 12 cycles (~42%). All 5 VS-fire cycles ended TPK R2-3. All 7 non-VS cycles ran R4-6 with varied outcomes. The encounter is essentially two different fights depending on one d6 per round. At recharge 6-only, P(fires in 3 rounds) = 42%, in 4 rounds = 52%. At recharge 5-6, P(fires in 3 rounds) = 70%, in 4 rounds = 84%.

  The solo beholder without VS is a genuinely interesting fight (LA economy, DR, frightened riders). With VS it's a near-certain TPK. Recharge 5-6 would make VS the expected fight-shaper rather than the lucky wildcard.

  **Recommendation:** Change void_scream spec `recharge: 6` to `recharge: 5`. Run 3 validation cycles on slice #7. If VS fires too reliably (>80%), revert. **Human sign-off required.** DB change: `combat_action_upsert("beholder-thrulm", "void_scream", {..., "recharge": 5, ...})`.

### FI-EV12-D (NEW): empty-void — Drain Divinity tactics gap: no guidance on DD failure adaptation (2026-05-31T19)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 19:00 UTC, slice #7 12th cycle. Seed 494515.

  Beholder spent 6 LA on DD against Marwen across R1-R2. Both times Marwen saved (CHA +1 vs DC 16, ~30% save rate, hit threshold both times at 17). No guidance in the tactics section for "what to do when DD fails." Result: beholder auto-retried DD on next LA budget, burning another 3 LA with zero return.

  **Recommended tactics addition** to beholder.md DD priority section:
  > "If DD fails (target saved): do NOT immediately retry DD on next LA budget. Use Void Ray (2 LA) once against that target to apply HP pressure, then retry DD on the following budget. Pressing the same save twice gives the caster free consecutive chances at 30% success rate each; the VR forces them to spend resources to stay up, which makes the next DD failure more costly."

  **Human sign-off required.** Edit to beholder.md tactics section only; no DB change needed. Low-risk.

### MQ-SCT6-A: shardcaller-team — 3-SC barrage designation not explicit in checklist (new, 2026-05-31T18)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 18:19 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 65th cycle. Seed 494514.

  The derro-shardcaller checklist (item 5) describes the stagger rule and provides 2-SC endgame guidance, but does not specify which SC is the designated barrage-firer in a 3-SC formation. The testbot simulation chose "2nd-highest-initiative SC fires Barrage", which is consistent with the 2-SC endgame rule, but the checklist doesn't state this explicitly for 3+ SCs.

  The ambiguity also caused a simulation error (SIM-BUG-SCT6-B): because the barrage designee wasn't pre-assigned before the first SC decided on CW targets, SC-A Call Weakness'd the barrage SC (whose advantage was wasted on a save-based attack).

  **Recommendation:** Add to checklist item 5 under the STAGGER paragraph: *"3-SC designation: at start of round, designate the 2nd-highest-initiative alive SC as Barrage this round; the 1st and 3rd multiattack. This designation must be made before the first SC acts so CW selection can exclude the barrage SC."*

  **Human sign-off required.** This is a clarification edit to the .md; no DB change needed. Low-risk.

### FI-SCT6-A: shardcaller-team — Marwen R1-R2 elimination near-automatic vs 3-SC formation (new, 2026-05-31T18)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 18:19 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 65th cycle. Seed 494514.

  With 3 SCs using stagger (1 Barrage + 2 multiattacks), Marwen (32 HP, AC 15 wizard) receives ~25 damage in R1 (surviving to 7 HP), then falls early R2 from a follow-up multiattack. Her R1 Fireball lands, but she is dead before a 2nd Fireball is possible. This pattern may repeat consistently across cycles since the 3-SC formation focuses fire on the lowest-AC target.

  **Not a balance issue** at the slice level (Shardcaller Team is meant to be dangerous). Note for human: if this slice is used mid-dungeon (Marwen already resource-depleted), it could be a near-instant kill. Consider whether the party has access to pre-combat positioning options before using this formation in-session.

### FI-SRR18-D: solo-rager-rush — Berserk 3-line output cap: add DM cue to narration? (18th cycle, new pattern confirm)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 17:00 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 18th cycle. Seed 494513. TPK R8.

  **FI-SRR18-D (18th-cycle confirm):** The Berserk DB output always prints 3 attack lines (labeled "target 1", "target 2", "target 3") regardless of how many enemies are actually in reach. The tactics .md says *"DB output always shows 3 attack lines — DM caps at actual in-reach creature count and skips excess lines."* This instruction is correct but lives in Tactics, not in the action output itself. At the table, a DM who presses the Berserk button sees 3 lines and must remember to discard extras — a non-trivial cognitive load in a fast-moving combat.

  **Recommendation:** Append a parenthetical to the Berserk `output` field narration line: *"(DM: cap at actual in-reach target count — discard excess lines)"*. This is a DB narration change, not a mechanical change. Would require `combat_action_upsert` to update the `output` field. Low-risk, high-DM-UX value.

  **Human sign-off required** before editing the DB. Confirm that the parenthetical style is acceptable for the other multi-target attack outputs.

### FI-SRR18-E: solo-rager-rush — fight outcome entirely Fireball-dependent (18th cycle, first TPK)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 17:00 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 18th cycle. Seed 494513. TPK R8.

  **FI-SRR18-E (new):** All 17 prior solo-rager-rush cycles were VICTORY. This cycle is the first TPK, caused by poor Fireball penetration (2/3 ragers made their Dex saves, dealing only half-damage 11 each). The structural pattern is clear: Fireball full-fail → VICTORY R3–4; Fireball half-penetration → TPK R5–8. The L5 party has no winning path against 3× CR2 ragers without one clean Fireball.

  **This is not a bug.** Solo-rager-rush is a pressure-test, not a balanced fight. The Fireball-dependency is expected given the action economy. However: (a) the slice has very low decision depth — it's essentially a single dice-check wrapped in 3–8 rounds of resolution; (b) a DM running this live would see Fireball succeed 17 out of 18 times and conclude the party "always wins," missing that one bad-luck cycle ends in TPK. The fight is more volatile than it appears.

  **No action required.** Logging as structural context for encounter design notes. If the slice is used as a warmup fight it should carry a DM note: *"This encounter is Fireball-gated. If Marwen's Fireball fails to drop at least 1 rager, the party should retreat."*

### MQ-SRR18-A: solo-rager-rush — Rager Greataxe damage modifier: +2 (DB) vs +3 (stat block saves)?

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 17:00 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 18th cycle. Seed 494513. TPK R8.

  **MQ-SRR18-A (new):** The Berserk and Multiattack DB outputs print `+2` as the damage modifier. The rager .md stat block shows "Saves Str +4, Con +4" — if Str save = prof(+2) + Str mod, then Str mod = +2. However, Str save +4 with proficiency +3 (CR 2) would give Str mod +1, not +2. The modifier is ambiguous from the stat block header alone.

  **Recommendation:** Verify the rager's Strength modifier against the original stat array. If Str mod = +2, DB is correct; if Str mod = +3 (half-plate melee tank intended), the DB spec needs updating via `combat_action_upsert`. A +1 difference per hit (~7 hits this cycle) equals ~7 HP of underestimated damage — not fight-changing, but affects accuracy of future sim calibration.

  **Human check required** (stat array file or design notes). No auto-fix applied.

### MQ-FC5-A: final-confrontation — stagger rule start-of-round check: add checklist prompt? (5th cycle, new)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 16:00 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 5th cycle. Seed 494512. TPK R3.

  **MQ-FC5-A (NEW):** The stagger rule says "Stagger is evaluated at the START of the round — check both STDs *before any actions resolve*." This is already in the .md under Tactics. However, the playtest sim violated it by checking at time-of-action (when STD-A acted at init 7, STD-B had already set its `ar_used` flag, making the "both have AR" condition false). A live DM faces the same cognitive load: by the time the lower-init STD acts, the higher-init STD has already gone, and the DM may not remember to have pre-marked the hold.

  **Recommendation:** Add a single bullet to shrine-touched-derro.md Start-of-turn checklist (round-start section) — *"⚑ STAGGER REMINDER: At the start of every round (before any STD acts), if BOTH shrine-touched derro have Ancient Resonance available, mark the lower-initiative one as 'AR HELD this round'."* The text in Tactics is correct; this is a DM-prompt duplication in the checklist where DMs are more likely to catch it.

  **Human sign-off required** before editing shrine-touched-derro.md. (Low risk — no mechanical change, documentation only.)

### MQ-SW20-A: shrine-wedge — downed PC counts as "enemy in cone" for UF priority? (20th cycle, new)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 12:00 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 20th cycle. Seed 494509. VICTORY R4.

  **MQ-SW20-A (NEW):** In R2, Bazgar was downed (0 HP, unconscious) entering STD-B's turn. STD-B had UF active. The .md says: "if UF active and only 2 enemies in cone, PREFER Multiattack over AR." The sim counted unconscious Bazgar as a 3rd cone enemy and fired AR instead of Multiattack. The actual tactical impact was minimal (AR downed Bazgar who was already at 10 HP with two passing saves for Sabriel/Marwen), but the ruling matters for future cycles where UF+AR is fired at a 2-standing-PC situation.

  **Recommendation:** Downed/unconscious PCs do NOT count as "enemies in cone" for UF priority purposes. They cannot take actions, cannot be meaningfully targeted by save effects, and their presence inflates the cone count artificially. Add one line to shrine-touched-derro.md under the UF tactics note: *"Unconscious or downed creatures do not count as active enemies in the cone for this calculation."*

  Note: this does NOT change the stagger rule or the below-20-HP AR-reckless rule — only the UF priority check.

  **Human sign-off required** before editing shrine-touched-derro.md.

### FI-BEL21-C: beholder-escorts-limited — manifest_thralls lair guidance when 1 survivor at low HP

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 06:18 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 21st cycle. Seed 494502. TPK R3.

  With Thrall-A and Thrall-B wiped by R1 Fireball, the R3 lair rotation reaches `manifest_thralls` with only Thrall-C alive at 6 HP. The lair action grants +1 temp HP and one reaction attack (MISS). Zero impact. The beholder's established lair rotation (UG→VE→MT→UG…) predictably reaches MT on R3, exactly when escorts are most depleted. **Recommendation:** add DM guidance note to beholder-thrulm.md tactics section — "If only 1 thrall alive at ≤ half HP when manifest_thralls lair slot triggers, use `unstable_ground` or `void_eruption` instead." This prevents tactically empty lair turns without changing the rotation structure. Human sign-off required on whether to add note to .md.

### MQ-BEL21-B: VS half-damage kills PC on a successful save when they are already low HP

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 06:18 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 21st cycle. Seed 494502. TPK R3.

  Marwen (15 HP entering R3) passed the Void Scream Wis save (d20+3 = 23 vs DC 16). Half of 40 psychic = 20 psychic. 20 > 15: Marwen went down on a successful save. This is mechanically correct 5e behavior, but may surprise players who assume a save means survival. **Recommendation:** add DM coaching note to beholder-thrulm.md tactics section: "VS at near-max damage can kill even characters who make the save if they are below ~20 HP. DM should note pre-damage HP before calling for saves, and narrate the half-damage death as momentum-collapse, not a betrayal." Not a spec change — documentation only. Human sign-off.

### FI-BEL23-C (NEW DESIGN DECISION): beholder-escorts-limited — VS tactical priority gap vs active grapple

- **Context:** 2026-06-01 09:16 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 23rd cycle. Seed 494529. TPK R5.

  Void Scream was available from R1 and never fired. In all 23 BEL cycles, VS has fired **0 times** while an active grapple was in progress. The root cause is a tactics conflict: the beholder's .md says both "fire VS the moment it's recharged" AND "grapple → Maw the grappled target." Once Marwen was grappled (R1 TL1 to-hit 26, str save 9 fail), the grapple-Maw loop dominated every subsequent beholder action choice. The grapple-Maw sequence is locally optimal (Maw auto-crits a grappled target), but VS + fear rider suppresses the entire party's offense for 2-3 rounds — potentially more cumulative value.

  **The .md is silent on which tactic to prioritize when both are simultaneously available.**

  **Recommended tactics addition (human decision required):**
  > *"VS interrupts the grapple-Maw loop: if VS is recharged AND ≥2 PCs are within 30 ft, prefer VS over Maw (even if a grapple is active — release it). The fear rider degrades the whole party's offense for 2-3 rounds. Exception: if only 1 PC is alive and within 30 ft, continue the Maw — no multi-target value to justify dropping the guaranteed crit."*

  This does not change any mechanical spec; it's a DM coaching note. Do not auto-fix.

### FI-TW20-A: tank-wall — CW range lockout confirmed 20th cycle; 2/3 charges structurally wasted

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 20:25 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 20th cycle. Seed 494492. VICTORY R6.

  **FI-TW20-A (DESIGN DECISION):** CW has 30 ft range. Standard tank-wall deployment: SC 45 ft from PCs, Rager 15 ft from PCs → SC-to-Rager = 30 ft at start (barely in range). Once Rager charges to melee (5 ft from PCs), SC-to-Rager gap expands to ~40 ft → **CW permanently unavailable for the rest of the fight.** This run: CW fired R1 (gave Rager nat-20 advantage on ATK1 — the CW worked correctly and was fight-relevant). But 2/3 charges sat idle Rounds 2–6. The prior 19th-cycle tank-wall run (2026-05-30T12-19-42) also confirmed 0/3 CW usage in a 3-round version. Pattern is structural, not variance.

  Three options for DM: **(a)** Increase CW range to 60 ft — SC can CW the Rager from back-line throughout the fight. **(b)** Accept current mechanic as "R1 only" — CW is a pre-charge buff; subsequent charges can be spent on PCs if Rager falls and party closes within 30 ft. **(c)** Tighten SC starting position to 25-30 ft from PCs (not 45-60 ft) — SC is more vulnerable but CW stays active. Option (b) requires adding the note explicitly to the .md so DMs don't hold charges waiting for Rager to come back in range (it won't). **Human sign-off required.**

### FI-TW20-B / MQ-TW20-B: tank-wall — PTV (Pack Tactics Voice) inactive in standard formation; "ally" definition ambiguous

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 20:25 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 20th cycle. Seed 494492. VICTORY R6.

  **FI-TW20-B + MQ-TW20-B (DESIGN DECISION):** PTV fires "when an ally within 30 ft hits." In standard tank-wall, the Rager is in melee ~40 ft from the SC → Rager's hits don't trigger PTV. SC's own hits: grammatically "an ally" implies another creature, not the SC itself. If this reading is correct, **PTV is inactive in every standard tank-wall run where Rager is in melee.** PTV only reliably fires in: (a) multi-SC formations (SCs within 30 ft of each other); (b) single-SC encounters where SC advances to mid-range; (c) if "ally" is reinterpreted to include the SC itself.

  **MQ-TW20-B ruling request:** Does SC's own hit count as "an ally hit" for PTV? If YES: PTV fires on every SC multiattack hit → the target of the hit has disadv on its next save (relevant for Barrage DC 13 the following turn). If NO: PTV never fires in solo-SC-plus-melee-Rager formation. This is a passive ability that either fires every hit or never fires — the reading changes PTV's power level substantially. **Human sign-off required on the "ally" definition.**

### FI-TP18-A: threshold-patrol — CW structural lockout 18th confirm, new mechanism: Fireball pre-emption (18th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 18:20 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 18th cycle. Seed 494490. VICTORY R2.

  **FI-TP18-A (DESIGN DECISION, 18th-cycle new mechanism):** Across all 18 threshold-patrol cycles, SC has used 0–1 CW charges per fight. This cycle adds a new lockout vector: Marwen and SC both rolled init 11; as a PC, Marwen goes first. Fireball R1 killed DW-A and DW-B before SC's turn, leaving SC with zero eligible CW targets (spec requires a living ally). Prior cycles saw lockout via HP guard (MQ-12: ≤20 HP) or already-acted guard (DD-39). This cycle: the allies simply don't exist when SC acts. **Pattern conclusion (18 cycles, 3 distinct lockout mechanisms):** CW is structurally non-functional in threshold-patrol regardless of seed. The 30-ft range and 3-charge pool are unworkable when: (a) Fireball kills DW allies before SC turn; (b) DWs hit half-HP threshold and switch to crossbow before SC can CW them; (c) DWs act before SC and are at ≤20 HP when SC follows. Recommend one of: (i) increase CW range to 60 ft; (ii) add a pre-combat CW declaration phase (SC calls out target before initiative); (iii) replace CW with a reactive passive buff. Human sign-off required.

### FI-TP18-B: threshold-patrol — Fireball R1 single-action encounter resolution (18th-cycle feel note)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 18:20 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 18th cycle. Seed 494490. VICTORY R2.

  **FI-TP18-B (FEEL NOTE):** 31 fire Fireball (hot roll ~85th pctile 8d6) hit all 3 NPCs with no saves passed — fight effectively over in Marwen's action. DW avg HP (27) is below avg Fireball dmg (28), so even an average roll kills both DWs on failed saves. With Marwen acting at or before init 11 (≈50% of runs), Fireball terminates the encounter before NPCs can apply sustained multi-round pressure. Recommend adding a terrain constraint that delays Fireball's range or clusters NPCs behind line-of-sight cover (pillar or door) requiring Marwen to advance before targeting. A 45 ft starting distance (vs current ~30 ft assumed) would push Fireball to R2, giving NPCs one full NPC round of output. This changes feel without changing the eventual outcome.

### MQ-EV10-A: empty-void — Hard trigger after successful persuasion: recommend Void Ray warning shot instead of DR surprise (new, 10th-cycle; 2nd-cycle confirm 11th-cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 17:18 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 10th cycle. Seed 494489. TPK R5. **2nd-cycle confirm: 2026-05-31 10:23 UTC, 11th cycle. Seed 494506. TPK R3.**

  **MQ-EV10-A (DESIGN DECISION):** In this run Sabriel's Exchange 2 persuasion succeeded (17 vs DC 14) — the beholder was actively open to negotiation. Exchange 3 (Marwen asking about the deeper shaft) triggered the documented hard trigger (FI-NEW-EV5-B: "explicit stated intent to investigate the lower shaft → immediate DR surprise round"). The transition from "actively negotiating" to "DR disintegration no-warning" felt abrupt even in simulation. **11th-cycle confirm adds new detail:** DR missed in surprise (Bazgar AC18, roll 9), then recharged d6=6 in ROUND 1 recharge check, pivoted to Marwen (AC15), killed her with 31 force. "Miss on Fighter, kill-on-Wizard" is a distinct two-phase pattern that will recur ~1/6 of runs (immediate recharge probability). **Recommendation:** When the hard trigger fires *after* a persuasion PASS (beholder was in a deal-state), replace the opening move with: (1) one Void Ray (2 LA) as a warning shot + initiative roll immediately; (2) if the party continues hostile action, full combat follows with DR available. If the hard trigger fires without a prior pass (beholder was in dismiss-state or neutral), the current immediate-DR rule stays. This preserves the punishing consequence while giving the table one beat to register the betrayal. Change needed in beholder.md tactics section under "Negotiation pacing." Needs human sign-off.

### MQ-EV10-B: empty-void — DR spec is single_attack (vs-AC) ~~RESOLVED 11th cycle~~

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 17:18 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 10th cycle. Seed 494489. TPK R5. **RESOLVED: 2026-05-31 10:23 UTC, 11th cycle. Seed 494506.**

  **MQ-EV10-B RESOLVED:** DB spec confirmed as `single_attack`, `to_hit_bonus: 6`. This is an attack roll vs AC, not a Dex save. In the 11th-cycle run, DR to-hit of 9 missed Bazgar (AC18) in surprise, then 25 hit Marwen (AC15) in R1. Both rolls are consistent with `to_hit +6` at-AC behavior. The mechanic is intentional per the DB. Items (b) and (c) from the 10th-cycle note remain open for human decision: `+6` vs. MM-standard `+7`, and whether to add a one-line mechanic note to the .md.

### MQ-EV11-A: empty-void — DR recharge timing ambiguity: start-of-round vs start-of-beholder's-turn (new, 11th-cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 10:23 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 11th cycle. Seed 494506. TPK R3.

  **MQ-EV11-A (DESIGN DECISION):** The beholder.md "Start-of-turn checklist step 1" says "if DR USED, roll d6 — recovers on 5–6." The sim ran this check at the START OF ROUND (before the lair action fires at init 20), rather than at the start of the beholder's actual turn (which comes after the lair action). In the 11th-cycle run, DR was used in the surprise round, then the recharge check ran at the start of Round 1 — returning DR available before the lair action. The beholder then used DR on its main turn. If the intent is that recharge happens at the START OF THE BEHOLDER'S TURN (i.e., after the lair action fires at init 20), the sequence is: lair → other PCs → beholder recharge check → beholder acts. Under this reading, the beholder does NOT know whether DR is recharged when the lair action fires. **Recommendation:** Clarify in the .md checklist whether "start-of-turn" means (a) start of the combat round (before lair action), or (b) specifically the moment before the beholder takes its own initiative action. Option (b) is more standard 5e phrasing and means lair actions always fire under "DR unknown" state. Needs human sign-off on which is intended.

### FI-EV11-C: empty-void — VS recharge-6 statistically never fires in sub-4-round fights (11th-cycle, 7th confirm)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 10:23 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 11th cycle. Seed 494506. TPK R3.

  **FI-EV11-C (FEEL NOTE / DESIGN DECISION):** VS did not recharge in 3 rounds (d6: 2, 2, 4). In all 11 empty-void cycles tracked, VS fired in the following rounds: R4 (2 cycles), R5 (3 cycles), never (6 cycles). Average fight length in empty-void: ~3.5 rounds before TPK. **VS recharge-6 (16.7% per round) fires in sub-4-round fights ~40% of the time** (1 − (5/6)^3 ≈ 42%). In practice, the beholder's main tactics (DR, grapple+Maw, Drain Divinity LA) end the fight before VS matters. The .md says "be patient" but the fight doesn't wait. **Options:** (a) Lower VS to recharge-5 (40% per round → 78% fires in 3 rounds); (b) Make VS a guaranteed lair option in the second round if PCs are clustered; (c) Accept the current design — VS only fires in longer fights, rewarding PC tactics that avoid clustering. Options (a) and (b) would change the empty-void balance significantly. Needs human sign-off.

### FI-EV10-A: empty-void — DR in surprise round from negotiation trigger = permanent PC loss at level 5 (10th-cycle, new context)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 17:18 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 10th cycle. Seed 494489. TPK R5.

  **FI-EV10-A (DESIGN DECISION, 10th-cycle new context):** With correct DR mechanics (attack roll, to-hit 23 vs Marwen AC 15), Marwen is disintegrated in the surprise round. At level 5, the party has no access to True Resurrection or Wish. Disintegration is permanent. Across 10 EV cycles the beholder has disintegrated Marwen in or near the surprise round repeatedly; this run adds the new context that it happened *after a negotiation persuasion success* — raising the narrative stakes. The beholder.md has a softening note: "DM discretion to soften this narrative outcome if it creates a table problem." **Recommendation** (strengthening earlier FI-EV7-A recommendation): in solo-beholder configuration, add an explicit tactics note: "HOLD DR when transitioning from active negotiation to combat. Open with Void Scream (if available) or Multiattack instead; reserve DR for the second round of sustained combat. A first-contact disintegration from a negotiation scene creates permanent PC loss before the table has had a chance to fight, which may undermine session investment more than the combat challenge justifies." This doesn't change the beholder's power level — it changes the opening move of the encounter's worst case.

### FI-SRR-16-A: solo-rager-rush — Wizard-taunter lowest-initiative death exposes Taunt split gap (new, 16th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 15:00 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 16th cycle. Seed 494487. VICTORY R4.

  **FI-SRR-16-A (DESIGN DECISION):** Grimjaw drew initiative 6 — the lowest roll of all 6 combatants. He was the rager assigned to taunt Marwen per FI-31 split-taunt rotation (R1→Marwen, R2→Sabriel, R3→Bazgar). He never acted: Fireball brought him to 26 HP, Sabriel's smite to 7 HP, Bazgar finished him. Marwen cast Fireball twice (R1+R2) completely uncontested. The split-taunt strategy assumes each rager acts before its target, which is only true if the rager wins initiative. The wizard typically has lower initiative modifiers (DEX +3 vs rager DEX −1, median gap ~4 pips), so the rager-assigned-to-wizard frequently loses the race. **Recommendation:** Revise rager tactics to say "whichever rager acts first should Taunt the wizard (highest-spell-threat) as its first bonus action — even if the 'designated' taunter hasn't acted yet. Priority: wizard > caster > whoever." This prevents one unfavorable initiative roll from nullifying the taunt strategy entirely.

### FI-SRR-16-B: solo-rager-rush — Berserk hit rate is AC-gated, not uniformly weak (16th-cycle clarification of FI-SRR-B)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 15:00 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 16th cycle. Seed 494487. VICTORY R4.

  **FI-SRR-16-B (DESIGN DECISION — clarification to existing FI-SRR-B):** Cycles 5-15 flagged "Berserk fizzle vs AC18-19" and recommended recharge 4-6. This run shows Berserk connected readily against Marwen (AC15): Bonesnap hit her R2 (19 vs 15), and 5 of 7 total Berserk attacks landed (compared to the near-whiff patterns in prior cycles that modeled only high-AC party members). Against AC19 (Sabriel) the fizzle pattern held (3 misses in 3 attempts this run). The recharge-4-6 recommendation from FI-SRR-B is still valid for AC18-19 scenarios, but Berserk is already doing meaningful work against AC≤16. **For human:** the recommendation to boost recharge applies specifically to the "all party members AC18+" scenario. If the encounter regularly features at least one low-AC PC (caster, rogue), Berserk stays threatening without a recharge change. Consider framing FI-SRR-B fix as "increase recharge only if run at full-plate party" rather than blanket change.

### FI-BEL20-A: beholder-escorts-limited — VS recharge-6 variance makes outcome VS-dependent (new, 20th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 13:31 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 20th cycle. Seed 494485. **VICTORY R6** — first slice-3 victory since cycle 10.

  **FI-BEL20-A (DESIGN DECISION):** VS failed to recharge for 6 consecutive rounds (d6 rolls: 5,2,2,1,4,4). P(no recharge in 6 rounds) ≈ 33%. With VS absent, the fight was a 6-round attrition grind — party took damage but remained functional (beholder died R6 from Marwen Fire Bolt + Bazgar longsword). In VS-present cycles (the other ~67%), the fight is a decisive TPK by R3-4. The outcome is strongly bimodal: VS fires → TPK; VS absent → possible party victory. **For human:** Is recharge-6 for VS intentional "rarely fires, devastating when it does"? The current variance creates wildly different fight textures. If the BEL slice should always be threatening/unwinnable, consider recharge-5 (36% per round, expected 2.2 fires in 6 rounds). If one devastating VS event is the design, recharge-6 is correct and this Victory run confirms that without it the party can win.

### FI-BEL20-B: beholder-escorts-limited — LoH revival loop vs DD monopoly priority conflict (new, 20th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 13:31 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 20th cycle. Seed 494485. VICTORY R6.

  **FI-BEL20-B (DESIGN DECISION):** Sabriel used Lay on Hands 4× to revive Bazgar (5HP each), contributing ~20HP of healing that directly extended the fight 3 rounds and enabled the party kill. The beholder's .md says: "spend 1 legendary action (Tentacle Lash, 1 LA) at the END of Sabriel's turn to pressure her HP" when she LoH-loops. This never fired because DD consumes all 3 LA every round, leaving no LA budget for Tentacle. The two tactics are mutually exclusive when budget is full (3 LA = one DD, no leftover). **For human:** should the LoH-pressure rule take priority over DD in specific conditions? Proposed resolution: "If Sabriel used LoH on an ally this turn AND Sabriel has L2+ slots remaining (making her a valid DD target next turn), skip DD this turn and instead use: Tentacle (1 LA) on Sabriel + Void Ray (2 LA) on the highest-threat PC. Resume DD next turn." This trades one DD for Sabriel HP pressure + VR offensive output, and prevents LoH loop from being entirely uncountered. Not auto-fixing — affects fundamental LA allocation logic.

### FI-SW18-A: shrine-wedge — Fireball and smite suppression need in-world DM cue (18th-cycle coaching note)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 11:18 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 18th cycle. Seed 494483. Victory R2.

  **FI-SW18-A (DM COACHING NOTE):** Marwen burned a 3rd-level Fireball expecting fire-vulnerability doubling (STDs have fire vulnerability). Altar zone suppressed it — normal damage only. Sabriel's Divine Smite radiant damage was similarly unsuppressed. This is **working as designed**, but there is no in-world narration cue that the altar zone is dampening the exploit. At the table, a player who casts Fireball and does not see doubled damage will wonder if a rule was misapplied. Recommend adding a single-line narration hint to the altar zone description in `world/factions/dulgarum-oathholds/locations/thrulm/_overview.md` or the shrine-touched-derro `.md` altar-zone callout: *"Fire chars the runes but doesn't bite the flesh — the altar absorbs the excess heat."* / *"Radiant light diffuses into the stone's ancient wards."* This gives the DM a ready phrase to narrate the suppression at the table. No spec change needed; editorial only. Not urgent — the mechanic has been working correctly for 18 cycles and players have presumably been told OOC about the zone.

  **MQ-SW18-A (infrastructure, non-urgent):** External random APIs (quantumnumbers + random.org) blocked for 51 consecutive Phase A cycles. The workaround (pre-seeding `dnd_roller._number_cache` with Python `random` before calling `roll_combat_action`) is reliable but requires the cron to know to do it. A proper fix: add a local `random.randint` fallback as last-resort in `dnd_roller._ensure_numbers()` (3-line change). Not urgent but would eliminate the pre-seeding ceremony from every future fire.

### FI-SCT-16-C/D: shardcaller-team — stagger-enforced encounter not threatening L5 party (new, 16th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 08:20 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 16th cycle. Seed 494480. Victory R2.

  **FI-SCT-16-C/D (DESIGN DECISION — new):** With stagger correctly enforced (only 1 Shard-Barrage R1, both targets saved → 6 piercing each), the 3× shardcaller encounter is not threatening a level-5 party. All PCs ended at 87-100% HP. The fight resolved in 2 rounds via Fireball (24 fire, all 3 SCs fail) + 2 smite swings. The encounter's "dangerous mode" requires either stagger enforcement failure (cycle 15 triple-barrage near-TPK'd) or a lucky triple-save-fail chain (uncommon). When stagger works as designed, the shardcaller-team slice is a 2-3 round VICTORY with minimal resource expenditure. This has now been confirmed across 16 cycles — DD-18 (Fireball dominance) and the stagger mechanic together make this slice feel like a warmup rather than a meaningful encounter. **For human:** is this the intended feel for the shardcaller-only formation? If not, consider: (a) HP increase to ~45 per SC; (b) a 4th shardcaller; (c) ensuring SC-B wins initiative (fires barrage before Fireball). The encounter as designed is appropriate as a patrol skirmish, not a standalone challenge.

  **MQ-SCT-16-A (clarification recommended, not urgent):** When SC-C acts after the barrage-slot SC has already fired (and the barrage-slot SC is at >20 HP), MQ-12 literally permits CW on the barrage-slot SC. But stagger guidance says "CW non-barrage multiattacking SCs." These two rules conflict when the barrage-slot SC has already acted and is above 20 HP. Recommend adding to the stagger CW guidance: "When no non-barrage-slot SC above 20 HP remains as a valid CW target, hold the charge — do not fall back to CW'ing the barrage-slot SC even post-barrage, as the barrage-slot SC is the highest-priority kill target."

### FI-SRR-15-A: solo-rager-rush — Healing Word revive into immediate re-down (new, 15th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 07:16 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 15th cycle. Seed 494479. Victory R6.

  **FI-SRR-15-A (DESIGN DECISION — new):** Sabriel used her only Healing Word (bonus action) to revive Marwen at 6 HP in R4. Rager-C targeted Marwen that same round and re-downed her with a multiattack (3+14 = 17 total damage, easily exceeding 6 HP). The heal was wasted. The root problem: Rager-C consistently targets the lowest-HP creature, and a PC revived to 6 HP is immediately the softest target. At the table this would feel terrible — the divine martial burns her only revive and it survives one enemy action. **Three questions for the human to consider:** (1) Should the .md add DM coaching guidance that Healing Word revives are risky until Rager-C is occupied or dead? (2) Should rager targeting behavior reset on a revive (i.e., rager stays on its current target rather than immediately pivoting to the fresh-revived 6-HP PC)? (3) Is there a design intent where Sabriel's "correct" play is to let Marwen stabilize via death saves rather than risk a heal-sink? Not a spec bug — DESIGN DECISION for human.

### FI-SRR-15-B: solo-rager-rush — Thunderwave vs Rager-C Con +4 unreliable (new, 15th cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 07:16 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 15th cycle. Seed 494479. Victory R6.

  **FI-SRR-15-B (DESIGN DECISION — new):** Marwen used Thunderwave (2nd-level, DC 14, 3d8 thunder, push 10 ft) as an emergency gap-creator after Rager-C closed to melee in R1. Rager-C succeeded the Con save (d20+4 = 21 vs DC 14) — result: half damage (5), no push. The push that would have created 10 ft of separation failed. DC 14 vs Con +4 is approximately a coin-flip (50% save rate), making Thunderwave unreliable as a "get out of melee" spell against ragers specifically. Marwen's primary emergency escape tool is a coin flip rather than a reliable counter. **For human consideration:** (a) should Rager Con be reduced from +4 to +3 to make Thunderwave a 55/45 DM-favored situation? (b) Is the 50/50 tension intentional — the choice to cast Thunderwave is itself a risky decision? (c) Does Marwen need a different go-to emergency spell vs high-Con melee? Not a bug, but affects wizard survivability feel in this slice.

### FI-SRR-B: solo-rager-rush — Berserk fizzle vs AC 18-19 (15th consecutive cycle confirm)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 07:16 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 15th cycle. Seed 494479. Victory R6.

  **FI-SRR-B (escalated — 15th consecutive SRR cycle confirmation):** In this cycle, 8 Berserk attack rolls across 4 Berserk uses produced 3 hits and 5 misses. The two fully-fizzled Berserk uses: (R1 Rager-B with aggro advantage + Madness Endurance +1: d20+5 adv vs AC 18 → 13 miss, vs AC 19 → 9 miss) and (R5 Rager-C recharged, 2 targets: vs AC 18 → 5 miss, vs AC 19 → 14 miss). Both complete fizzles occurred under good conditions. The structural math: Berserk to-hit bonus +4, vs AC 18 = 30% hit rate, vs AC 19 = 25% hit rate. With a Recharge 5-6 (33%), the expected value is roughly 1 Berserk use per 3 turns, at 30% per target, meaning the expected damage contribution is modest. The sweep *narrative* (a rager spinning through multiple PCs) fires dramatically but often deals 0 damage. This pattern has now been confirmed across 15 consecutive SRR cycles. Prior recommendation (recharge 4-6 or miss-consolation effect such as "on a miss, the target must make a Str save or be pushed 5 ft") stands. **This item needs a human decision before the 16th cycle.**

### MQ-FC15-A: final-confrontation — Disintegration Ray spec inconsistency: .md says DC15 Con save, DB has none (15th cycle, new)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 14:24 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 15th cycle. Seed 494486. TPK R3.

  **MQ-FC15-A (DESIGN DECISION — new):** `beholder-thrulm / disintegration_ray` DB spec has `rider_on_hit: "If this damage reduces the target to 0 HP, target is disintegrated"` — no saving throw. The beholder's `.md` file states: "on hit DC15 Con save or disintegrated." These are mechanically different: (a) DB design = deal 10d8 force, disintegrate only if HP reaches 0; (b) .md design = hit triggers a Con save first, fail = disintegrated regardless of HP. In 5e MM the standard beholder DR follows design (a). The .md variant adds a Con-save layer. In practice, DR missed in this run (and in most runs) so the inconsistency hasn't manifested — but if DR lands a hit, the DM needs to know whether to call for a Con save or just deal damage. **For human:** which design is intended? If the .md's Con save is correct, add `pre_save: {dc: 15, ability: "con", on_fail: "disintegrated"}` to the DR spec (or a rider in the DB). If the DB's "reduce to 0 HP" design is correct, remove the Con save language from the .md. Either choice is balanced; they just create different drama at the table (Con save = tension on a hit even before damage; reduce-to-0 = tension only on near-dead targets).

### FI-FC14-B: final-confrontation — Antireality "< AC+2" trigger (2nd cross-slice confirmation, escalated)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 06:25 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 14th cycle. Seed 494478. TPK R4.

  **FI-FC14-B (DESIGN DECISION — 2nd confirmation of FI-BE3-03):** Sabriel's R1 longsword total was 19 vs beholder AC 17+2=19. Antireality fired (total ≤ AC+2 = 19), +2 AC applied (effective AC = 19), attack total 19 ≥ 19 → HIT STILL LANDS. Reaction consumed with zero mechanical benefit. This is now confirmed across TWO SEPARATE SLICES (slice #3 R1 with Bazgar; slice #4 R1 with Sabriel) and TWO SEPARATE PLAYER BUILDS. The "≤ AC+2" edge case is not a one-off — it's structurally present whenever any melee PC rolls exactly AC+2-from-beholder total (beholder AC 17 → any roll of 19 triggers the degenerate case; +3 atk PC needs d20=16; that's a 25% d20 hit window where the trigger fires but zero-benefits). **Escalating to confirmed DESIGN DECISION for human review.** Recommendation: change trigger to `atk total < AC+2` (strict less-than), ensuring Antireality only fires when the +2 AC will actually turn a hit into a miss.

### FI-FC14-D: final-confrontation — VS range gate; beholder shrine_drift distance determines who gets caught

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 06:25 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 14th cycle. Seed 494478. TPK R4.

  **FI-FC14-D (DM coaching note, not a spec change):** Beholder shrine_drifted to 20 ft from altar before firing VS. VS radius 30 ft from that position reaches 50 ft from altar. Marwen was at threshold (60 ft from altar) = 10 ft outside VS radius, surviving until R4. If beholder had drifted to 30 ft instead, VS would have caught all 3 PCs (30+30=60 ft = threshold). DM should count distance before firing: "Beholder at X ft + 30 ft radius = catches everything within X+30 ft." To maximize VS coverage against a party at ~60 ft, beholder must be at ≥ 30 ft from altar. This also means exposing the beholder to OA from Bazgar during the drift (VS descent OA note in Tactics). DM tradeoff: drift closer for full coverage vs stay at 20 ft for OA safety.

### FI-BE3-03: beholder-escorts-limited — Antireality margin trigger with no benefit (19th-cycle, edge case)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 19:20 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 19th cycle. Seed 494467. TPK R4.

  **FI-BE3-03 (DESIGN DECISION):** Bazgar's R1 attack total was 19 vs beholder AC 17. Per DD-43, Antireality triggers when `atk ≤ AC+2` (17+2=19). The +2 AC raises effective AC to 19. Bazgar's atk (19) equals the new AC exactly → hit still lands. The reaction was consumed with zero benefit. At the table this reads as "the beholder flinched for nothing." The current trigger condition (`atk ≤ AC+2`) creates a degenerate case where an atk exactly equal to `AC+2` triggers the reaction but cannot be negated. The intended purpose of the reaction is to convert borderline hits into misses.

  **Recommendation:** Tighten trigger from `≤ AC+2` to `< AC+2` (i.e., atk 17 or 18 only), so Antireality always has a chance to negate the hit when it fires. This removes the "trigger but zero benefit" case and makes the reaction more legible at the table. Do NOT auto-fix — requires updating the threshold stated in both the .md Tactics block and DD-43 if formally adopted.

### FI-BE3-02: beholder-escorts-limited — Drain Divinity monopolizes LA budget (19th-cycle confirm of FI-NEW-BEL10-B)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 19:20 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 19th cycle. Seed 494467. TPK R4.

  **FI-BE3-02 (DESIGN DECISION — repeat of FI-NEW-BEL10-B):** DD (3 LA) consumed the entire legendary action budget after Bazgar's turn in every round. VR and Tentacle Lash never fired as legendary actions across 3 active rounds. LA tracker showed 0/3 for all turns after the first PC's. Confirming the 10th-cycle finding: the DD-vs-VR+TL tradeoff is mechanically sound (DD > VR+T when a L2+ slot target is in range) but the feel consequence is that the beholder appears to "do nothing" on 3 of 4 PC turns per round. This is the 19th consecutive BEL cycle; the pattern is structural, not variance. See FI-NEW-BEL10-B for the full recommendation (reduce DD to 2 LA).

### FI-BE3-01: beholder-escorts-limited — All thrall escorts wiped by single Fireball (table coaching note)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 19:20 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 19th cycle. Seed 494467. TPK R4.

  **FI-BE3-01 (TABLE COACHING NOTE):** Thralls A and B were clustered near the beholder at altitude (~10 ft separation), both within the Fireball blast radius. One L3 Fireball (34 fire, both failed Dex saves) killed them both in R1. Thrall C survived only because it had been directed toward Marwen (across the chamber). The escort pressure function evaporated in 1 action. Thralls (22 HP, no fire resistance) are appropriate CR 1/4 HP but clustering them enables single-Fireball wipes. **Recommendation (DM coaching, no stat change):** Add a line to `_overview.md` or the encounter setup note: "Thrall positions: stagger placement so no two thralls occupy the same 20-ft zone. This prevents a single Fireball from eliminating all escorts." The fix is scene setup, not a stat change.

### DD-TW-18-1: tank-wall — Rager durability insufficient vs smite-burst party (18th-cycle repeat)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 18:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 18th-cycle. Seed 494466. Victory R3.

  **DD-TW-18-1 (DESIGN DECISION):** Derro Rager at 52 HP collapses in Round 1 against a level-5 party with a smite-capable PC. In this run: Sabriel smite hit for 25 (10 + 15 smite), Scorching Ray added 8, Bazgar closed for 17 — total ~50 damage in Round 1. Rager was at 2 HP entering R2 and died immediately. The "tank wall" concept requires the Rager to absorb enough punishment to let Taunt redirect and Berserk fire. At 52 HP the Rager doesn't survive long enough for either mechanic to matter. This failure pattern has appeared in at least 3 independently documented TW cycles (cycle 9 FI-TW-1, cycle 12 FI-NEW-TW12-A, and now cycle 18). **Recommendation (do not auto-fix):** Consider one of: (a) HP increase to ~70-80; (b) Resistance to radiant damage (smite is the single-biggest damage source vs the Rager); (c) add a "Pain Surge" mechanic granting 10 temp HP when the Rager drops below 50% HP (one-time soak). The human author should decide which fits the creature's identity.

### DD-TW-18-2: tank-wall — CW range 30ft structurally unworkable in this formation (18th-cycle repeat)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 18:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 18th-cycle. Seed 494466.

  **DD-TW-18-2 (DESIGN DECISION — repeat of FI-TW-1 / FI-NEW-TW12-A):** Call Weakness (30ft range) cannot reliably reach the Rager in tank-wall geometry. The Rager charges 30ft on R1; the SC stays at the back line. By the time the SC acts, the Rager-SC gap is ~40-50ft. This run: SC-to-Rager distance was ~20ft before Rager charged → ~50ft after. CW used 1/3 charges on Bazgar (valid, R1 pre-charge), then 0/2 remaining charges after Rager death. 18 consecutive cycles, 0 CW charges used on a Rager in any TW run. **Recommendation (do not auto-fix):** Either raise CW range to 60ft, or add terrain direction: "The Shardcaller should start no more than 25ft behind the Rager in the tank-wall formation." The current range creates a dead ability by default.

### DD-TW-19-1: tank-wall — CW range lockout (19th-cycle confirm, action required)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 12:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 19th-cycle. Seed 494484. Victory R3.
