SC started at 70 ft from party (40 ft behind Rager at 30 ft). After Rager charged to melee (5 ft from party), SC-to-Rager gap = 65 ft — more than twice CW range. CW 3/3 charges unused at fight end. **This issue has been flagged every single tank-wall cycle since cycle 1 without resolution.** The slice's stated purpose is to test "taunt + call_weakness pairing" — CW has never successfully paired with the Rager in 19 cycles. **This warrants a morning decision: the fix is either (a) raise CW range to 60 ft in the DB spec, or (b) add a terrain setup note placing SC ≤25 ft from Rager at encounter start.** No auto-fix — author sign-off required.

### DD-TW-19-2: tank-wall — Rager durability vs Fireball (19th-cycle confirm, action required)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 12:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 19th-cycle. Seed 494484. Victory R3.

  **DD-TW-19-2 (DESIGN DECISION — 19th consecutive confirm of DD-TW-18-1):** Rager absorbed 38 dmg in R1 (Bazgar Action Surge 10 + Marwen Fireball 28), ending at 14/52 HP before Sabriel even acted. A single L3 Fireball (avg 28 dmg, both NPCs failed Dex saves) effectively removes the Rager from the fight in one action. In 19 cycles, the Rager has never survived past Round 3. Madness Endurance and Berserk are design-intent features that require the Rager to absorb hits across multiple rounds; neither mechanic gets to demonstrate its value. **Recommendation (unchanged from DD-TW-18-1):** One of (a) HP increase to 65–70, (b) resistance to fire/radiant, (c) damage-reduction trigger at ≤50% HP. Author sign-off required before any change.

### MQ-SW17-C: shrine-wedge — stagger hold release scope: "until next round" vs "until first fires" (17th-cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 16:20 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 17th-cycle. Seed 494464. Victory R3.

  **MQ-SW17-C (DESIGN DECISION):** The tactics text says the lower-initiative STD "holds Resonance for the next round." But the current implementation (and harness) releases the hold immediately when the first STD fires AR. This creates a window where, if STD-A fires early in initiative order and STD-B hasn't yet taken its turn (same round), STD-B can fire AR on its turn within the same round — effectively both ARs in R1 if initiative spread is large enough. This run demonstrated: STD-A fired at init 16, released STD-B's hold, STD-B fired at init 7 — both ARs in R1. If AR had dealt real necrotic (not the harness-bug 0), this would have been devastating (up to 20+ necrotic + psychic riders per PC, two cones). **Recommendation:** Clarify that the stagger hold lasts until "the start of the next round" after the first fires, not "immediately when the first fires." This prevents same-round double-AR while still allowing the second to fire freely next round. Mark as DESIGN DECISION — affects balance if two large cones could both fire R1 in favorable initiative.

### FI-SCT-B: shardcaller-team — CW never fires; recommend explicit R1-opener rule (15th-aggregate)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 13:19 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 15th-aggregate cycle. Seed 494461. Victory R3.

  **FI-SCT-B (DESIGN DECISION):** All 9 CW charges (3 per SC) went unused in this playtest. The root cause: with Barrage recharge 5-6, SCs frequently all have Barrage available simultaneously (SC-B and SC-C both recharged on d6=5 at the start of R2). When all SCs have Barrage, the stagger rule forces two SCs to multiattack — but the simulation stagger enforcement broke, letting all three barrage. Even with correct stagger, the pattern is: R1 barrage+barrage(stagger-correct would multiattack)+barrage(stagger-violation); rapid recharge means R2 is the same. CW only fires when a SC is explicitly multiattacking and another SC is also multiattacking (to CW cross-unit). The tactics text says "In shardcaller-only formations, stagger creates multiattack turns — CW on each other." But stagger requires per-round DM tracking that is not in the checklist (auto-fixed this run: FI-SCT-A), and CW instruction is buried in the Tactics prose.

  **Recommendation:** Add an explicit R1 opener rule to the .md: "OPENER (3 SCs): SC-A (highest init) fires Shard-Barrage; SC-B and SC-C MUST Multiattack this round and CW each other. This guarantees 2 CW activations R1 and preserves SC-A's area coverage while SCs-B/C land advantage-enhanced attacks." This converts a theoretical mechanic into a reliable table procedure. Without it, the shardcaller-team's signature coordination ability never materializes. Do NOT auto-fix without human sign-off (changes authored tactics intent).

### FI-EV9-B: empty-void — FI-EV8-A revised: Sabriel CAN smite when DD saves land (9th-cycle counter-example)

- **Context:** 2026-05-30 09:25 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 9th cycle. Seed 494481. TPK R3.

  **FI-EV9-B (DESIGN DECISION — REVISION OF FI-EV8-A):** The 8th cycle (FI-EV8-A) found "DD strips all Sabriel L2 smites — 0 smites fired, paladin identity stripped." The 9th cycle disproves this as a universal pattern. Key difference: in R2, Sabriel made her Cha save (d20+2=18 vs DC16 — a 25% pass) and retained her second L2 slot long enough to smite in R1 (L2 smite, 17 dmg) and again in R2 (L1 smite after R2 slot drain, 24 dmg). Total smite damage: ~41 HP, making Sabriel the party's primary damage dealer in 3 rounds — beholder took 53 HP total damage (most since 4th EV cycle). **Revised finding:** DD creates a ~75% per-round strip rate (DC16, Cha +2 mod → fail on 1-13). Over 2-3 DD attempts, Sabriel loses her L2 slots ~57% of the time across both attempts. In ~43% of EV runs, Sabriel retains at least one smite. FI-EV8-A's claim that paladin identity is "systematically removed" reflects the 8th cycle's extreme save-failure variance, not a guaranteed structural outcome. **The paladin identity issue is real when saves fail but is not deterministic.** No spec change needed; update mental model for balance assessments.

### FI-EV7-D: empty-void — lair rotation collapses to 2 options in solo beholder (feel note, 9th-cycle confirm)

- **Context:** First noted 2026-05-29 06:23 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 7th cycle. Confirmed 8th and 9th cycles.

  **FI-EV7-D (FEEL NOTE — 9th CONFIRM):** In the empty-void solo beholder configuration, `manifest_thralls` is a dead lair action — no thralls exist, summoning fails, action wasted. The DM-per-rules lair rotation (FI-129: do not repeat same lair action 2+ consecutive rounds) reduces to VE↔UG alternation only. This creates a mechanical repetitiveness: VE odd rounds, UG even rounds (or vice versa). The 9th cycle ran VE→UG→VE across 3 rounds — exactly the pattern. At table this is fine (2 meaningfully different lair actions), but the lair action menu looks like it has 3 options when it effectively has 2. **Low-priority fix recommendation:** Add a DM note to beholder-thrulm.md lair actions section: *"Solo configuration (no thralls): skip `manifest_thralls` from the rotation — it has no effect. Rotate between `void_eruption` and `unstable_ground` only."* This is editorial only; no spec change.

### FI-EV8-C: empty-void — paladin identity stripped by combined DD+healing-hazard+DR (feel note, new)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 14:19 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 8th cycle. Seed 494462. TPK R5.

  **FI-EV8-C (FEEL NOTE):** In the empty-void solo configuration the beholder applies three independent suppression layers to Sabriel simultaneously: (1) Disintegration Ray in the surprise round removes Marwen, stripping the party's arcane anchor; (2) Drain Divinity fires every round (after both PC turns) stripping all L2 smite slots by R2, leaving Sabriel with only L1 slots; (3) the void chamber backfire hazard blocks ALL healing spell use (Cure Wounds, Healing Word deal necrotic self-damage instead). The combined effect is that Sabriel — a paladin, whose combat identity is "heavy hitter with smite + emergency healer" — enters R3 with: no smites available, no healing spells viable, basic attack only, and LoH as her sole class feature. She landed 0 smites and 0 heals across 5 rounds. This is mechanically correct and the TPK is by design, but the *feel* question is whether a paladin should be this thoroughly identity-stripped before dying. The fight doesn't feel like "Sabriel fought and lost" — it feels like "Sabriel's toolkit was systematically removed and then she died." This may be exactly the intended horror of Thrulm, or it may want a small opening window.

  **Recommendation:** Consider adding one of: (a) a single-use Thrulm lore roll (DC 15 Religion) on approach that tells Sabriel "healing magic backfires here" — so the healing suppression is known/navigable, not a surprise ambush; (b) confirm in the beholder's Weaknesses section that sanctified dwarven weapons bypass the DD drain (i.e., holy weapon enchantment is not a "spell slot" and thus not DD-targetable) to preserve one divine identity hook. Neither is an auto-fix; log for human review.

### FI-SCT-C: shardcaller-team — PTV disadv cascade makes Dex saves near-impossible (feel note)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 13:19 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 15th-aggregate cycle. Seed 494461.

  **FI-SCT-C (FEEL NOTE):** Pack Tactics Voice applies disadvantage to the NEXT saving throw a hit target makes. With 3 SCs and barrage recharge 5-6, the PTV curse is perpetually refreshed — every barrage targets someone who was already hit this round or last. All 6 Dex saves against barrages in rounds 1-2 were failed (saves: 7,5,6,6,8,4,7,5 — all vs DC 13). Bazgar's +1 Dex modifier and Marwen's +2 Dex modifier are essentially negated. This is mechanically correct per the spec ("Toggle, not stackable — multiple hits refresh the duration"), but the table experience is "we always fail these saves." At a real table, players will notice and may feel the mechanic is invisible (they don't see why they keep failing). **Recommendation:** Add a DM callout phrase to the start-of-turn checklist PTV note: "announce 'Voice marks you' when the ally hit lands — players should know the disadv is pending." This is a presentation fix, not a mechanics fix. Do NOT auto-fix the spec.

### FI-SRR-B: solo-rager-rush — Berserk fizzle vs AC 18-19 (5th consecutive cycle confirm)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 12:20 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 14th cycle. Seed 494460. Victory R8.

  **FI-SRR-B (DESIGN DECISION):** Berserk (recharge 5-6, +4 to-hit) vs the Compass Edge's front line (AC 18-19) yields only 30-35% hit rate even with Madness Endurance +1. In this cycle: R2 Rager-A Berserk hits all 3 PCs (all in melee, lucky seed), but R3 Rager-A Berserk misses both surviving targets (AC 18 and 19) despite recharging. R4 Rager-B Berserk also misses both surviving targets. R5 Rager-C correctly skips Berserk (1 target) and uses Multiattack instead. Pattern: Berserk frequently fires (5-6 recharge = 33% per round, and clustered ragers often satisfy the "2+ in reach" prereq) but against a heavy-armor party it often produces 0 hits. This is the 5th consecutive solo-rager cycle confirming the pattern (prior cycles also logged Berserk fizzle at low HP in tank-wall).

  The feel issue is "full-Berserk, no hits" — a high-drama action that resolves as dead weight. This is especially pronounced in R4 of this cycle where Rager-B spent its action on Berserk (no-move prereq) and hit nothing, while Multiattack would have had the same hit rate but recovered freedom of movement.

  **Recommendation:** One of: (a) reduce recharge to 4-6 (44% per round) to compensate for low hit rate, (b) add a consolation effect on zero hits ("Rager gains advantage on next attack roll" — "the spin finds its momentum"), or (c) add a minimum damage on Berserk even on miss (pushed 5 ft, frightened 1 round DC 10 — "the sweep forces a dodge"). Current version: feels high-risk, frequently low-reward vs armored PCs. Do NOT auto-fix (balance call).

### FI-FC13-F: final-confrontation — correct beholder play → 2-round TPK with zero PC counterplay window (13th-cycle confirm)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 11:16 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 13th cycle. Seed 494459. TPK R2.

  **FI-FC13-F (DESIGN DECISION):** The full final-confrontation encounter resolves as a 2–3 round TPK in the majority of cycles where all major abilities fire correctly. The beholder correctly held VS in R1 (chose DR instead — range 120 ft vs VS 30 ft radius; DR fires at range, VS requires descent), then descended and fired VS in R2, winding down the fight before the party had meaningful turns against the beholder. Beholder took 0 HP across 13 FC cycles. Party counterplay consists of: clearing thralls (partial — 1 of 4 killed by Fireball) and wounding STDs (STD-B 19/45 HP). Bazgar never reached beholder melee. Sabriel never landed a smite on beholder.

  The pattern is not a bug — it's the encounter behaving as designed (CR13 vs L5 = TPK). The question is **whether a 2-round TPK feels "earned"** vs "overwhelming." The party had meaningful turns (Fireball, DD resistance, Bazgar attacks) but nothing to show for it against the beholder. If the design intent is "the party should feel like they fought before losing," the beholder may need a structural weakness that occasionally lets the party land meaningful damage: e.g., the sanctified weapon rider (+1d8 if Sabriel wields one) or the holy water flee mechanic. Currently, neither of these surfaces in the simulation because the fight ends before they can be established.

  **Recommendation:** Add a callout in the beholder-thrulm .md's Tactics section: "At-table pace note: if the fight ends in fewer than 3 rounds with no hits on the beholder, consider rolling back VS to R3 or starting the encounter with 2 thralls instead of 4 — the party should feel the pressure, not skip directly to death." Do NOT auto-fix (table-culture call for the DM).

### FI-NEW-BEL10-B: beholder-escorts-limited — Drain Divinity monopolizes legendary action economy (10th-cycle new)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 10:26 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 10th cycle. Seed 494458. Victory R6.

  **FI-NEW-BEL10-B (DESIGN DECISION):** Drain Divinity costs 3 LA — the beholder's entire per-round legendary budget. In every round where a living slot-holder was within 30 ft, the beholder fired DD after the first PC's end-of-turn, consuming all 3 LA. Void Ray (2 LA) and Tentacle Lash (1 LA) never fired as legendary actions across 6 rounds. The "legendary" sequence became: DD after PC-1 → nothing after PC-2 → nothing after PC-3. No VR force chip, no Tentacle harass. The monotony is doubly confirmed in empty-void cycles (where DD vs VR priority is the same). **Recommendation:** (a) Reduce DD to 2 LA so it competes with VR rather than consuming everything — the beholder then gets DD (2 LA) after the first PC's turn and VR (2 LA) or TL (1 LA) after a second PC's turn. Or (b) add a cap: "DD once per round, even if LA budget is available." The effect (slot drain pressure + additional LA damage) would feel much richer with option (a). Do NOT auto-fix — spec change required.

### FI-TW-1 (9th-cycle confirm): tank-wall — Call Weakness structurally dead in standard formation

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 09:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 9th cycle. Seed 494457. Victory R4.

  **FI-TW-1 (9th-cycle confirm of DD-41 / FI-163):** CW 3/3 charges unused again. SC started 50 ft from party; Rager engaged at 10 ft from party → SC-to-Rager gap ~40 ft throughout, exceeding the 30-ft CW range. Across all tank-wall cycles, CW fired on the Rager in exactly 1 of 9 cycles (cycle 3, SC won initiative, advantage uncollected as Rager rolled nat-1). The slice is labelled "tests taunt + call_weakness pairing" but CW paired zero times out of nine. **FI-TW-2 (secondary):** Rager Berserk fizzled at 12 HP in R2 — all 3 attacks missed (rolls 11/5/6+4). The Rager's climactic ability failed to land before death. Both issues should be considered together when redesigning the slice.

  **Recommendation (same as FI-163):** Either (a) reposition SC to 20–25 ft from party start (SC-to-Rager gap ≤30 ft at engagement point, enabling R1 CW), (b) extend CW range to 60 ft in the spec, or (c) rename the slice and test something the formation actually exercises. If (a), validate that the new SC position still prevents one-round elimination by the party. Do NOT auto-fix.

### FI-SW-8-A: shrine-wedge — outcome near-deterministically linked to initiative (8th-cycle confirm)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 08:17 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 8th cycle. Seed 494456. Victory R2.

  **FI-SW-8-A (DESIGN DECISION, 8th-cycle confirm of FI-159):** Across 8 shrine-wedge cycles, the primary determinant of outcome is who wins initiative. In the 5 VICTORY cycles, the party won the overall initiative block and Fireball/Action Surge landed before STD-A could fire AR. In the 3 TPK cycles, STD-A won initiative, fired AR before any PC acted, and all 3 PCs failed DC 14 Dex saves. The encounter's tension lives almost entirely in the initiative roll rather than in positioning or tactical decisions. Recommendation: consider one or more of — (a) giving the party a scouting/surprise option to close initiative variance; (b) reducing DC to 12 so AR is threatening but not save-or-suffer; (c) requiring 2+ PCs in melee range (not just "in cone") before AR fires. Do NOT auto-fix; this changes encounter design.

### FI-TP-1: threshold-patrol — SC needs column cover to survive past R2 (DM guidance, 16th-cycle)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 15:19 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 16th cycle. Seed 494463. Victory R4.

  **FI-TP-1 (DM GUIDANCE NOTE):** The Shardcaller entered R3 at 2 HP and was killed by Sabriel's first attack before getting a turn. In this run, the SC spent R2 firing shard-throws at Marwen (killing her) but absorbed Sabriel's full R2 assault (two hits, 10+11 radiant). The result: SC never fired a second Barrage (which recharged naturally at the start of R3 — there is no way to use it, the SC died before acting), never triggered Call Weakness in a productive way, and never attempted Tactical Retreat.

  The SC's .md states it fights from "40–60 ft behind the front line" and uses terrain columns for cover, but no column placement is specified in the encounter layout. Without explicit column placement in the DM setup notes, SC is typically played in open ground where focus-fire collapses it in R2.

  **Recommendation:** Add a DM setup bullet to the threshold-patrol encounter description (in `encounters.md` or `_overview.md`) specifying that the SC starts behind a column that requires a PC to spend 15 ft of lateral movement to get line-of-sight. This prevents R1 attacks on the SC from both Bazgar (melee) and Sabriel (ranged), buying the SC a second meaningful turn. Not a spec change — this is a DM setup note. Do NOT auto-fix the NPC .md itself; the tactics are correctly authored. The gap is in encounter terrain setup.

### FI-TP11-C: threshold-patrol — Shardcaller CW 3/day structurally wasted in short TP fights (DESIGN DECISION)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 07:19 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 11th cycle. Seed 494455. Victory R3.

  **FI-TP11-C (DESIGN DECISION, 11th-cycle confirm of FI-TP9-A pattern):** In threshold-patrol, the shardcaller fights alongside 2 DW allies who typically die within 2 rounds. SC's Call Weakness (3/day) is structurally bottlenecked: CW can only fire on a living DW ally with >20 HP who hasn't already acted this round (per DD-39/MQ-12/MQ-27). DW-B typically takes damage from Bazgar before SC's bonus action in R2, pushing DW-B to ≤20 HP and triggering the DD-8/DD-25 guard. Result: CW fires at most once (R1 on DW-B, correct), then is withheld for the rest of the fight. SC ends every TP fight with 2/3 charges unused. Over 11 cycles, CW has fired productively exactly once (this cycle: DW-B collected advantage, landed 2 hits for 10 dmg). Recommendation: either reduce CW to 1/day in this formation (matching the structural availability), or adjust DW HP upward to survive into R3+ where CW can cycle multiple times. Do NOT auto-fix; this changes encounter design.

### FI-TP-0-B: threshold-patrol — CW 3/day dead weight in patrol formation; 0/3 charges usefully fired (1st-cycle 2026-05-31)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 11:24 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 1st-cycle in this rotation pass. Seed 494507. Victory R3.

  **FI-TP-0-B (DESIGN DECISION, reinforces FI-TP11-C):** This confirms the structural CW lockout from a new angle. In this run, Bazgar (init 14) acted before SC (init 12) and drove DW-A from 27 → 12HP in R1 before SC's bonus action. By the time SC moved, DW-A (12HP) and DW-B (1HP after Sabriel R1 smite) both violated the ≤20HP DD-8/DD-25 guard. SC had zero valid CW targets and should have held all 3 charges. Sim incorrectly spent CW on DW-A at 12HP — this is a sim fidelity note, not a DB bug. The underlying design issue is real: in the standard patrol formation, the DWDs lose HP faster than SC can usefully deploy CW. Unless SC wins initiative over all PCs (≤30% of runs), CW is dead on arrival. Across all threshold-patrol cycles, CW has fired usefully exactly 0 times in >15 cycles. **Recommendation (same as FI-TP11-C):** either reduce CW to 1/day in patrol formation context, or increase DWD HP to 35+ so they survive to R2+ with >20HP. Do NOT auto-fix.

### MQ-TP-0-B: threshold-patrol — SC/DW-B initiative tie determines CW validity; tie-breaking not specified in encounter (1st-cycle 2026-05-31)

- **Context:** 2026-05-31 11:24 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 1st-cycle. Seed 494507. Victory R3.

  **MQ-TP-0-B (MECHANICAL QUESTION):** SC and DW-B both rolled init=12 (after Dex mod). When SC acts BEFORE DW-B in a tie, SC can Call Weakness on DW-B (27HP, valid) giving advantage before DW-B's first attack — this is the tactically optimal play per the shardcaller checklist (highest-init ally who hasn't acted). When DW-B acts first (my sim assumption, DW before SC), DW-B has already acted and the ≤20HP window closes within the round. The tie-breaking direction is a meaningful tactical swing — roughly 0.75 CW advantage per fight if SC wins ties vs 0 if SC loses them. **Recommendation:** Add a DM note to the shardcaller .md or the encounters.md: "In threshold-patrol, the Shardcaller holds its initiative position — in initiative ties with DW allies, the DW acts first (they are trained soldiers who react faster), so SC's CW window is R1-only if SC wins initiative over all PCs." This makes the intended flow explicit and avoids ambiguity. Do NOT auto-fix .md without human sign-off.

### FI-EV7-C: empty-void — Drain Divinity DC 16 may be too low vs Cha-save paladin (DESIGN DECISION)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 06:23 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 7th cycle. Seed 494454. Indeterminate R3.

  **FI-EV7-C:** Sabriel saved against Drain Divinity at *exactly DC 16* twice in consecutive rounds (R1 and R2, d20=16+0=16 both times). A level 5 paladin with Cha +3 has Cha save +6 total — she saves on a d20=10 or higher (55% save rate). The beholder's 3-legendary-action "strip divine power" ability succeeds only 43% of the time against Sabriel. For the beholder's most expensive LA option (3 = full budget), this feels inconsistently threatening against its primary intended target. Recommendation: raise DD DC to 17 (50/50 vs Sabriel) or 18 (43% save rate). This is a change to the spec — needs human sign-off. Do NOT auto-fix.

### MQ-EV7-B: empty-void — Surprise round vs. beholder initiative advantage (DESIGN DECISION)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 06:23 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 7th cycle.

  **MQ-EV7-B:** The beholder's Dex +8 means it wins initiative against the Compass Edge party in ~75% of rolls (needs d20=1-9 to lose). In this run it rolled 24 (Dex+8 on d20=16) and Sabriel rolled 18. The "hard threat = surprise round" rule in the beholder .md (FI-NEW-EV5-B) adds overhead (flat-footed tracking, surprise adjudication) for a scenario where the beholder would go first anyway most of the time. 7th EV cycle: beholder has won natural initiative 5/7 runs. Recommendation: remove the surprise round from the hard-threat trigger; state instead that the beholder acts on the result of its natural initiative roll (which is almost always first). The punishing *feel* of "you threatened it and now it's shooting first" is preserved without the mechanical complexity of surprise. Needs human sign-off.

### FI-35: shardcaller-team — Pack Tactics Voice structurally blocked by initiative math (DESIGN DECISION)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 05:24 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 5th cycle. Seed 494453. Victory R3.

  **FI-35 (DESIGN DECISION): PTV reliably triggers but never pays off against a Barrage save.** Root cause: the shardcaller cannot Barrage and multiattack in the same turn. The stagger rule means the Barrage-firing SC (highest init) acts BEFORE the other SCs multiattack — so PTV from a multiattack hit always trails the Barrage by one round. Cross-round PTV consumption is blocked by initiative order: Marwen (init 15) acts before SC-C's Barrage window (init 14), so the PTV disadv expires before SC-C can fire. Across 5 SC-team cycles, PTV has triggered 3 times and been consumed 0 times against a Barrage save.

  **Options:**
  - Change PTV to grant disadvantage on the next **attack roll** (not save) — this would benefit melee allies (Rager) but shardcallers have no melee allies in this slice.
  - Change PTV to trigger *before* the Barrage-SC acts: e.g. "when this creature fires Shard-Barrage, each target within 30 ft who was hit by an ally since the start of this creature's last turn has disadv on the Barrage save." This makes PTV a Barrage rider rather than a passive.
  - Accept that PTV is a nice-to-have bonus that only pays off in specific initiative orders, not a reliable mechanic.

### FI-37: shardcaller-team — Tactical Retreat distance razor-thin vs 30 ft PC speed (DESIGN DECISION)

- **Context:** 2026-05-29 05:24 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 5th cycle. DD-47 RESOLVED.

  **FI-37 (DESIGN QUESTION): TR grants 30 ft of retreat movement. A Fighter with 30 ft speed can spend their full move to close exactly 30 ft, nullifying the retreat.** In this cycle, SC-A retreated 30 ft (to ~35 ft from Bazgar's new position) and Bazgar moved 30 ft to close the gap, ending up 5 ft away and attacking. The "kiting" escape only works if the SC has a head start or there's terrain (column, corner) that adds pathing distance. On an open vault floor, TR is a temporary delay, not guaranteed escape.

  **Decision needed:** Is this razor-thin tension intentional (creates dramatic "almost got away" moments) or should TR retreat 40 ft to guarantee escape vs standard 30 ft PCs? If intentional, add a DM note to encounter header: "SCs' TR only guarantees escape if there are columns between them and melee PCs — place 2–3 columns in the vault's mid-section."

### FI-NEW-SRR2 / MQ-NEW-SRR2: solo-rager-rush — "taunt-induced movement" is undefined (DESIGN DECISION)

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 18:19 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 13th cycle. Seed 494442. Indeterminate R3; projected PC victory R4–5.

  **FI-NEW-SRR2 / MQ-NEW-SRR2 (DESIGN DECISION): The slice #5 test description says "Tests berserk recharge, aggro-mark riders, taunt-induced movement." Taunt has no movement component whatsoever — it only grants disadvantage on attack rolls vs non-rager targets.** There is nothing in the Taunt spec (DB or .md) that forces, incentivizes, or rewards PC movement toward the rager. "Taunt-induced movement" in the slice description is ambiguous:

  - **(Interpretation A)** "The rager moves toward its taunted target" — narrative only, no mechanical compulsion on the PC. This is what the current Taunt does implicitly (rager wants to stay in reach of its taunted prey), but it's not a mechanic to test.
  - **(Interpretation B)** "The PC is compelled to move toward the rager on a failed save" — not in the current spec. Would require adding a movement-compulsion rider (e.g. "on a failed save, target must spend its movement moving toward the rager on its next turn").

  **Recommendation:** If movement-compulsion was the intended design, add it as an explicit rider. If purely narrative, update the slice #5 description to "Tests berserk recharge, aggro-mark riders, and taunt coverage in rager-only formation" (remove "movement"). Either way, the current slice test cannot verify a mechanic that doesn't exist.

### FI-NEW-SRR1: solo-rager-rush — Berserk saturation in 3-rager clustered fights

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 18:19 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 13th cycle.

  **FI-NEW-SRR1 (FEEL ISSUE): With 3 PCs clustered and all 3 ragers in melee reach, Berserk fires 4 times across 3 rounds** (R3 in R1, R2 in R2, R1 in R3, R3 in R3). Recharge 5–6 means each rager has a ~33% chance to recover each turn; with 3 independent ragers, at least one Berserk fires almost every round once first-uses are spent. The "desperate all-or-nothing sweep" feel is diluted when Berserk is a near-constant AoE pattern.

  **Options for human review:**
  - **(A) Accept it** — three CR2 ragers vs a level-5 party is already heavily stacked for the party; the constant Berserk pressure is appropriate for an overwhelming encounter design.
  - **(B) Raise recharge to 6-only** — reduces per-rager Berserk frequency from 33% to 17% per turn. In a 3v3 fight, 50% chance at least one fires (vs ~68% at 5-6). More "desperate moment" feel.
  - **(C) Gate Berserk on below-half HP** — "only when HP ≤ 26" — fits the cornered-animal narrative and prevents R1 Berserk openers.

### FI-NEW-SRR3: solo-rager-rush — excessive manual tracking overhead for 3-rager formation

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 18:19 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 13th cycle.

  **FI-NEW-SRR3 (FEEL/DM-OVERHEAD): A 3-rager encounter requires tracking 12 independent state variables:** 3× Madness Endurance (+1 to-hit if took damage), 3× Incoming Damage Aggro (advantage vs last attacker), 3× Berserk recharge die, 3× active Taunt target. All four are "DM applies manually" and none are surfaced in the dispatch output.

  At a live table this is significant cognitive load for a CR2 minion type. Compared to the beholder (which has similarly many variables but is a solo, unique monster), the rager's complexity-per-unit-count is higher.

  **Recommendation:** Consider one of:
  - Drop Incoming Damage Aggro entirely (thematically redundant with Madness Endurance — both reward "hit the rager and it hits harder back").
  - Encode Madness Endurance as a `rider_on_hit` note in the multiattack/berserk DB specs so the dispatch output reminds the DM: "DM: if this rager took damage last turn, add +1 to the printed to-hit values."
  - Leave as-is for solo-rager encounters where one DM tracks one rager; note it as a "3-rager complexity warning" in the encounter overview.

### FI-NEW-BEL3-A: beholder-escorts-limited — VS round-1 Marwen one-shot (feel issue)

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 16:00 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited). Seed 494440. TPK R2. Phase A 28/28 clean (DD-10 27th consecutive network-block). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  **FI-NEW-BEL3-A (FEEL NOTE): Void Scream fires R1 and nearly one-shots Marwen before she takes a second turn.** The beholder starts with VS available and can descend via shrine_drift (OA-safe) on its first turn to bring the whole party into the 30-ft radius. Average 6d10=33 psychic one-shots Marwen (32 HP) ~60% of the time even on a failed save (she has no HP buffer). With any prior damage (ThrallA hit for 5 in this run) the threshold drops to near 100%.

  Result: Marwen has one meaningful action (Hypnotic Pattern here, which fizzled on beholder's Wis +7), then is removed from combat for the rest of the fight. For an overwhelming-by-design encounter this may be acceptable, but if the intent is for the party to feel the full encounter before dying, Marwen's arc is "cast one spell, unconscious forever."

  **Options:**
  - **(A) Accept it** — the beholder is CR 13 vs level-5 party. VS is supposed to be decisive. Marwen's role in the fight is "first to fall, forcing Sabriel LoH decisions."
  - **(B) Add a tactical gate:** tactics note says "use VS the moment it's recharged." Consider revising to "use VS R2+ to allow at least one full exchange; R1 use Multiattack instead." This would not change the fight outcome (party still loses) but gives the caster one more exchange and makes the fight feel less instant.
  - **(C) Bump Marwen's max HP** in the roster (currently 32 = wizard minimum). A d6 hit die wizard at level 5 with Con 10 = 17 HP + 4×3.5avg = 31 HP. If Con 12 (+1), max-first-die: 6+5×4+5 = 31 HP. Not much headroom. If Joe wants Marwen to survive one VS hit on average, she'd need ~34+ HP (saving half of 6d10=16.5+1=17.5; needs 34 HP to not die from the half-damage hit on top of 5-ish prior damage).

  **Recommendation:** (A) — accept for slice-3. Log for human review. If Marwen consistently dying on beholder's first turn (regardless of slice) becomes a pattern, revisit.

### FI-NEW-TW12-A: tank-wall 12th-cycle — Call Weakness 30-ft range structurally unworkable in 2-NPC formation

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 15:18 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 12th cycle. Seed 494439. VICTORY R6 — Bazgar 19/49, Marwen DOWN R3, Sabriel 17/44. Phase A 28/28 clean (DD-10 26th consecutive network-block). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  **FI-NEW-TW12-A (DESIGN DECISION — 12th confirm): CW 30-ft range is structurally insufficient in the Rager+SC formation.** Across all 12 tank-wall cycles, CW has fired **0 times on the Rager after R1** and fires in R1 only when SC wins initiative over Rager (~50% of cycles). In this cycle, SC and Rager tied initiative (both 4); Rager acted first per sim order; Rager charged to melee (~50 ft from SC) before SC's turn; CW was permanently out of range. Across the fight, SC's flagship tactical mechanic (Advantage on ally attack rolls) contributed 0 combat value for 6 rounds and 3 wasted charges.

  **Root cause:** the Shardcaller's "back-line, 40–60 ft from enemies" positioning puts it permanently outside the 30-ft CW window once the Rager closes to melee. The only window is R1 pre-charge, which requires SC to act before the Rager — a coin flip at best.

  **Options for human review:**
  - **(A) Increase CW range to 60 ft** — doubles the usable window; CW would reach a melee Rager when SC is at 50 ft. Cleanest fix; no positioning compromise required.
  - **(B) Add terrain note to TW encounter setup:** SC starts 20–30 ft behind Rager (not 50 ft). SC uses Barrage R1 + CW R1 (they don't conflict — CW is bonus, Barrage is main action). This makes CW available R1 regardless of initiative and keeps it in range through R2. No spec change needed.
  - **(C) Accept the lockout** — argue that CW's value is felt in multi-SC formations (shardcaller-team slice) and tank-wall is just an unlucky formation for the mechanic. But then the TW-specific "call out the Rager's opening" flavor never fires at the table.

  **Recommendation:** Option (A) with a note that CW on a charging melee ally (range 60 ft) is already lore-consistent ("voice carries strangely far, like the stone repeats it").

### FI-NEW-SW7-A: shrine-wedge 7th-cycle — STD Wis +0 too low vs Hypnotic Pattern DC 15

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 14:30 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 7th cycle. Seed 494438. TPK R7 (SIM BUG: HP incapacitation not enforced — true result likely VICTORY ~R3). Phase A 28/28 clean (25th consecutive network-block). 2 bugs auto-fixed (MQ-55, stagger low-HP note).

  **FI-NEW-SW7-A (DESIGN DECISION): Shrine-touched Wis save +0 too low vs Hypnotic Pattern (DC 15).** Across 7 shrine-wedge cycles, both STDs fail HP saves on the same turn in most cycles where Marwen casts it (this run: 5 and 3). At +0, STDs have 75% per-STD fail rate, meaning ~56% chance BOTH fail simultaneously. When both are locked, the encounter is over — PCs kill helpless STDs with advantage in 2-3 rounds at zero risk. The fight outcome is essentially: "Did STD2 fire AR before Marwen acted?" (Yes → extended fight; No → VICTORY via HP). Options: (A) Give Shrine-Touched Wis proficiency (+2, reduces double-lock chance to ~42%); (B) Add shrine-vicinity Wis advantage (near altar, already immune charmed/frightened — lore-consistent); (C) Accept init-dependence as designed (FI-159 remains open). **Human decision required — do not auto-fix spec.**

### FI-NEW-EV6-A / FI-NEW-EV6-B / FI-NEW-EV6-C / FI-NEW-EV6-D: empty-void 6th-cycle — RECORD damage 70 HP; FI-184 smite partial break; DD-on-unconscious gap auto-fixed; neg pacing positive

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 12:28 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 6th cycle. Seed 494436. TPK R5 (Marwen DISINTEGRATED surprise, Bazgar DISINTEGRATED R4, Sabriel DEAD R5). Beholder **40/110 HP** remaining — highest party damage across all 6 EV cycles. Phase A 28/28 clean (DD-10 23rd consecutive network-block). 1 bug auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-NEW-EV6-A (RECORD EV DAMAGE — design data point, no fix needed):** Party dealt ~70 HP (sim) / ~80-90 HP (corrected for AS shortfall) to the beholder — ~64% of its HP pool, compared to 50-63% in prior cycles. Enabling factor: Sabriel won initiative (21 > beholder 16) allowing her to land a smite before VS suppressed all PC agency. **Pattern confirmed:** beholder's solo combat output is dramatically shaped by initiative order. When beholder goes first → party enters R1 blunted; when party goes first → they get 1-2 meaningful actions before VS fires. This is not necessarily a problem (it mirrors the unpredictability of solo-boss encounters) but worth noting at table: "this fight can look very different depending on who rolls well for initiative."

  2. **FI-NEW-EV6-B (FI-184 PARTIAL BREAK — DESIGN DATA POINT):** Sabriel finally deployed a smite in an EV cycle (L2 Divine Smite = 16 damage R1). Previous 5 EV cycles: 0 smites. This breaks the streak. Root cause of prior streak: Sabriel was always killed before she could act (beholder winning initiative → VS before Sabriel's turn, or DR one-shotting her). This cycle: init 21 let her act first. **Conclusion:** FI-184 (smite-stranding) is primarily an initiative-dependence issue, not a structural slot-stranding problem with the class design. Sabriel *will* use smites when she acts before the beholder.

  3. **FI-NEW-EV6-C (AUTO-FIXED):** In R4, beholder spent 3 LA (Drain Divinity) on unconscious Sabriel (still had slots) while Bazgar (7 HP, no Action Surge left) was attacking freely in melee. Optimal play: VR (2 LA) + Tentacle (1 LA) on Bazgar to kill him faster. An unconscious target cannot heal, smite, or threaten — the standing fighter is the active risk. Added note to beholder-thrulm.md Legendary priority order: "**DD on unconscious target (FI-NEW-EV6-C):** if any standing threat is in melee range, downgrade to VR+Tentacle (2+1 LA) instead of DD (3 LA)."

  4. **FI-NEW-EV6-D (FEEL POSITIVE — neg pacing FI-NEW-EV5-B fix confirmed):** The 2-exchange minimum before combat trigger (FI-NEW-EV5-B fix) played out exactly right. Marwen passed Arcana (19, intrigued beholder), Sabriel failed Persuasion (7, beholder suspicious), then Bazgar triggered combat by explicitly stating lower-shaft intent. The sequence felt dramatic and earned — Bazgar's impatience caused the fight, and the party paid for it immediately.

### FI-NEW-FC4-A / FI-NEW-FC4-B / FI-NEW-FC4-C / MQ-NEW-FC4-D: final-confrontation 1st-cycle — TPK R2; 63% beholder HP; VS overkill; thrall finishing blow; DR to-hit vs save discrepancy

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 07:26 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 1st cycle. Seed 494431. TPK R2. Beholder 70/110 HP. Party dealt only 40 HP total damage. Phase A 28/28 clean (21st consecutive network-block). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-NEW-FC4-A (DESIGN DECISION): 2-round TPK at 63% beholder HP — party had almost no agency.** DR evaporated Marwen R1 (immediately LoH-revived by Sabriel), VS killed Bazgar R2 from 9 HP, thrall swarm finished Sabriel at 6 HP. PCs collectively landed one longsword hit (11 dmg) and one Fireball (29 dmg). The beholder won without legendary resistance, without all LAs, and without DR recharging. **Design question:** Is this the intended feel for the "final confrontation" slice — a 2-round demonstration of overwhelming power — or should the party last 4-5 rounds and reach ~50% beholder HP before the TPK? The difference is whether this slice is a "taste of doom" (current) or a "hard-fought loss" (target). If the latter, consider: (A) reducing thrall count from 4 to 2 (thrall swarm was 30+ damage on Sabriel); (B) giving Bazgar/Sabriel reaction abilities; (C) Thrulm holding VS until R3 (per tactics "be patient"). **Do not auto-fix — fundamental balance question for human.**

  2. **FI-NEW-FC4-B (VS overkill / FI-149 3rd FC-context confirm): VS killed Bazgar (9 HP → 42 psychic overkill); fear rider immediately wasted.** Bazgar was softened by lair void_eruption (21→9 HP) then one-shotted by VS. The fear rider (disadvantage on Bazgar's attacks for 2-3 rounds, per FI-149) never applied — he was unconscious before his next turn. FI-149 notes this as a known pattern: VS fear rider only matters if the target *survives* VS. With a melee-heavy party that closes on the beholder, VS at sub-20 HP frequently overkills rather than debuffing. **Log only; no fix — this is inherent to the mechanic and the lair softening pattern.**

  3. **FI-NEW-FC4-C (feel gap): Final killing blow was Thrall2 (CR 1/4) dagger on Sabriel at 6 HP.** Three thralls consecutively hit Sabriel for 5+6+6=17 damage after VS dropped Bazgar and the beholder's main action was spent. The swarm-finish is narratively coherent but may feel anticlimactic at the table — "the void-beholder's thralls killed me, not the beholder." **Log for human; consider narration guidance** — *"Thrulm watches from 60 ft as its thralls finish the last defender; it doesn't need to spend resources on what's already broken."* Alternatively, if the human wants the beholder to land the final blow, add a tactics note: "Below 3 PCs, use VS or DR as soon as available rather than waiting for optimal positioning."

  4. **MQ-NEW-FC4-D (DESIGN DECISION + simulation note): Disintegration Ray spec is to-hit (+6), not a save.** The DB defines DR as `single_attack` with `to_hit_bonus: 6`. The Phase A regression dispatch rolled to-hit 12, which misses Marwen AC15. The sim used Dex-save resolution instead (Marwen rolled 15 vs DC16, just failed, took 39 dmg and died). If the actual dispatch result had been used in the playtest, Marwen would have SURVIVED R1 (DR missed), Sabriel wouldn't need LoH, and the fight would extend. Standard 5e beholder lore uses a Dex/Con save for disintegrate — the to-hit implementation diverges. **Two separate actions needed:** (A) Fix simulation to use the DB dispatch to-hit result directly (harness bug); (B) Human review: was to-hit intentional for this non-standard beholder? If yes, add a line to beholder-thrulm.md tactics section noting "Disintegration Ray is a ranged *attack*, not a save — roll to-hit, not a save throw." **Do not auto-fix the DB spec until human confirms intent.**

### FI-NEW-BEL6-A / FI-NEW-BEL6-B / FI-NEW-BEL6-C / FI-NEW-BEL6-D / MQ-NEW-BEL6-A / MQ-NEW-BEL6-B: beholder-escorts-limited 6th-cycle — TPK R5; VS R1 6th-confirm; Sabriel smite-stranding 5th BEL confirm; compel_thrall dead weight; VS 2nd-fire dramatic close; FI-128 POSITIVE; multiattack sim targets downed PCs; lair-on-downed auto-fixed

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 06:00 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 6th cycle. Seed 494430. TPK R5 (Bazgar DOWN R2 T2 tentacle 16 bludg; Sabriel DOWN R2 Maw 17 piercing; Marwen DOWN R5 VS 2nd fire 34 psychic at 5 HP). Beholder 57/110 HP. Party dealt 53 total damage to beholder. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 20th consecutive network-block). 1 authoring fix applied.

  1. **FI-NEW-BEL6-A (6th-cycle confirm FI-165 — DESIGN DECISION): VS R1 opener with beholder winning init (21) → 40 psychic → Bazgar 9/49 + frightened, Sabriel 4/44 + frightened before either PC acts.** This pattern has occurred in 5 of 6 BEL cycles (the exception being the 5th cycle where VS was accidentally omitted from the sim harness, FI-194). Both melee fighters miss all attacks at disadvantage (frightened); the fight becomes Marwen alone vs. beholder from turn 2. The VS 30-ft radius at 30-ft altitude catches both melee PCs; Marwen correctly stays at 40 ft to stay out of range. **Design question:** Is this R1 VS elimination acceptable as the intended feel? The party has no counterplay unless Sabriel has a readied action or Marwen goes before the beholder and disrupts it. If the intent is genuine counterplay, consider: (A) VS recharge-5 (more frequent but requires held preparation); (B) the beholder holds VS for R2 to let the party close before using it; (C) VS 25-ft radius (slightly smaller, less total-party catch). Current feel is "if beholder wins init, fight is decided in 30 seconds." **Do not auto-fix — requires human design intent decision.**

  2. **FI-NEW-BEL6-B (5th consecutive BEL cycle confirm FI-184 — DESIGN DECISION): Sabriel's smite slots entirely intact at death — all L1×4, L2×3, L3×2 unused.** Downed in R2 by Maw (17 piercing) from 4 HP after VS opener. FI-125 LoH-loop countermeasure never triggered (Sabriel never survived to use LoH). Five consecutive BEL cycles where Sabriel contributes zero smite damage. Her AC19 doesn't protect her at 4 HP. **Implication:** In BEL, Sabriel functions as a damage sponge for the VS opener rather than a divine combatant. Her HP pool (44) is not enough buffer after a 40-psychic VS hit. **Possible mitigations:** Sabriel readies an attack before beholder acts; party delays entering the vault until after beholder's initiative count (unlikely at table); Sabriel uses the Action to Dodge in R1 (disadvantage on all attacks against her). All require metagame knowledge of VS threat. **Log for human; no auto-fix.**

  3. **FI-NEW-BEL6-C (new feel issue): `compel_thrall` bonus action dead weight after melee PCs are downed.** Beholder spent 4 consecutive bonus actions directing Thrall-A toward Marwen (R2–R5), but Thrall-A hit 0/4 attempts (+1 to-hit vs AC15 — 35% base; rolled 9, 12, 8, 8). Once both melee PCs are down, `shrine_drift` would be more useful (close on Marwen for VS range; reposition safely). The compel_thrall Cha save is DC16 — many thralls resist it entirely. **Recommendation:** Add a tactics sentence: *"Once all melee-range PCs are downed, switch bonus action from compel_thrall to shrine_drift — there is no worthwhile redirect target."* Low-risk editorial; can auto-fix next cycle if confirmed.

  4. **FI-NEW-BEL6-D (new, POSITIVE feel): VS second fire at R5 (d6=6 on 4th recharge check) delivers killing blow to last-standing Marwen at 5 HP.** Marwen missed the DC16 Wis save by exactly 1 (rolled 15). The suspense of 4 consecutive failed recharge checks (d6: 5, 4, 2, then 6) made the eventual second VS firing feel earned. At-table this would be a dramatic moment. **Positive finding:** recharge-6 mechanic is working as intended — rare enough to feel like a "comeback" when it fires, but guaranteed in a 5+-round fight.

  5. **FI-NEW-BEL6-E (POSITIVE, FI-128 fix confirmed working):** Beholder correctly chose VR (2 LA, 22 force) over DD (3 LA, +2 temp HP) in R4 when Marwen's highest remaining slot was L1. FI-128 fix ("DD only worth 3 LA when target has L2+ slots") functioned correctly — first BEL cycle where this exact threshold was testable and correct.

  6. **MQ-NEW-BEL6-A (sim harness bug — no spec change):** Multiattack in R3-R4 targeted downed Sabriel (AC19) instead of living Marwen (AC15). Sim logic checked "Bazgar alive else Sabriel" but both were downed. At table, DM would naturally attack Marwen or use VR main action. Corrected outcome: TPK R4 (beholder uses VR in R3-R4 instead of wasting multiattack on downed PCs). **Harness fix:** add "or if no melee PCs available, use VR as main action" branch to multiattack handler.

  7. **MQ-NEW-BEL6-B (lair gap — AUTHORING FIX APPLIED):** `unstable_ground` lair action fired in R2 and R3 when both Bazgar (−7) and Sabriel (−13) were already downed. FI-129 note ("skip unstable_ground if target prone or unconscious") didn't cover the case where ALL melee-range PCs are down. Added explicit wording to beholder-thrulm.md: *"if ALL melee-range PCs are unconscious/down, skip unstable_ground entirely and rotate to void_eruption or manifest_thralls."*

### FI-NEW-SW6-A / FI-NEW-SW6-B / FI-NEW-SW6-C / FI-NEW-SW6-D / MQ-NEW-SW6-B / MQ-NEW-SW6-C: shrine-wedge 6th-cycle — TPK R4; FI-159 init-dependence 2nd TPK confirm; OBR+UF Sabriel trap 2nd confirm; STD-B untouched 3rd cycle; AR all-fail pattern; multiattack header mislabel; OBR no-dice

- **Context:** 2026-05-28 04:00 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 6th cycle. Seed 494428. TPK R4 (Sabriel DOWN R2, Marwen DOWN R3, Bazgar sole survivor 22 HP vs STD-B 45 HP untouched → projected TPK R5). Phase A 28/28 clean (DD-10 18th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

- **FI-NEW-SW6-A — FI-159 6th-cycle confirm, 2nd SW TPK:** STD-A init 21 > Marwen 18 → AR fires before any PC action → all 3 PCs fail DC 14 Dex save → party enters R2 at ~35-65% HP → Sabriel downed R2 by UF multiattack. Outcome is binary: PCs-win-init = VICTORY (cycles 2, 3, 5), NPCs-win-init = TPK (cycles 4, 6). This is the same root cause as the 4th-cycle TPK (FI-159 first raised). **Design question:** Is this level of init-dependence acceptable? Options: (A) raise STDs' initiative modifier asymmetrically (STD-B –2 mod, creating reliable initiative split); (B) add an "entryway cover" rule (STDs start in hold position, party gets one action before Resonance is available); (C) reduce AR to Recharge 4–6 so R1 fire is less guaranteed when STDs win.

- **FI-NEW-SW6-B — FI-162 2nd confirm (OBR+UF Sabriel-kill loop):** Sabriel smites STD-A R1 (20 dmg, good). OBR reaction fires (misses). UF activates (≥10 dmg threshold met). R2 STD-A uses Multiattack with advantage → kills Sabriel (13 HP at start R2). The sequence: divine martial smites → OBR counter-threatens → UF activates → UF kills the divine martial next round. Feel implication: Sabriel's highest-impact action (smite) reliably triggers the mechanic that kills her. Recommend adding a DM callout in the shrine-wedge encounter guide: *"If Sabriel smites STD-A and it survives, expect UF advantage next round targeting her — don't smite if she's below 25 HP."*

- **FI-NEW-SW6-C — STD-B-stays-fresh (3rd cycle pattern):** Cycles 4, 5, and 6 all end with STD-B at ≥40/45 HP after R3. Stagger concentrates R1 PCs on STD-A (which acts first and draws attention). STD-B acts last in R1, deals multiattack damage, draws no fire. After STD-A dies in R3, STD-B enters as a fresh second wave. This is possibly intentional (creates a two-act structure) but it means the fight always resolves as "kill STD-A, then face fresh STD-B alone." If this feels repetitive, consider positioning STD-B closer to the party's entry so it naturally draws melee attention from Bazgar while STD-A holds range.

- **FI-NEW-SW6-D — AR DC 14 all-fail pattern:** 6/6 PCs failed both AR fires across R1-R2 in this cycle. With party Dex saves at +1/+2/+3 and DC 14, failure rates are ~65/70/75%. With 2 AR fires in the first two rounds, the party absorbs ~80–110 total necrotic+psychic damage — decisive burst that effectively decides the fight before Round 3. This is by design if the intent is "the party must disrupt AR," but the party has no reliable R1 disruption when STDs win initiative. **Design question:** Is DC 14 the right floor? Bump to DC 15 adds ~5% marginal save rate per PC, or reduce to 1d8 necrotic (down from 2d10) for a softer but more frequent AR.

- **MQ-NEW-SW6-B — Multiattack header damage-type mislabel (outside blast radius):** Output: `Shrine-Axe 1 to-hit 19 / dmg 11 slashing (incl +3 necrotic extra_damage)`. The label "11 slashing" includes necrotic damage — only 8 points are slashing, 3 are necrotic. A DM tracking slashing resistance would apply resistance to the full 11 instead of just 8. The per-roll breakdown below the header is correct. Fix is in `scripts/dnd_roller.py` formatter — outside blast radius. **Recommend** human fix: change header to show split type ("8 slashing + 3 necrotic") or remove the type label from the aggregated line.

- **MQ-NEW-SW6-C — OBR reaction "buff" type: no dice output:** OBR is typed `reaction_kind: "buff"` in the DB. The roller prints the effect description ("+4 to hit, on hit 1d8+1 slashing + 1d8 necrotic...") but does NOT roll dice. DM must manually roll to-hit and damage for every OBR trigger. OBR fired 3 times this cycle; 0 hits (all manual misses). The self-damage (d4) is described in the effect text but also requires manual roll. This is functional but creates a gap between the auto-rolling NPC experience and OBR's manual-roll experience. No `reaction_kind` value currently supports "counter_attack" (to-hit + damage) automatically — would require adding a new kind to `dnd_roller.py`. **Design question:** Should OBR be a `single_attack` action instead of a `reaction`? That would give it auto-rolling but lose the reaction framework (no "Reaction USED" footer, no trigger text). Current "buff" typing is the safe status quo.

### FI-NEW-TP9-A: threshold-patrol 9th-cycle — Call Weakness 0/27 structural lockout across all 9 TP cycles

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 18:17 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 9th cycle. Seed 494418. VICTORY R3 — Bazgar 36/49, Marwen DOWN, Sabriel 44/44. Barrage double-roll divergence (dispatch 9, sim 16 — corrected). Phase A 28/28 clean. 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-NEW-TP9-A (DESIGN DECISION): Call Weakness has never fired in threshold-patrol — 0/27 total across 9 cycles.** Root cause is consistent: Fireball (L3) drops both DW from 27 HP to ≤9 HP in R1, tripping the ≤20 HP guard, leaving SC with no valid CW target before any DW acts again. The only scenario where CW fires is if (a) SC wins initiative over Marwen AND (b) both DW are untouched when SC acts. Even in this cycle with DW1 at init 24 (highest), Marwen at init 19 fires Fireball before SC at init 16. CW is structurally unavailable unless Marwen delays her Fireball or the party lacks AOE. **Design question:** Is Call Weakness intended to contribute in the threshold-patrol context? If yes: possible mitigations — (a) increase DW HP to 40+ so Fireball doesn't drop them below guard; (b) add a 3rd DW to the patrol (CW on the survivor); (c) drop the ≤20 HP guard to ≤10 HP (higher risk but enables more CW fires). If CW is accepted as irrelevant to TP (patrol NPCs are simply too fragile to benefit), document that the SC in TP functions as a Barrage-delivery platform only and remove CW from its tactical guidance for this slice. **Do not auto-fix — requires human decision on CW intent and TP slice tuning.**

### FI-NEW-EV5-B / FI-NEW-EV5-C / DD-11-5th-EV / MQ-NEW-EV5-a/b/c: empty-void 5th-cycle — 2-pass negotiation breakdown; Maw autocrit 5th confirm; smite stranding 5th confirm; sim VR divergence

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 17:20 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 5th cycle. Seed 494417. TPK R3 — Marwen disintegrated surprise round, Sabriel grapple+Maw autocrit R2, Bazgar VS R3. Beholder 110/110 HP (0 damage, 5th consecutive EV cycle). First 2/3-pass negotiation in EV history. Both PCs saved VS R1 (rare). Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues — 16th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-NEW-EV5-B (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): 2/3-pass negotiation → surprise attack feels better than prior 0-exchange surprises, but still needs DM guidance.** This cycle's surprise was narratively earned (Arcana success naming the god's aspect; Persuasion success on shaft-sealing offer; then Bazgar's overreach triggered it). However, there is no text in beholder-thrulm.md's Interaction Notes advising the DM on: (a) minimum number of exchanges to run before allowing the truce to collapse, (b) whether the beholder gives a verbal warning before attacking, (c) whether the party can leave after a truce collapses vs being attacked on sight. **Recommendation:** Add to Interaction Notes: *"Even on a failed negotiation, the beholder allows at least 2 exchanges before combat — it is not impulsive. If the party makes a critical error (names an intent to investigate the seal or the lower shaft), the beholder fires Disintegration Ray in a surprise round. If the error is softer (overreach, bluster, no artifact), the beholder says: 'Come back when you have proof.' PCs may leave the vault without combat. The second entry is when the gloves come off."* This change directly addresses FI-104 (dead-end branch = party with no artifact) and DD-53 (0-counterplay window) without requiring a spec change. **Low-risk editorial fix — recommend applying in next EV cycle.**

  2. **FI-NEW-EV5-C / FI-184 (5th CONSECUTIVE CONFIRM): Sabriel smite slots 100% intact at death across all 5 EV cycles.** Pattern: (a) surprise round: no action; (b) R1: Sabriel acts last (init 6) after beholder fires VS; (c) R2: grappled and killed before her turn OR at very low HP. Not one L1/L2/L3 smite has been spent in any EV run. **Design question:** Does the encounter's phase structure (negotiation → surprise → immediate beholder R1 main action) structurally prevent Sabriel from contributing? If yes, is that intentional (she's the "healer anchor" that falls first)? Options: (a) add DM note that beholder does NOT use its surprise-round action if negotiation reached 2+ exchanges — party gets one free round to position before combat starts; (b) accept that Sabriel's smite budget is the "theoretical reserve that makes the party feel they could have won" — a deliberately frustrating experience; (c) make beholder's first round restricted to shrine_drift + compel_thrall to give PCs one combat round before deadly abilities fire. **Do not auto-fix — fundamental design intent question.**

  3. **DD-11 5th EV CONFIRM (URGENT — unresolved since cycle 3 BEL):** Maw grapple autocrit continues to one-shot any PC with <44 HP who is caught in melee range. Sabriel: 31 HP → TL2 grapple → Maw autocrit 43 piercing = dead in one multiattack. This has now occurred in: BEL cycles 2/3/4/5, EV cycles 3/4/5 (total 7 confirms). **This is not a sim artifact — it is the intended mechanic (grapple + crit is a standard beholder move) and it is working correctly. The question is whether the lethality is appropriate for a CR 13 vs L5 encounter that is explicitly designed as a TPK.** If yes: no change needed, add DM note that grapple = effectively dead. If no: consider removing the autocrit rider and keeping grapple as a position-lock only. **7th confirm — priority escalating. Human decision needed before next EV or BEL cycle.**

### FI-NEW-C / MQ-NEW-3b / MQ-NEW-4 / MQ-NEW-5 / DD-18-6th: shardcaller-team 6th-cycle — CW lockout via TR; stagger double-barrage; sim bugs; Fireball confirm

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 16:16 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 6th cycle. Seed 494416. VICTORY R4 — Bazgar 29/49, Marwen 0→10 downed×1, Sabriel 7/44. Init: SC-C(18) > SC-A(16) > Sabriel(13) > SC-B(9) > Marwen(8) > Bazgar(5). Fireball R1 low-roll (24 fire, all 3 SCs saved half = 12 each). Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues — 15th consecutive). 1 bug auto-fixed (MQ-NEW-2 Taunt-on-unconscious → derro-rager.md).

  1. **FI-NEW-C (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): CW lockout via TR conflict is now mechanized and confirmed.** 6th consecutive SCT cycle with CW 0-1/9 effective. The specific mechanism is now explicit: in R1, SCs use CW but target the stagger-slot Barrage holder (advantage wasted per "don't CW a Barrage-firing ally" rule). In R2+, all SCs face melee threats → all use TR → CW bonus action unavailable. The CW+TR mutual exclusion leaves zero rounds where CW can fire toward a multiattacking ally. **Design question:** Is Call Weakness intended as a primary tactical tool? If yes, consider converting it to a triggered/passive ability (e.g., "on hit with Shard-Throw, one ally within 30 ft gains advantage on next attack") that doesn't compete with TR. If the current CW-as-bonus-action design is intentional, accept that it's a ghost ability in all-shardcaller formations and document accordingly. **Do not auto-fix — requires human decision on ability purpose.**

  2. **MQ-NEW-3b (NEW — MECHANICS GAP): CW targeting should check stagger before firing.** SC-C acts first (init 18) and CW'd SC-A without knowing SC-A is the stagger-slot Barrage holder for that round. The existing tactics rule "do not CW an ally who plans to use Shard-Barrage" requires knowing another SC's plan before your own turn. In a table play context, this is a quick sidebar check; in sim/solo-DM context it requires explicit stagger-check before CW. **Recommendation:** Add to tactics: "Before spending CW, verbally confirm with yourself which SC is the stagger-slot holder this round. Never CW the stagger-slot SC. If all alive SCs have Barrage available, hold CW." Minor doc fix — low priority; can apply next SCT cycle.

  3. **MQ-NEW-4 / MQ-NEW-5 (SIM BUGS — harness only, no spec change):**
     - **MQ-NEW-4:** Dispatch multiattack output format `Shard-Throw N to-hit X / dmg Y piercing` not matched by sim parse regex. All SC multiattack damage was unapplied in sim. Correction applied manually in narrative above (Marwen 32→1 HP end R1 after 6+5+9 multiattack hits; later downed by 6 piercing to 0). Real party HP is lower than logged sim HP.
     - **MQ-NEW-5:** Stagger mid-round violation — SC-A died at init 13 (Sabriel's turn), promoting SC-B to "first alive" at init 9, who then fired a second Barrage same round. Fix: track a `barrage_fired_this_round` flag at round level, not by checking alive status. Both harness-only fixes; outside cron blast radius.

  4. **DD-18 6th SCT confirm:** All 3 SCs still alive at end R1 (first time in SCT history — prior cycles Fireball always killed 1-2). Fight extended to R4 (longest SCT since Slow-R1 5th cycle). Root cause: Fireball low roll (24) + all saves. Even so, VICTORY. The encounter has not been flipped by this event — party is just more taxed (Marwen downed, Sabriel at 7 HP). Design decision still open: scatter SCs to prevent all-3-Fireball hits.

### FI-NEW-A / FI-NEW-B / FI-177-BROKEN / MQ-NEW / MQ-NEW-2 / MQ-71-11th: solo-rager-rush 11th-cycle — Slow intra-R1 break; first Berserk damage; longest SRR fight; sim Berserk-parser gap; Taunt-on-unconscious gap

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 15:00 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 11th cycle. Seed 494415. VICTORY R5 — Bazgar 29/49, Marwen 0→stabilized, Sabriel 44/44 untouched. Init: Marwen(18) > RG1(18) > RG2(16) > Bazgar(15) > Sabriel(5) > RG3(5). Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues — 14th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-NEW-A (NEW — FEEL): Slow broke intra-R1 (first occurrence in 11 SRR cycles).** RG1 failed the Slow save and was Slowed; RG2 passed. On RG2's turn (init 16, before Bazgar and Sabriel), RG2 charged Marwen and landed a crit-hit (4 damage). DC10 concentration save, Marwen's +2 CON rolled a 4 — fail. Slow lasted 0 effective rounds. This is the structural risk of Slow as an R1 opener in **mixed-initiative** fights: if a non-Slowed rager acts before the party's melee screen (Bazgar/Sabriel), the concentrating caster has no cover. **DM note to add to encounter prep:** Slow is safest when Marwen has cover or when PCs win full initiative. In mixed-initiative, consider Fireball R1 over Slow to avoid concentration risk.

  2. **FI-177 BROKEN (MILESTONE): First Berserk damage in 11 SRR cycles.** RG3 survived to R4 (party spent R2–R3 on RG1/RG2) and triggered Berserk vs Bazgar+Sabriel (both in melee reach). Berserk hit Bazgar for 13 slashing (to-hit 22 vs AC18). Prior 10 cycles: Berserk fired but missed or was Slowed (1 attack), dealing 0 damage. **This cycle's enabling conditions:** (a) RG3 was the last priority target, (b) both melee PCs were adjacent, (c) fight lasted to R4. **Design note:** the FI-177 "Berserk never fires" pattern is corrected — Berserk DOES fire and hit when the rager is the last survivor against 2+ adjacent PCs. The fix is encounter design: if ragers are eliminated in decreasing priority, the last one almost always reaches Berserk conditions. Not a spec change — a DM-tactics note to consider.

  3. **FI-NEW-B (NEW — FEEL): 5-round fight is the longest SRR in 11 cycles. Mixed-initiative consistently creates better encounters than all-PC-first.** This cycle had: Slow gambit (R1) → Slow breaks + RG1 whiff (R1) → Fireball vs both ragers (R2, both saved for half) → Hold Person swing (R3) → Berserk finale (R4) → cleanup (R5). The all-PC-first cycles (cycles 7, 8, 10) resolved in 2–4 rounds with less narrative variety. **Recommendation reinforces FI-176 option (b): a staggered entry mechanic (1 rager pre-adjacent at combat start) would consistently produce mixed-initiative dynamics, making every SRR cycle as engaging as this one. Human sign-off needed — do not auto-fix.**

  4. **MQ-NEW (SIM BUG — no spec change): Phase B Berserk parser missed "Greataxe (target N)" format.** Berserk spec uses attack name `"Greataxe (target 1)"` vs multiattack's `"Greataxe 1"`. Sim regex `Greataxe\s+\d+` matched `\d+` not `(target N)`. Berserk was dispatched and shown but damage was not applied. Corrected state: Bazgar 42→29 HP in R4 (not 42). **Outcome unchanged (VICTORY R5 still correct).** No DB spec change needed. Sim harness fix: use `Greataxe\s+(\d+|\(target \d+\))\s+to-hit` or dispatch output diff. Outside cron blast radius — harness fix for human.

  5. **MQ-NEW-2 (NEW — minor gap): Taunt targeting logic doesn't exclude unconscious creatures.** RG3 in R4 targeted unconscious Marwen for Taunt. Unconscious creatures auto-fail Cha saves (RAW) but can't make attack rolls — so Taunt's effect is null. The .md tactics say "redirect to whoever is threatening the back line" but don't explicitly filter out unconscious targets. **Minor clarification recommended:** Add to derro-rager.md tactics: *"Skip unconscious/dead creatures as Taunt targets; if all valid targets are down or immune, Taunt is wasted — skip it."* Low priority; can defer to next rager-focus cycle.

  6. **MQ-71 (11th-cycle confirm — still pending human sign-off): ME not applied in R1.** Consistent with all prior cycles. RG2 and RG3 took damage in R1 but had no established prior turn → ME correctly withheld. Recommendation: add explicit note to checklist item 2 in derro-rager.md: *"(Does not apply in Round 1 — ME requires an established prior turn.)"* **Awaiting human confirm before auto-fixing.**

### MQ-84 / FI-198 / FI-199 / FI-200 / MQ-85 / MQ-86: final-confrontation 10th-cycle — sim artifact R1 TPK; DR+VS mutual exclusion auto-fixed; VE+DR combo 10th confirm; thrall Fireball-sink 10th confirm

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 14:00 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 10th cycle. Seed 494414. Sim-reported TPK R1 (artifact — corrected estimate: TPK R2). Beholder 83/110 HP (after Fireball chip).   1. **MQ-84 (NEW — RESOLVED by auto-fix): DR and VS are both main actions; a turn cannot use both.** Sim dispatched `disintegration_ray` then `void_scream` in sequence on the beholder's turn — impossible per RAW (only one main action per turn). This collapsed what should be a 2-round TPK into a 1-round wipe, making the sim output unrepresentative. **Auto-fix applied:** Added checklist item 5 to beholder-thrulm.md: *"Main action (choose exactly one per turn): multiattack / disintegration_ray (if available) / void_scream (if available). DR and VS are mutually exclusive — only one fires per turn."* No DB spec change. This is a doc clarification to prevent DM (and sim) confusion.

  2. **FI-198 (CONFIRM — FI-173 10th-cycle): VE lair fires before any PC acts R1 — confirmed for 10th consecutive FC cycle.** Lair action at init 20 always precedes the party (highest PC init was 19 this run) in the final confrontation. Party arrives at R2 already at 50-65% HP. FI-173 DESIGN DECISION (DM guidance: prefer unstable_ground R1, reserve VE for R2+) remains open for human review. This is the 10th data point supporting option (a) from FI-173 as a low-risk editorial fix.

  3. **FI-199 (NEW — SIM BUG): STD Fireball damage not applied in altar-zone branch.** Code logged STD save result but skipped `take_dmg()` call for shrine-touched derro. Corrected: STD-A 32/45 (saved Fireball), STD-B 18/45 (failed Fireball). In a real R2 with these values, STD-B at 18 HP is vulnerable — one Scorching Ray sequence kills it. Does not change the estimated TPK R2 outcome (VS fires R2 and wipes all 3 PCs before STD-B acts, since Sabriel init 13 > STD-B init 11 > Beholder init 13 tie). **Sim harness fix needed, not a spec change.**

  4. **FI-200 (NEW CONFIRM — FI-167 10th-cycle): All 4 thralls one-shotted by Fireball in R1.** 10th consecutive FC cycle where thralls deal 0 damage before dying to Marwen's first spell. Thrall HP 22 vs 8d6 avg 28 fire = auto-wipe on failed save; all 4 failed. Thralls serve as a Fireball-sink (costing Marwen 1 L3 slot) and as Fireball bait that draws her L3 away from targeting the beholder directly. If the design intent is thrall-as-resource-drain: working correctly. FI-167 DESIGN DECISION (raise thrall HP or add Evasion) still open.

  5. **MQ-85 (NEW — TIEBREAK AMBIGUITY): Bazgar and STD-A tied at initiative 19.** Sim used PC-priority (Bazgar acts before STD-A). RAW tiebreak: highest Dex (STD-A +3 wins over Bazgar +2). If STD-A acts before Bazgar, AR fires into Bazgar at 34 HP (pre-VE) before Bazgar can attack. This changes the feel of Bazgar's first turn (he'd be at 21 HP with no attacks yet vs 34 HP with 2 failed attacks). Outcome is the same (TPK) but the init-tie ruling matters for table feel. **Recommend adding tiebreak convention to _overview.md or encounter notes.** Do not auto-fix.

  6. **MQ-86 (NEW — SIM, no spec change): Stagger check fires mid-round, not at round start.** Same pattern as MQ-61 from FC 8th cycle. No impact this run (STD-A higher init than STD-B → correct stagger assignment), but the harness remains vulnerable when STD-B has higher init than STD-A. Harness-only fix, not a spec issue.

### FI-194 / FI-195 / FI-196 / FI-197 / MQ-82 / MQ-83 / DD-11 5th-confirm: beholder-escorts-limited 5th-cycle — VICTORY (sim artifact, VS absent); LoH loop confirmed again; 4 auto-fixes applied

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 13:15 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 5th cycle. Seed 494413. VICTORY R5 — Bazgar 12/49, Marwen 0/32 (1 death save fail, stable), Sabriel 21/44. Beholder down R5 (Bazgar longsword finish); all 3 thralls eliminated by Fireball R2. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues — 12th consecutive). 4 bugs auto-fixed (FI-125/FI-128/FI-129 applied to beholder-thrulm.md, MQ-82 prone immunity note added).

  1. **FI-194 (NEW — SIM ARTIFACT, NOT DESIGN ISSUE): First BEL victory in 5 cycles is a sim harness gap.** The beholder turn handler dispatched compel_thrall + multiattack but never checked Void Scream availability. VS starts combat available (confirmed by FI-165); per tactics it should fire when ≥1 PC is within 30 ft — either as R1 main action (if party is at ground level) or after shrine_drift descent. Without VS, the beholder's R1 is a pure melee multiattack that missed entirely (AC 18 wall vs +6 to-hit = 45% hit rate per tentacle; three-attack sequence whiffed). All prior BEL TPK cycles had VS firing R1 (cycles 3–4) or R2 (cycles 1–2). This victory outcome is not representative of expected table play. **Sim harness fix needed: add VS availability check to beholder turn handler before selecting main action.**

  2. **FI-195 (NEW — SIM BUG, no spec change): VS check absent from Phase B beholder turn dispatch logic.** The Phase B sim selects beholder main action as: compel_thrall (bonus) → multiattack (main). VS should be checked first: if VS available AND at least one PC within 30 ft (accounting for altitude/shrine_drift), fire VS as main action. This is the beholder's highest-priority main action per tactics (.md line "Void Scream the moment it's recharged"). Implementation: add `if vs_available and any PC within 30 ft: dispatch("beholder-thrulm", "void_scream")` before the multiattack branch. No DB spec change needed.

  3. **FI-196 (NEW — FEEL, 5th-BEL-cycle confirm of FI-125): LoH revival loop re-observed.** Sabriel spent 4 consecutive turns cycling LoH to revive Bazgar (who was grappled/downed by multiattack). This was the pattern from cycle 3 (FI-125: 6 consecutive LoH turns). The FI-125 fix (Tentacle LA targeting Sabriel end-of-her-turn) has now been applied to beholder-thrulm.md. **Cycle 6 should show whether the LA pressure disrupts the loop.** If Sabriel < 30 HP when she cycles LoH, the Tentacle LA (1 action) forces self-LoH next turn instead of ally-LoH — depleting the 25-point pool faster.

  4. **FI-197 (NEW — FEEL, confirms FI-129 gap): Lair action wasted targeting unconscious Bazgar.** Unstable Ground R4 targeted Bazgar who was at 0 HP (unconscious). RAW: unconscious creatures are prone automatically; lair action dealing forced-prone to an unconscious creature is a null action. FI-129 lair rotation fix applied: skip unstable_ground if target is already unconscious OR prone. Applied to beholder-thrulm.md this cycle.

  5. **MQ-82 (NEW — RESOLVED, applied to beholder-thrulm.md): Battlemaster Trip Attack vs hovering beholder — immune to prone.** R1 Bazgar attempted Trip Attack (Battlemaster maneuver: on hit, force DC 10+ Str save or prone). Beholder has fly speed 30 ft (hover). RAW: hovering creatures cannot be knocked prone. The Trip Attack hit deals normal damage, but the prone component is negated automatically. Added to beholder-thrulm.md tactics: *"Hovering creature — prone immunity: the beholder cannot be knocked prone by Trip Attack, Topple mastery, Thunderwave, or similar. Redirect to standard hit; state the ruling at table when it arises."*

  6. **MQ-83 (NEW — SIM NOTE, no issue): Fireball range and DC vs beholder.** Marwen (L5, spell save DC 13) fired Fireball in R2 catching the beholder within 20 ft of center. Beholder rolled DC 13 Dex save with +6 Dex modifier (total 22) — easily passed, took half (13 fire). Beholder's Dex proficiency makes Marwen-DC Fireball a reliable half-damage at best against it. At-table note: Marwen's DC 13 vs beholder Dex +6 means beholder saves on any d20 roll ≥ 7 (65% pass rate). Marwen should target thralls (no Dex bonus) with Fireball and use Scorching Ray (to-hit, not save) against the beholder.

  7. **DD-11 (5th-CONFIRM — still pending human): Maw autocrit on same-turn grapple.** R3 this cycle: Tentacle Lash grappled Bazgar in the multiattack sequence, then Maw used as standalone action (not in same sequence). The question remains whether a grapple applied in the same multiattack sequence enables Maw autocrit for the third attack. Sim treated as normal hit pending DD-11 human sign-off. At-table, this must be pre-ruled before the beholder's first multiattack.

### FI-192 / FI-193 / MQ-80 / MQ-81: tank-wall 11th-cycle — Slow strips Rager identity; SC isolated; Slow AoE geometry; 1 auto-fix

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 12:18 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 11th cycle. Seed 494412. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 32/49, Marwen 24/32, Sabriel 36/44. Init: Marwen 21 > Sabriel 18 > Bazgar 13 > Rager 10 > SC 4. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues — 11th consecutive). 1 bug auto-fixed (FI-192 Slow+Taunt checklist note in derro-rager.md).

  1. **FI-192 (NEW — auto-fixed in derro-rager.md):** Slow completely neutralizes the Rager's identity mechanics. A Slowed Rager: (a) AC 16 → 14 (trivially hittable by L5 party), (b) loses Taunt — must choose action OR bonus action, not both, (c) Berserk restricted to 1 attack anyway per MQ-63, (d) half movement prevents repositioning/gap-closing. Combined, the Rager under Slow deals 1 attack per turn with ~35% hit rate vs AC 18/19 and has no tactical signature whatsoever. The checklist didn't call this out explicitly; FI-182 (shardcaller) was fixed last cycle, Rager needed the same. **Auto-fix applied: added "Slowed exception" to checklist item 4.** No balance change — this is a doc clarification that the DM applies automatically.

  2. **FI-193 (NEW — FEEL):** When the Rager falls in R1, the SC is left alone against 3 L5 PCs with no melee cover, no ally CW target, and 85 ft of unobstructed corridor between itself and the party. The SC gets 1 Barrage (17 pierce dispatch-authoritative) and then trades hits at long range for 2 actions before going down. The "tank wall" feel — Rager absorbing hits while SC calls weaknesses — has never been achieved in 11 cycles. The slice name no longer describes the observed experience; both NPCs are separately destroyed rather than functioning as a formation. **This is the 11th-cycle confirmation of FI-163 (structural pairing gap) and FI-164 (initiative collapse).** No new recommendation — FI-163/164 DESIGN DECISION block still open for human.

  3. **MQ-80 (NEW — ruling confirmed):** Slow RAW: the creature "can take only one action or one bonus action" per turn. Taunt (bonus action) + Multiattack (action) cannot both occur when Slowed. The FI-192 auto-fix correctly documents this. Confirm with user that this reading is correct — some DM interpretations of Slow allow a full turn's actions at the end (the "slower action economy" reading). Standard 5e RAW is action-OR-bonus per turn.

  4. **MQ-81 (NEW — sim geometry bug):** Slow is a 40-ft cube AoE. Rager at 30 ft from party, SC at 85 ft from party. Centering the cube at the Rager catches it but not the SC (SC is 55 ft past the Rager, outside the 20-ft cube half-width). This cycle's simulation offered the SC a Wis save against Slow — incorrect. SC was outside range. SC passed the save so outcome was unchanged, but future simulations should not give the SC a Slow save unless it has repositioned within 20 ft of the Slow center point.
