### DD-53 / FI-184 / MQ-74 / MQ-75 / MQ-76: empty-void 4th-cycle — surprise-round DR opener; smite slots stranded; Antireality threshold; LA fallthrough

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 09:26 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 4th cycle. Seed 494409. TPK R7 — beholder 86/110 HP. Party entered diplomatic posture (3 negotiation exchanges); beholder fired DR mid-negotiation (surprise round) killing Marwen instantly; VS R1 dropped survivors to 13/18 HP + frightened. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues). 2 authoring fixes applied (MQ-74, MQ-75).

  1. **DD-53 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION):** The "negotiation → surprise attack" opener in the empty-void slice creates a zero-counterplay window: Marwen disintegrated before initiative is rolled, then VS hits both remaining PCs before their first turn. This is a 4th-cycle confirmation that the empty-void slice, when played as a diplomatic entry, produces immediate character-defining destruction that bypasses all the legendary/lair economy the slice is supposed to test. **Recommendation:** The empty-void slice description should specify that the beholder gives one final warning before attacking (removing mechanical surprise), OR the slice should begin with the beholder mid-air without the diplomatic opener. If the intent is to test the beholder's negotiation dynamics, the party needs at least one round to respond before facing DR+VS. This is the second time this pattern appeared (1st cycle vs 4th cycle) — the "surprise during diplomacy" framing is the empty-void opener that most consistently prevents the slice's stated goal ("tests legendary/lair flow") from being observed. Human review required before changing the slice description.

  2. **FI-184 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION):** Sabriel's smite slots were stranded in all 4 empty-void cycles. Across 4 runs: 0 Divine Smites have been successfully delivered against the beholder. Root causes vary (R1 VS + frightened lock = cycles 1/2/4; DR death mid-fight = cycle 3), but the structural constant is that Sabriel is either frightened (disadvantage = misses) or dead before she can land a smite. **Design question:** Is the "paladin can't get a smite off against the beholder" an intended part of the encounter's difficulty, or should the empty-void slice have a mechanic/narrative moment where Sabriel's divine power specifically interacts with the void? If the former, document it. If the latter, consider giving the beholder a vulnerability (or Sabriel a special action) that makes the divine-vs-void tension interactive rather than auto-suppressed by fear.

  3. **MQ-74 (RESOLVED — auto-fixed in .md):** Antireality trigger "estimated 10+ damage" was ambiguous between pre-resist and post-resist estimates. Clarified in `beholder-thrulm.md`: the beholder estimates from weapon average (greatsword ≈ 10, longsword ≈ 7) before seeing damage dice. No spec change needed.

  4. **MQ-75 (RESOLVED — auto-fixed in .md):** When all spell-slot users are dead, the beholder's Legendary Actions had no clear fallback (DD-28's Drain Divinity priority remained in force even with no valid targets). Added explicit rule: "Once all slot-holders are down, use Void Ray (2 LA) after each PC's turn if ≥ 2 LAs remain." In R4–R7 of this run, 3× LA budgets (9 total LAs) were wasted because Sabriel was dead; with the fix, those convert to ~3 additional Void Rays against Bazgar, ending the fight in R4-R5 rather than R7.

  5. **MQ-76 (NEW — sim artifact, no spec change):** Simulation used `void_ray` as the beholder's fallback main action when DR and VS were spent. Void Ray is a legendary action (2 LAs) only — the correct fallback main action is `multiattack`. Harness fix needed: add a guard in Phase B dispatch that blocks `void_ray` as a main action and substitutes `multiattack`. No change to beholder.md or DB spec needed.

### FI-181 / FI-182 / MQ-72 / MQ-73: shardcaller-team 5th-cycle — TR fires first time; Slow interaction; bonus-action conflict

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 08:24 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 5th cycle. Seed 494408. VICTORY R5 — Marwen downed twice, SC-B sole survivor lasted 4 rounds post-SC-A+SC-C death. Marwen used Slow R1 (vs Fireball) to extend the fight. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues). 3 authoring fixes applied.

  1. **FI-180 (POSITIVE):** TR fired for the first time in 5 shardcaller-team cycles. SC-C at 7/33 HP in R3 had Bazgar (init 17) in melee at the START of SC-C's turn (init 21). TR fired → SC-C retreated 30 ft and then multiattacked Marwen, downing her again. The fix from DD-47 ("bonus action not main action") is working. TR appears when: (a) SC survives past R1 focus-fire, AND (b) SC's initiative fires AFTER the PC closes in the previous round. Still rare (1/5 cycles) but confirmed achievable.

  2. **FI-181 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION, auto-fixed in .md):** TR and CW are both bonus actions. When SC-C used TR, it could NOT also CW. The fight demonstrated: in the 2-SC endgame (one SC using TR, the other needing CW buff), the TR event costs a CW charge. Current tactics didn't address this conflict. Fix applied: added "TR and CW cannot both be used in same turn; TR wins" to checklist item 3 and tactics. No DB spec change needed.

  3. **FI-182 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION, auto-fixed in .md):** Slow spell creates an action/bonus-action fork for the shardcaller. SC-B (SLOWED) could not pair Multiattack + TR. SC-B chose Multiattack (correct per tactics) and abandoned TR even though melee threat (Bazgar 10-15 ft) was within range. The interaction is tactically interesting — Slow effectively pins a shardcaller in place. DC 15 vs Wis +4 (55% save rate) means ~1 SC slowed per cast. This feels balanced: the party spent a L3 slot to hobble one SC for 1+ rounds. No balance change needed.

  4. **MQ-72 (NEW — documented, auto-fixed in .md):** CW advantage + Slow disadvantage = straight roll per 5e RAW. SC-B had both simultaneously (SC-C granted CW, Slow gave disadv). Net result was two misses vs AC 19 Sabriel (rolls 6+4=10 and 14+4=18). Rule interaction now documented in tactics. No DB spec change needed.

  5. **MQ-73 (NEW — documented, auto-fixed in .md):** TR fires at the START of the NPC's OWN turn, not as a reaction. If SC acts before the threat closes this round (SC init > PC init), TR is unreachable until next round. This is the structural root cause of DD-47's "TR never fires" pattern: most cycles, SC-C (init 21) fires before Bazgar (init 17), so on SC-C's R1/R2 turns Bazgar hasn't closed yet. TR then fires in R3 when Bazgar was ALREADY in melee before SC-C's turn started. Documented in .md as "timing clarification" — no rule change, just DM reminder.

### FI-176 / FI-177 / MQ-71: solo-rager-rush 10th-cycle — VICTORY R4; init-swing design question; Berserk 0-dmg 10th confirm; ME R1 ambiguity

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 07:20 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 10th cycle. Seed 494407. VICTORY R4 — party untouched except Marwen −10 dmg. Init: Bazgar 20, Sabriel 14, Marwen 11, RG3 8, RG2 4, RG1 1. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-176 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): Solo-rager-rush outcome is highly initiative-dependent.** 10th SRR cycle. PCs rolled 20/14/11; ragers rolled 8/4/1 — all PCs acted before all ragers in R1. Action Surge (4 attacks) + smite dropped RG1 to 1 HP; Fireball finished it and chipped the others. RG1 died before its first action. RG2 died R2 before its second action. RG3 Slowed and ground down R4. Party took 10 total damage. This is the extreme end of the distribution, but confirms: at L5, front-loaded resources (Action Surge + Fireball + smite) can entirely negate the ragers' first turn. When ragers go first (~50% of fights) the outcome would likely be closer. **Design options:**
     - **(a) Accept as-is:** initiative variance is normal D&D; the 50% rager-first case creates real danger.
     - **(b) Staggered entry mechanic:** one rager is already adjacent (surprise-adjacent) when combat starts, guaranteeing at least one rager acts in R1 regardless of initiative.
     - **(c) Replace 1 rager with 1 thrall-derro:** adds ranged pressure immune to the melee-only initiative dependency.
     **Do not auto-fix.**

  2. **FI-177 (NEW — FEEL): Berserk has contributed 0 damage in all 10 SRR cycles.** The combination of recharge 5–6 (~33% per turn), hit rate +4 vs AC 18 (~30%) or AC 15 (~35%), and Slow restricting to 1 attack (MQ-63) means expected Berserk DPR over a 4-round fight is effectively <2. This run: 1 use, 1 Slowed target, miss. Across cycles: FI-53/64/85/96/121/136/141/177. **Design options:**
     - **(a) Accept:** Berserk's value is positional/threat, not damage; zone-control forces PCs to split or cluster.
     - **(b) Lower recharge to 4–6:** more frequent fires; hit rate issue persists.
     - **(c) Raise to-hit to +5:** marginal hit-rate improvement; doesn't change structural rarity.
     **Do not auto-fix.**

  3. **MQ-71 (NEW — MECHANICAL AMBIGUITY): Madness Endurance "last turn" trigger in Round 1.** The .md says *"If rager took damage last turn: +1 to attack rolls this turn."* In R1, ragers took Fireball damage from Marwen (init 11) before their own turns (init 8/4). Sim applied +1 ME when those ragers acted in R1. This is likely **incorrect** — "last turn" implies an established prior turn (previous round). A rager in R1 has no prior turn. **Recommended clarification to derro-rager.md:** Add to Start-of-turn checklist item 2: *"(This does not apply in Round 1 — ME requires an established prior turn. R1 ME applies only if the rager was already in combat before the encounter starts, which is not the case for Thrulm encounters.)"* **Do not auto-fix — human confirms intent.**

### FI-165 / FI-166 / FI-167 / FI-168 / MQ-69 #4 / MQ-70: beholder-escorts-limited 4th-cycle — TPK R5; VS guaranteed R1; DD+VS double-punch; thrall negligible output; Bazgar 0 dmg; Maw grapple ambiguity 4th confirm

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 05:19 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 4th cycle. Seed 494405. TPK R5 — Beholder 76/110 HP (34 total dmg). Init: Beholder 20, Sabriel 19, Thrall-B 16, Bazgar 14, Thrall-A 13, Thrall-C 7, Marwen 6. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-165 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): Void Scream fires guaranteed R1 when beholder wins initiative (~50% of all fights).** VS starts available at combat start (no "used" flag reset between encounters). Beholder rolled init 20 (max with +4); VS fired before any PC acted: Bazgar 24/49+FRIGHTENED, Sabriel 10/44+FRIGHTENED before either PC's first turn. Over 4 BEL cycles: VS fired R1 in 3 (beholder won init) and R2 in 1 (beholder lost init). R1 VS is not a rare event — it's the expected path when beholder wins init. **Design options:**
     - **(a) VS starts SPENT at combat start** — beholder must earn VS in play; prevents guaranteed-R1 fire; more DM narrative control.
     - **(b) Raise recharge to 5–6** — more frequent fires overall (~2× as common), but same R1 availability issue.
     - **(c) Accept current behavior** — R1 VS-on-initiative-win is intended opener; the CR 13 beholder is supposed to be terrifying. Most flavor-consistent.
     **Do not auto-fix.**

  2. **FI-166 (NEW — FEEL): VS + Drain Divinity R1 double-punch strips Sabriel's agency before her first action.** Cycle sequence: R1 VS → Sabriel 10/44+FRIGHTENED, then DD (end of beholder turn, 3 LA) → Sabriel loses L3 slot. Combined: Sabriel entered R2 at 10 HP with no L3 slot, frightened. She never cast a spell this combat. Confirmed pattern across cycles 2, 3, and 4 (every BEL cycle where beholder won init). Mechanically correct per tactics. **Design question: should Drain Divinity have a R1 restriction** (e.g., "beholder must first observe the target casting before identifying and draining the slot — never R1")? This preserves fear from VS while giving divine martial a chance to act before being systematically dismantled. **Do not auto-fix.**

  3. **FI-167 (NEW — FEEL): Thrall mechanical damage is structurally zero against this party.** 3 thralls over 5 rounds = 2 total slashing damage. Hand Axe +1 vs. AC 15–19 = 15–35% hit rate; 1d4+0 = 2.5 avg/hit. Fireball-sink function works (Marwen correctly spent L3 on them, killing 2 + dealing 15 chip to beholder). But thralls as independent threats are invisible. If the design intent is "resource drain only, not damage dealers," current spec is correct. **If thralls should feel threatening independently, raise to-hit to +3 or add a pack-attack rider (+2 if adjacent thrall ally is attacking same target). Do not auto-fix — human decision.**

  4. **FI-168 (NEW — FEEL / DM NOTE): Bazgar dealt 0 damage over 3 rounds (fear + disadvantage chain).** VS fear (DC 16 Wis, +2 mod = 30% pass rate per turn) kept Bazgar at disadvantage R1–R3; he failed 3 consecutive saves and missed 6/6 attacks before going down. This is correct and intended (fighter neutered by fear is the beholder's control design). **Low-risk DM note suggestion:** add to beholder-thrulm.md tactics — *"When Bazgar is frightened, narrate each near-miss as the void deflecting his weapon — the fear condition is the beholder's most durable melee suppressor; honor it with description to make the player's bad rolls feel meaningful rather than invisible."* Optional editorial; not blocking.

  5. **MQ-69 (4th CONFIRM — DD-11 URGENT): Maw autocrit vs same-turn grapple ambiguity unresolved for 4 consecutive BEL cycles.** Does a grapple established by Tentacle Lash in the current multiattack grant the Maw autocrit in that same multiattack turn? Prior cycles (FI-56 cycles 1–3) all raised the same question; DD-11 flagged URGENT after cycle 3. **Recommend adding explicit clarification to beholder-thrulm.md Maw description:** *"Autocrit applies only to targets grappled at the START of the beholder's turn. A grapple established by Tentacle Lash in this multiattack does NOT enable Maw autocrit until next turn."* This is a rules-as-written clarification (not a balance change); human can approve and apply next cycle. **Do not auto-fix without human sign-off.**

  6. **MQ-70 (NEW — pattern confirm of FI-127): VS recharge rate (recharge-6) yields 0–1 fires per fight.** This cycle: 0/4 post-R1 recharge rolls (rolls: 2, 5, 3, 1). Prior cycle 3: 0/8. Expected: ~1 recharge per 6 rounds. BEL fights averaging 5–8 rounds → VS fires once per fight. FI-127 (design decision: once-per-fight swing vs. recurring threat) still pending human decision on recharge rate. No new angle this cycle.

### FI-159 (DESIGN DECISION): shrine-wedge 4th-cycle — initiative-dependence too high; encounter outcome is a coin-flip on STD init vs Marwen init

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 17:29 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 4th cycle. Seed 494393. TPK R3 — first shrine-wedge TPK; prior 3 cycles all VICTORY.

  1. **FI-159 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): The shrine-wedge encounter outcome is entirely determined by whether STD-A's initiative beats Marwen's.** Record: STD-A wins init → TPK (1×); Marwen wins init → VICTORY (3×). Mechanically: if Marwen acts first, Slow slows STD-A (−2 AC, no reactions), removing OBR and AR on the following turn. If STD-A acts first, AR fires into a fresh party (all fail DC14 saves → 15 dmg each), then stagger-MA kills Marwen before she acts. The 2-point initiative delta (STD +5 vs Marwen +3) generates a coin-flip with huge outcome variance. **Design options for human review:**
     - **(a) Party surprise round** if they stealth the approach (recon the chamber before engagement). Removes the coin-flip; rewards tactical play. Most narrative fit.
     - **(b) Script delayed AR** — STDs don't fire AR until R2. R1 they use multiattack only ("still resonating"). Guaranteed one PC turn before AR. Moderate difficulty reduction.
     - **(c) Reduce STD initiative bonus** (+5 → +3 or +2). Narrows the gap; doesn't eliminate variance. Weakest fix.
     - **(d) Accept current variance** — 75%/25% VICTORY/TPK split may be intentional. Some tables prefer high-variance combat.

  2. **FI-160 (NEW FEEL):** Marwen downed R1 without taking a single action — feels worst-case for player agency. The most punishing outcome in tabletop is a player whose character never acts. This outcome (initiative beat + AR damage + stagger-MA) should be considered when choosing fix option above.

### FI-172 / FI-173 / FI-174 (DESIGN DECISION): final-confrontation 9th-cycle — VE+DR R1 double-punch record-low beholder damage; STD-A AR-silent; lair choice guidance needed

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 06:18 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 9th cycle. Seed 494406. TPK R3 — Marwen DISINTEGRATED R1 by DR, Sabriel downed R2 by DR (−40HP, threshold -44 → not disintegrated), Bazgar downed R3 by VE lair. Beholder 102/110 HP (8 dmg total — record low for any FC cycle). Init: Lair 20, T1 20, Beholder 18, T3 18, T4 17, T2 12, Sabriel 11, STD-B 9, Marwen 6, STD-A 4, Bazgar 3. Phase A 28/28 clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 network-block continues). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-172 (NEW — FEEL / DESIGN NOTE): Beholder took record-low 8 HP over 3 rounds.** Bazgar landed 1 of 4 attacks (8 slashing R2). No other PC connected with the beholder. This is structurally the result of: VE R1 pre-softening all PCs (Marwen→16HP, Sabriel→28HP) before any PC acted, then DR eliminating the primary caster R1. With Marwen gone and Sabriel at 28HP, Bazgar was the only upright attacker from R2 onward — and faced VE+DR again R2 (Sabriel downed) then VE R3. The fight never reached a "the party is fighting back" phase. **FEEL NOTE: 8 HP taken in a 3-round fight is narratively unsatisfying even for an overwhelming encounter. The party should feel like they left a mark. Consider whether lair + beholder always acting in the same "pre-PC" burst is the intended design.**

  2. **FI-173 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): VE lair action fires at init 20 (beholder init 18) — always before beholder in the same round, creating a guaranteed 2-action damage burst before any PC acts when the party enters near the altar.** In this cycle: VE → Marwen 16HP prone, Sabriel 28HP prone → then DR eliminates Marwen. This is mechanically optimal and correct per rules, but means the very first round of the final confrontation begins with the party already at 50% HP before a single PC acts. **Design options:**
     - **(a) DM guidance (soft):** Add explicit note to beholder.md tactics: *"R1 lair: prefer unstable_ground on Bazgar (the melee threat) unless 3 PCs are clearly clustered near the altar center. Reserve VE for R2+ when PCs have had one action. The first round should feel like the beholder reacting to the party, not the other way around."* This preserves rules legality while steering DM narration. Low-risk.
     - **(b) Change lair priority order:** Update tactics to treat VE as R2+ only (R1 = unstable_ground or manifest_thralls by default). Hard-coded suggestion, easy to override, low mechanical change.
     - **(c) Accept current behavior:** VE R1 + DR R1 is correct for a CR13 encounter intended as a TPK; the overwhelming first round IS the design. Most consistent with existing encounter intent.
     **Do not auto-fix without human sign-off.** Suggestion: option (a) is a low-risk editorial that improves narrative without changing mechanics; recommend applying.

  3. **FI-174 (NEW — FEEL): STD-A AR never fired in this 3-round simulation** (stagger held R1 and R3; only 1 upright PC when STD-A had free AR access in R2). STD-A's defining ability was unused every round. With 4 thralls, 2 STDs, and beholder all in the same fight, the stagger rule + fast fight pace structurally silences the lower-init STD's flagship action. **FEEL NOTE: In FC slice (7-NPC fight), the stagger rule may be overconstrained — with this much firepower the party dies whether AR fires once or twice. Consider waiving stagger for FC slice (DM discretion) so both STDs can flex AR in R1 for a more dramatic opening. This is a DM guidance note, not a spec change.**

### FI-163 / FI-164 (DESIGN DECISION): tank-wall 10th-cycle — CW-Rager synergy structurally absent; initiative collapse primary failure mode

- **Context:** 2026-05-27 04:17 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 10th cycle. Seed 494404. VICTORY R3 — Bazgar 45/49, Marwen 22/32, Sabriel 38/44. Init: Sabriel 22 > Marwen 18 > Bazgar 14 > Rager 8 > SC 6.

  1. **FI-163 (NEW DESIGN DECISION): After 10 cycles, Tank Wall has never meaningfully tested the Taunt + Call Weakness pairing.** CW was used 0/3 this cycle (Rager out of range, already in melee before SC's turn). Summary across cycles: CW fired on Rager in 1 out of 10 cycles (cycle 3, SC won initiative), and even then advantage was uncollected (Rager rolled nat-1). The slice description says "Tests taunt + call_weakness pairing" but the structural constraint (DD-41: CW only reaches Rager if SC acts first in R1, ~50% probability) means the intended test fails roughly half the time from initiative alone, and fails the other half because the Rager is dead or dying by SC's turn. **Recommendation:** Redesign the slice or change its stated intent. Options: (a) give the SC a scripted surprise-round CW on the Rager before initiative (guaranteed pairing test); (b) rename the slice "Ranged Support Only" and remove the Rager entirely, testing SC self-sufficiency; (c) add a second Rager to increase fight duration and give CW multiple firing windows.

  2. **FI-164 (NEW DESIGN DECISION): Initiative collapse is the Tank Wall primary failure mode across 10 cycles.** In this cycle: full party (Sabriel 22, Marwen 18, Bazgar 14) acted before both NPCs (Rager 8, SC 6). Rager received 44 damage before taking its first action, acting at 8/52 HP. Taunt fired but was meaningless (Rager dead R2 turn 1). This is not a rare event: the Rager has +1 Dex (low initiative baseline) and a level-5 party's Dex modifiers comfortably outpace it. **Recommendation:** Give the Rager +3 initiative (Dex ASI flavor: "pain-fueled adrenaline surge"), or run Tank Wall as a surprised-party encounter where the derro act in a surprise round.

### FI-152 / FI-153 (DESIGN DECISION): empty-void 4th-cycle — DR double-miss creates first sub-50% beholder HP; sim artifact overstates party survival; double-roll infra urgency

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 15:19 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 4th cycle. Seed 494391. TPK R5 — Bazgar −32/Marwen −43/Sabriel −37 (all down from double-VS R4-R5). Beholder 50/110 HP. Init: Beholder 20 | Sabriel 13 | Bazgar 10 | Marwen 5. Phase A 17/28 env-fail (DD-10 streak broken, same pattern as prior cycles). 2 bugs auto-fixed (FI-149 VS fear note + MQ-64 shrine_drift descent note to beholder-thrulm.md).

  1. **FI-152 (NEW POSITIVE — DESIGN DECISION): First EV cycle where beholder drops below 50% HP. Party dealt ~60 HP damage (prior record: 39 HP cycle 3).** Root cause: DR double-miss R2-R3 (d20+6=14, then d20+6=10 vs AC 15 — 16% compound event) allowed Marwen to survive and cast Scorching Ray through R3; Bazgar landed 2/2 hits in R3 (18 slashing). **This cycle establishes: IF DR misses 2+ consecutive times post-R1 AND VS doesn't recharge early, party deals ~20 HP/round and beholder could be at ~20 HP by R5–6. A party victory in EV is non-trivial but possible (~5% probability).** DECISION NEEDED: Is there any intended scenario where the party defeats the beholder in the EV slice (heroic dice scenario), or should the encounter be designed so victory is structurally impossible? The current stat block doesn't prevent it. If the beholder should be unkillable in negotiation, consider: (a) add HP, (b) add Legendary Resistance (which it already has 3×), (c) add a "retreat to the lower shaft at ≤40 HP" rule. Option (c) is most narrative — it preserves the beholder's "something deeper scares it" lore.

  2. **FI-153 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): The sim systematically overstates party survival due to chronic dispatch-vs-sim double-roll (MQ-65, 6th occurrence: MQ-25/MQ-34/MQ-49/MQ-59/MQ-62/MQ-65).** Under authoritative dispatch values, Marwen is disintegrated R1 (48 force vs 32 HP) in every cycle where DR hits — which it does ~60% of rounds. The "interesting" multi-round fights (including this 5-round cycle) only occur in the sim because the sim re-rolls damage independently. At table: Disint likely ends Marwen in R1; fight resolves in 2-3 rounds. **The sim is generating misleading data about party viability and beholder damage taken.** URGENT fix needed in dnd_roller/Phase B sim: parse the dispatch output's damage number rather than re-rolling. This is the same issue as MQ-34 (noted as HIGH priority in final-confrontation section). Outside cron blast radius — human must fix the infrastructure.

  3. **FI-148 (4th EV confirm):** Negotiation dead-end structural — all four failure modes logged (cycle 1: VS wipe; cycle 2: partial window, relic absent; cycle 3: Persuasion 18 succeeds but shaft blocks; cycle 4: Persuasion fails outright). No new angle this cycle. **Human must decide Interaction Notes fix before encounter goes to table.**

### FI-145 (DESIGN DECISION): shardcaller-team 7th-cycle — SC clustering enables Fireball wipe; scatter positions?

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 14:15 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 7th cycle. Seed 494390. VICTORY R4.

  1. **FI-145 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): Should shardcallers start scattered to prevent single-Fireball wipe?** 7 SC-team cycles: in 6 of them Fireball hits all 3 SCs (clustered in back chamber), dealing average 28 fire and reducing 2+ SCs below 10 HP before they act. This cycle (21 fire) is the only exception, and the 4-round fight that resulted was the most interesting SC-team cycle in the series. Root cause: the chamber description doesn't specify SC starting positions, so the sim defaults to "clustered 50 ft back." At table, tactical DMs might scatter SCs naturally; the sim doesn't. **Options:** (a) Add explicit positioning note to _overview.md or shardcaller.md: "SCs should start no closer than 15 ft to each other — Fireball's 20-ft radius cannot catch all 3 if spaced correctly." This is a pure positioning doc fix with no mechanical change. (b) Give SCs Evasion passive. (c) Raise HP to survive average Fireball. Option (a) is lowest-effort and most realistic. **Human decision needed: is SC clustering by design, or should they spread?** Tactical answer: SCs should spread (they're ranged kiting skirmishers, not melee blocks). Story answer: they might cluster near the shrine. **Do not auto-fix.**

  2. **DD-18 (7th confirm — ESCALATION): Marwen's Fireball remains the structural fight-decider in all SC-team cycles.** Seven cycles: 6 = 2-round fight (Fireball R1 drops 2 SCs), 1 = 4-round fight (low Fireball roll). The encounter resolution is overwhelmingly determined by one die roll in R1. This is a valid data point for the user to weigh against option (a) above.

### FI-143 (DESIGN DECISION): solo-rager-rush 9th-cycle — Slow too effective vs ragers; Wis save proficiency question

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 13:19 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 9th cycle. Seed 494389. VICTORY R3.

  1. **FI-143 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): Should derro-ragers have Wis save proficiency?** Current ragers have no Wis save proficiency (+0 assumed). All 3 failed DC15 Slow saves in R1 (rolls 2, 3, 3 — 34% all-fail event at +0). With Wis proficiency (+4), DC15 requires a natural 11+, making all-fail 12.5% — rarer but still possible. Thematically, derro-ragers have Madness Endurance (pain tolerance, not psychic clarity), so low Wis (+0 or negative) is flavor-correct. **The question is whether Slow should be a reliable tool vs ragers at table.** At +0: ~70% single-fail rate means DM can reliably debuff 1-2 ragers per cast. At +4: ~50% single-fail rate, feels riskier. If the table dynamic should punish wizards who "waste" a 3rd slot on Slow, add proficiency. If Slow should be a valid alternate play (as FI-82 and this cycle suggest), keep +0. **Human decision. Do not auto-fix.**

  2. **FI-141 / FI-96 continued (design gap): Berserk recharge fires but is anticlimactic.** Rager-B recharged Berserk (d6=6 R3) and swung all-miss (1, 2, 5 vs 18/15/19 ACs, ~5% event). The recharge mechanic works; the feel depends on RNG. At table, a all-miss recharged Berserk needs DM narration ("three wild swings carve air") to land. No fix needed — note for DM prep.

### FI-130 (sim/MQ-61) / FI-131 / FI-132 (NEW kill pattern) / FI-133 / FI-134 / MQ-61 / MQ-62: final-confrontation 8th-cycle — TPK R3; double-AR sim bug; back-to-back Disint; lair kills Sabriel; party deals 38 dmg (most in FC history)

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 12:21 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 8th cycle. Seed 494388. TPK R3 — Beholder 76/110 HP (38 dmg taken). Init: STD-B:25, T2:21, T4:20, Sabriel:15, Marwen:14, T1:11, Bazgar:10, STD-A:9, Beholder:8, T3:5. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 33rd consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-130 (NEW — sim harness / MQ-61): Stagger rule violated when STD-B has higher init than STD-A.** STD-B init 25, STD-A init 9. The sim evaluates stagger at STD-A's block (init 9), but STD-B already fired AR at init 25. Result: double-AR fires in R1 (STD-B + STD-A both used AR). The stagger rule text says "evaluated at START of round, before any actions resolve." At table this is correctly handled by the DM; the sim needs a pre-round stagger check before the first combatant acts each round. This is a sim harness issue — the actual game rule is fine. Recommend fixing in the next sim iteration.

  2. **FI-131 (NEW — feel/DM note): Sabriel LoH revive → immediate Disint kill of Marwen.** Sabriel spent her R2 action reviving Marwen (10 HP via LoH). Beholder's next action (Disint recharged d6=6 in R2) immediately killed Marwen again. The "revive-and-die" loop is mechanically correct and narratively brutal — this is the intended despair moment. **Add DM note to beholder.md tactics:** "If Sabriel just revived Marwen at low HP (<15), prioritize Marwen for Disintegration on the next main action. This creates the 'you cannot save her' moment — do not soften this. The correct cruel play exposes the futility of reviving under Disint pressure." Low-risk doc addition, no balance change.

  3. **FI-132 (NEW POSITIVE — kill-feel): First FC cycle where lair action delivers a killing blow.** Sabriel (5 HP after DD + STD-B AR stripping) was one-shot by Void Eruption R3 (13 force, fail save). Previously all FC kills were from Disintegration, Void Scream, or thrall/STD attacks. The lair-kills-Sabriel pattern feels earned: she was methodically weakened by Drain Divinity (R2 stripped L2) and STD-B AR before the altar finished her. This is the most narratively coherent FC death sequence in 8 cycles. No fix needed — positive finding.

  4. **FI-133 (NEW — feel/positive): Party dealt 38 HP to beholder (most in any FC cycle).** Marwen's Scorching Ray (3 hits, 27 fire R2) after being revived by LoH was a meaningful counterplay moment. The fight had genuine two-sided pressure. Beholder at 76/110 HP is a visible path to a 4–5 round kill if party could sustain. **Consider adding a DM encouragement note:** "At table, call out the Scorching Ray sequence — 'three lines of fire score across its hide.' This validates the party's output even in a losing fight."

  5. **FI-134 (NEW — feel/DM note): STD multiattack vs high-AC Bazgar (AC18) whiffed 0/4 times before Bazgar was VE-softened.** STDs need either AR (save-based) or VE lair support to threaten Bazgar. Recommend adding tactic note to shrine-touched-derro.md: "When Bazgar (AC18) is the last standing PC and AR is on cooldown, signal the lair action — narrate the altar pulsing as DM cue. VE's Dex save is more reliable than multiattack vs high AC." Low-risk doc addition, no balance change.

  6. **MQ-61 (NEW — sim harness): Pre-round stagger check.** Must fire before any combatant acts. Current sim evaluates at STD-A's block (mid-round) — fails when STD-B has higher initiative. Correct implementation: identify which STD acts first in initiative order; at round start, if both STDs have AR available, mark the LOWER-INIT STD as holding. This mirrors the at-table DM check.

  7. **MQ-62 (NEW — dispatch/sim dice gap, pattern continuation): Void Eruption sim dice differ from dispatch dice.** VE dispatch showed 10 force; sim independently rolled 4 (Bazgar) and 13 (Sabriel). For Sabriel (5 HP), outcome same regardless. This continues the known pattern (MQ-34, MQ-49, MQ-59). Harness limitation — not a bug, not fixable without merging dispatch + sim dice systems.

  8. **DD-33 (8th FC confirm): STDs consistently win high initiative in FC.** STD-B init 25, STD-A init 9 this cycle. The beholder (init 8) fires late. High-init STDs create devastating R1 pressure before party acts. Party has never had a "won initiative" R1 in 8 FC cycles. This is by design (overwhelming pressure), but DM should note that STD-B winning init 20+ (probability ~30%) essentially decides the fight in the first two actions.

### FI-125 / FI-127 (DESIGN DECISION) / FI-128 / FI-129 / FI-56 3rd-confirm / MQ-59 / MQ-60: beholder-escorts-limited 3rd-cycle — TPK R8; LOH loop; VS recharge question; Drain Divinity tactic gap

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 11:20 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 3rd cycle. Seed 494387. TPK R8 — Beholder 51/110 HP. Init: Thrall-1: 19 | Sabriel: 9 | Thrall-2: 9 | Bazgar: 7 | Marwen: 7 | Beholder: 5 | Thrall-3: 5. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 32nd consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-125 (NEW — feel/tactic gap): Sabriel LOH revival loop dominates.** Sabriel used Lay on Hands every single round R3-R8 to revive Marwen, never attacking the beholder after R1. Six identical turns. Mechanically correct (LOH void-safe, 1 HP pool point, costs action). The beholder wins by eventually killing Sabriel (R8 tentacle) whereupon Marwen has no reviver. **Recommendation (tactic note in beholder.md): "If Sabriel appears cycling LOH each turn, spend 1 legendary (Tentacle, 1 LA) targeting Sabriel specifically at the end of her turn — pressure her HP to force self-healing rather than ally-healing. LOH cannot be stopped by game mechanics but the beholder can make Sabriel spend it on herself." Low-risk authoring fix, no balance impact.**

  2. **FI-127 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): Void Scream recharge frequency question.** VS recharged on turn 1 (roll: 5 = not yet) and fired R2 (roll: 6 = recharged). After R2, rolled 5/2/5/2/2/1/5/4 across 8 turns — never recharged. VS shaped the entire fight (Bazgar frightened R2-R8, Sabriel took 17 psychic) then was absent for 6 rounds. **Design question:** Is VS intended as a once-per-fight swing (recharge-6 ≈ 1-2 fires per full fight, with suspense between fires) or a recurring threatening ability (recharge 5-6 ≈ 2-3 fires, sustained pressure)? Current recharge-6 creates one dramatic moment and long silence. If sustained fear pressure is desired, raise to recharge 5-6. **Human decision needed — do not auto-fix.**

  3. **FI-128 (NEW — tactic doc fix): Drain Divinity dead-weight once only L1 slots remain.** DD fired once (R1 strips Sabriel's last L2), then the beholder had no valid L2+ targets for the remaining 7 rounds. DD on L1 costs 3 legendary actions for +2 temp HP; Void Ray (2 LA) does 22 avg damage — clearly better. Current beholder.md Tactics say "burn legendary on Drain Divinity" but don't specify the threshold. **Add clarifying note: "Drain Divinity worth 3 LA only when target has L2+ slots remaining. Once highest available slot is L1, switch to Void Ray instead." Can auto-apply next cycle if human approves.**

  4. **FI-129 (NEW — lair feel/doc fix): Lair action monotony post-thrall-wipe.** Void Eruption fired 4× in a row (R2-R5), then Unstable Ground 3× (R6-R8). At-table this would feel repetitive. **Add lair-priority note to beholder.md start-of-turn checklist:** "Lair rotation: Void Eruption if 2+ PCs near altar; Unstable Ground on active melee threat (especially if grappled); Manifest Thralls if HP > 70 and delay is useful. Avoid same choice 3+ consecutive rounds." Can auto-apply next cycle if human approves.

  5. **FI-56 (3RD CONFIRM — sim harness, DD-11 URGENT pending): Maw autocrit on grappled not enforced.** R3: Tentacle2 grapples Bazgar (15 HP), Maw misses (11 vs AC18, no autocrit triggered). R6: Tentacle1 grapples Bazgar (6 HP), Maw lands (24 vs AC18) — sim applied 19 piercing. Should be autocrit (2× 4d8+3, avg ~47). Bazgar would have died R3 rather than R6. At-table the encounter is MORE lethal than simulated. DD-11 (grapple+Maw autocrit structural) — third confirm in 3rd-cycle beholder-escorts run. **Human sign-off on DD-11 still needed: is this intended? The autocrit + 4d8+3 on a grappled L5 fighter (49 HP) is near-instant-kill.**

  6. **MQ-59 (sim harness): void_eruption save type confirmed Dex.** Sim used DC 14 Str; DB outputs DC 16 Dex. No push rider in DB. Correct for table: DC 16 Dex save, no push. Sim fix needed next cycle.

  7. **MQ-60 (spec gap): compel_thrall and thrall resistance saves use inconsistent stats.** compel_thrall DB spec: "[ASK PLAYER: DC 16 Cha save]" (for PCs). thrall-derro.md: thrall ordered against another derro makes "DC 14 Wis save." Two different save types, two different DCs, in two different files. Needs single-pass authoring clarification: what happens when beholder compels a thrall toward a PC (does the thrall save?), and separately, what happens when a thrall is ordered to attack another derro (DC 14 Wis per thrall.md). Current DB spec doesn't model either scenario.

### FI-120 (POSITIVE) / FI-121 (MILESTONE) / FI-122 / FI-123 / FI-124 (POSITIVE) / DD-24/DD-26/DD-41 confirms / MQ-57/MQ-58: tank-wall 3rd-cycle — VICTORY R2; first CW-R1 + first Berserk in tank-wall history; Sabriel untouched 3rd cycle; sim harness bugs

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 10:19 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 3rd cycle. Seed 494386. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 38/49, Marwen 15/32, Sabriel 44/44. Init: SC 14 | Marwen 10 | Rager 9 | Bazgar 7 | Sabriel 3. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 31st consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

The Taunt + CW R1 combo coexisted correctly. **Recommend adding tactic note: "CW on Rager is only viable R1 when SC acts before Rager.   2. **FI-121 (NEW MILESTONE — DD-26 first positive data): Berserk fires for first time in 3 tank-wall cycles (R2).** Rager entered R2 at 3/52 HP, 3 PCs in reach, no movement that turn.   5. **FI-124 (NEW POSITIVE — feel): SC Barrage R1 threatens Marwen for first time in tank-wall.** SC acted first (init 14), fired Barrage before Marwen: Marwen fails DC13 save, takes 12 piercing → 20/32 HP entering R2.   6. **DD-24 (3rd tank-wall confirm): Taunt + Fireball bypass — Marwen taunted, casts Fireball anyway.** Taunt's disadvantage on attack rolls does not affect save-based spells. No new information; pattern confirmed.

  7. **DD-26 (continued — 4th tank-wall cycle): Fight ends R2 even with Berserk firing.** Bazgar's R1 burst (Precision Attack advantage + smite = 37 total) reduces Rager to 3 HP. ### FI-114 (Phase A env) / FI-115 (UF 3rd confirm) / FI-116 (fire suppression 2nd confirm) / FI-117 (OBR miss self-damage) / FI-119 (shrine-wedge undertuned) / MQ-54 (cron cache) / MQ-55 (OBR+UF ruling) / MQ-56 (stagger mid-round recharge): shrine-wedge 3rd-cycle — VICTORY R2; Phase A failed network-blocked container; structural findings confirmed

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 09:19 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 3rd cycle. Seed 494385. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 36/49, Marwen 32/32 (untouched), Sabriel 40/44. Init: STD-Beta 19 | Sabriel 17 | Bazgar 16 | Marwen/STD-Alpha 9. **Phase A: 17/28 FAILED** (first failure in cron history — environmental, not spec errors). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-114 (NEW — infrastructure): Phase A failed 17/28 — first Phase A failure since cron started (DD-10 streak broken).** Root cause: fresh ephemeral container, no pre-seeded `~/.cache/dnd_roller/quant_numbers.bin`, `QUANT_API_KEY` unset, random.org blocked (HTTP 403). All 17 failures are dice-rolling actions (single_attack/multiattack/area types); all 11 utility/non-dice actions passed. No spec errors. **Two remedies (human decision): (a) add a Python `random` pseudo-random fallback in `dnd_roller._ensure_numbers()` for cron/test contexts — easy, low-risk, keeps cron healthy; (b) commit a pre-seeded cache binary to the repo so containers clone it — more bytes in repo but zero code change. Option (a) recommended.** Outside cron blast radius (scripts/dnd_roller.py). See MQ-54.

  2. **FI-115 (3rd structural confirm — FI-80): Unstable Form activated but never used.** 3rd consecutive shrine-wedge cycle. STD-Alpha took 19 damage in R1 (≥10 threshold triggered correctly), but was beaten to 1 HP in R2 before acting with UF advantage, then downed by SG aura. **Pattern is confirmed across 3 cycles: UF triggers but STD doesn't survive to use it.** DM should be aware UF is a "rare, spectacular moment" mechanic — not a reliable per-round feature. If it should fire more often, lower the trigger threshold (10 → 7 damage) or give it immediate effect (reaction, vs next-turn-only current behavior).

  3. **FI-116 (2nd structural confirm — FI-81): Fire vulnerability suppression zero-impact.** Fireball (8d6=25) killed STD-Beta R1 even without vulnerability doubling. For the altar-pull puzzle to be discoverable by players, the STDs need to survive long enough for positioning to matter. With 45 HP STDs facing a level-5 Fireball, the fight resolves before terrain strategy emerges.

  4. **FI-117 (NEW — design question): OBR self-damage on miss is a meaningful STD liability.** Both OBRs this cycle missed (vs AC 19 and AC 15); self-damage totaled 6 psychic across 2 misses. Without self-damage, STD-Alpha would have had 35 HP entering R2 instead of 29, potentially surviving 1 extra round. The .md is explicit ("regardless of whether the attack hits") — so this appears intentional. **If intentional: add a DM callout in the .md noting that OBR is a calculated risk vs high-AC PCs (Sabriel AC 19 → OBR hits ~25% of the time, self-damages 100% of the time; each miss costs the STD an expected ~2.5 HP). If unintentional: change effect to "self-takes 1d4 psychic only on a hit."**

  5. **FI-119 (NEW — balance): Shrine-wedge (2 STDs) undertuned for Level 5 party with stagger fix applied.** Cycle summary: Cycle 1 = TPK (stagger bug; double-AR was a sim error, not balanced design); Cycle 2 = VICTORY R3; Cycle 3 = VICTORY R2. With stagger working, 2 STDs deal ~12 total damage to the party before dying. Resources cost: 1 L3 + 1 L2 + 1 L1 slot + Action Surge — all recoverable on a short rest. **DESIGN DECISION: If shrine-wedge is meant to be a meaningful challenge (not just a warm-up), options: (a) 3× STDs (cheapest, most raid-like); (b) add 1 thrall-derro as a distraction; (c) add altar lair action (2d6 necrotic, 30-ft burst, Dex DC 13 save, every other round — supported by existing shrine-bound lore); (d) accept 2-STD slice as "atmosphere encounter" — sets tone, doesn't tax resources, lets players feel the altar zone mechanics before the beholder.**

  6. **MQ-54 (NEW — cron infra): Phase A dice-actions need a Python fallback in `dnd_roller._ensure_numbers()`.** See FI-114 above. No fix applied this cycle (outside cron blast radius).

  7. **MQ-55 (NEW — rules ambiguity): Does UF advantage apply to OBR reaction attacks?** .md says "advantage on ALL attacks until end of its next turn." If "all attacks" includes reactions, OBR with UF is substantially more dangerous (~45% hit vs Sabriel AC 19 with advantage vs ~25% without). Current sim assumed NO (UF only applies to action attacks). **Recommend adding "including reaction attacks if UF is active" or "UF does not apply to reaction attacks" to the shrine-touched-derro.md UF description.**

  8. **MQ-56 (NEW — rules ambiguity): Stagger rule mid-round recharge.** If STD-Alpha recharges AR mid-round (on its own turn) while STD-Beta already has AR, should the stagger rule apply and force Alpha to hold? Current .md: "stagger is evaluated at START of the round." This implies mid-round recharges can fire freely. **Recommend adding: "A mid-round recharge is NOT subject to stagger evaluation — fire it immediately if the tactical conditions apply. Stagger is START-of-round only."**

### FI-109 (POSITIVE AUTO-FIXED) / FI-110 / FI-111 (DD-39 NUANCE) / FI-112 / FI-113 / MQ-52 / MQ-53: threshold-patrol 7th-cycle — VICTORY R3; MQ-41 validated; triple-barrage 2.8% event; DD-39 root-cause corrected; CW structural gap confirmed

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 08:15 UTC, slice #0 (threshold-patrol) 7th cycle. Seed 494384. VICTORY R3 — Bazgar 27/49, Marwen 15/32, Sabriel 35/44. Init: SC-X 22 | DW-A 16 | Marwen 16 (tie) | Sabriel 14 | Bazgar 8 | DW-B 6. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 30th consecutive). 1 bug auto-fixed (corridor-Barrage trigger note added to derro-shardcaller.md).

Barrage R1 is the correct DM default in narrow corridor approaches; distributes pressure to PCs normally protected by DW focus-fire.   2. **FI-110 (NEW — exceptional RNG): Triple-Barrage (3 consecutive fires) via back-to-back recharge d6=6, d6=5. Joint probability ~2.8%.** Unprecedented in any TP cycle. Total output 25 piercing across 3 fires (Bazgar −21, Marwen −17, Sabriel −9). Marwen at 15/32 entering R4 (fight ended R3) — genuinely threatened for first time in TP history. No spec change needed — Recharge 5-6 is correct. This is a meaningful high-variance event, not a design flaw.

  3. **FI-111 (NEW — DD-39 ROOT CAUSE CORRECTION): DW-A acted for first time in 7 cycles (init 16); 0 damage output even with CW advantage.** DD-39 pattern (DW-A always pre-turn casualty) was attributed to low initiative in prior analysis. This cycle disproves the initiative-only explanation. DW-A acted at initiative 16 (3rd overall), had CW advantage on both attacks — and still missed twice (AC 18 vs +2 to-hit; need 16+ even with advantage). Root cause is DW-A's melee accuracy vs level-5 PC ACs (18-19), not initiative. DW-A is structurally unable to contribute damage against these PCs regardless of when it acts. **DESIGN DECISION: Is DW-A's role as a combat-ignorable "damage sponge" intentional? If not, options: (a) raise DW-A to-hit to +4 (matching crossbow); (b) give DW-A a conditional ability (readied shot) that fires regardless of initiative; (c) accept DW-A as a narrative threat/lore element with no mechanical bite at level 5.**

  4. **FI-112 (NEW — structural): CW advantage on DW-A zero conversion (2nd cycle).** CW advantage applied correctly (before DW-A's R1 turn this cycle, since SC-X init 22 > DW-A init 16). Both attacks still miss. Across 7 TP cycles: CW on DWs converted 1 hit total (cycle 6, FI-73). The structural issue: DWs only target high-AC melee PCs (Bazgar AC 18, Sabriel AC 19). +2 to-hit + advantage = ~36-44% hit chance against AC 18. CW is near-worthless as a force-multiplier in this formation. No spec change needed, but DM should be aware CW is low-EV here.

  6. **MQ-52 (NEW — harness): Barrage R2+ targeting switches to Bazgar+Marwen rather than Bazgar+Sabriel. Reasonable as positioning changes. No fix needed.**

  7. **MQ-53 (harness note): dispatch barrage dmg (quantum cache) ≠ sim barrage dmg (local random). Expected dual-source behavior. No bug.**

### FI-99 (NEW) / FI-100 (NEW) / FI-101 (NEW) / FI-102 (NEW) / DD-18 (7th SC-team confirm — ESCALATION) / MQ-48 (NEW): shardcaller-team 6th-cycle — VICTORY R2; triple-barrage R1 first occurrence; Marwen downed; CW structurally unworkable; DD-18 escalation

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 06:18 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 6th cycle. Seed 494382. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 9/49, Marwen DOWN (−3 HP), Sabriel 18/44. Init: Marwen 20 | SC-A/B 18 | Sabriel 17 | SC-C 6 | Bazgar 4. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 26th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-99 (NEW — NOTABLE): First triple-barrage R1 in any shardcaller-team cycle — insufficient to flip outcome when Fireball goes first, but most punishing SC-team encounter on record.** All 3 SCs fired Shard-Barrage R1 (no stagger enforced — each SC chose Barrage independently on seeing 2+ PC targets). Combined barrage output: Bazgar −32, Marwen −25, Sabriel −26 HP. Despite this, party wins R2 because Fireball (20 fire) had already weakened SC-B/C to 13 HP each → Sabriel kills SC-B R1 before it can act again. In R2, SC-A dies to Scorching Ray; SC-C's lone multiattack downs Marwen (7 HP) but Bazgar kills SC-C in the same round. **Finding: triple-barrage R1 is the SC formation's maximum damage output event. Even at max, a Fireball-first win is preserved — but this cycle produced a downed PC, the first in SC-team history.** The stagger rule (fire 1 barrage per round) was designed precisely to prevent this "all-in-R1-then-nothing" pattern; DM needs explicit guidance on when triple-barrage is ever the right call. **Recommendation: add to shardcaller tactics — "Triple-barrage R1 is only correct if the caster (Marwen) has NOT yet acted this round (i.e., acts after all SCs in initiative). If Marwen went before SCs and Fireball was cast, 1 barrage per SC is enough for R1; save remaining 2 for R2–R3 when party is weakened and barrage recharge is unknown."**

  2. **FI-100 (NEW): All 9 CW charges spent R1, 0 effective outcomes — triple-barrage makes CW invalid.** Each SC used CW on an ally. Per the tactics: "Do not Call Weakness an ally who plans to use Shard-Barrage this turn — Barrage is a save-based area effect (no attack roll), so the advantage is wasted." In a triple-barrage R1, every SC uses Barrage → every CW target is a Barrage-user → all 3 CW bonuses are wasted. Additionally, SC-B/SC-C both called on SC-A, violating the "stagger targets — don't double-buff the same ally" rule (see MQ-48). **Authoring recommendation (low-risk): add to tactics — "If all 3 SCs fire Barrage R1, hold ALL Call Weakness charges for R2. There are no valid CW targets in a triple-barrage round. Spend CW R2 on surviving SCs using multiattack."**

  3. **FI-101 (NEW): First downed PC in shardcaller-team history — Marwen DOWN (−3 HP) from SC-C Throw 1 R2.** Prior cycles ended with Marwen at 5–28/32 HP. This cycle: Marwen at 7/32 entering R2, taken out by 10 piercing. The chain that enables this: (a) triple-barrage R1 reduces Marwen to 7 HP; (b) Marwen wins R2 initiative, kills SC-A with Scorching Ray; (c) SC-C survives to act, targets Marwen (caster priority). The party has Sabriel's 20 LoH available — workable, but the resource cost is now real (LoH spent, Bazgar at 9/49 going into whatever follows). **Observation: triple-barrage is the mechanic that makes SC-team dangerous even when Fireball goes first. The rarity (first occurrence in 6 cycles) is because SC stagger tactics correctly prevent it most of the time — and when stagger fails (all-in-R1), the SCs sacrifice R2 coverage.**

  4. **FI-102 (NEW — structural, nth DD-18 confirm from new angle): CW stagger impossible once Fireball kills SCs before their turns.** SC-A (init 18) died R2 before acting — Scorching Ray from Marwen (init 20). Both CW boosts assigned to SC-A (from SC-B and SC-C in R1) were wasted. The "prefer highest-init alive ally" rule correctly pointed to SC-A. The rule can't help when the highest-init ally is killed by the caster who goes before SCs. **Root fix: DD-18 (terrain constraint or HP buff). No independent fix for FI-102.**

  5. **DD-18 (7th SC-team cycle confirm — ESCALATION):** Marwen init 20, Fireball R1, fight shaped before SCs act. Seven consecutive SC-team cycles; six with Marwen-first Fireball. Only cycle 4 broke the pattern (Marwen lower init). **ESCALATION: seven cycles is a large enough sample to declare DD-18 a structural feature of the encounter as designed. This cron will continue logging DD-18 confirms but will NOT raise additional detail per-cycle unless a new angle emerges. Human must decide on DD-18 implementation before next shardcaller-team cycle. Options: (a) terrain column constraint (Fireball max 2 SCs); (b) SC HP buff to ~45; (c) accept the pattern as a feature of this encounter zone.**

  6. **MQ-48 (NEW — sim harness): Double-CW on SC-A not prevented.** SC-B and SC-C both used CW on SC-A in R1. The sim's CW logic picks "highest-init living ally ≠ self" without tracking whether that ally was already CW'd this round. Result: `cw_advantage["SC-A"]` written twice (refreshed, not stacked — toggle rule respected). No mechanical error this cycle (only 1 CW advantage was active), but the "stagger targets — don't double-buff same ally" tactic was violated. Harness-only fix: track CW recipients per round and skip already-buffed targets.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 0

### FI-103 / FI-104 / FI-105 / FI-106 / FI-107 / FI-108 / MQ-49 / MQ-50 / MQ-51: empty-void 3rd cycle — TPK R4; middle-option negotiation dead-end; beholder dead main-action turn; VE first appearance; VR+Disint set-up kill pattern

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 07:20 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 3rd cycle. Seed 494383. TPK R4 — Marwen disintegrated R1, Bazgar disintegrated R4, Sabriel down −5 HP from VE. Beholder 71/110 HP. Init: Marwen 13 | Beholder 11 | Bazgar 2 | Sabriel 1. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 29th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-103 (NEW): First EV cycle where Marwen acts before beholder (init 13 > 11) — 15 fire dealt before R1 Disint.** In prior cycles (1 and 2), the beholder won initiative and Disint'd Marwen before she acted. This cycle reversed the order. Marwen's 2/3 Scorching Ray hit for 15 fire, reducing beholder to 95/110 before Disint fired. The beholder's Disint still connected and Marwen still died R1 — the 15 fire dealt had zero impact on the beholder's ability to one-shot her. **Finding: initiative order changes the FEEL of R1 but not its mechanical outcome in EV.** The beholder's Disint (+6 to-hit vs AC 15 = ~55% base hit rate plus prior VR softening) kills Marwen at or above full HP. No action needed.

  2. **FI-104 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): Middle-option negotiation (Persuasion 18) succeeds on dice but party lacks the relic to pay.** Both Arcana and Persuasion succeeded (24 and 18 respectively). The beholder offered: *seal one consecrated relic into the void*. Party had no relic. Combat started anyway. **The negotiation has a hidden prerequisite (relic in party inventory) that the mechanics don't reflect.** A player who rolls a 20 on Persuasion should feel the option is achievable. Currently it isn't, unless session prep placed a relic. **DECISION NEEDED:** Either (a) plant a Dulgarum relic in the preceding session, or (b) allow Sabriel's consecrated holy symbol to serve as a valid sacrifice — at cost of losing her spellcasting focus for the rest of the session. Option (b) requires no external setup and creates a meaningful player choice at the table.

  3. **FI-105 (NEW): Beholder dead main-action turn R3 — first in EV slice.** Disint d6=2 (fail, needs 5+), VS d6=1 (fail, needs 6). Beholder at altitude, out of melee range. Main action wasted. With 3 legendary spent on Drain Divinity (Sabriel saved), R3 was a near-zero damage round from the beholder. **Frequency estimate:** Disint fail rate per round = 4/6 ≈ 67%, VS fail rate = 5/6 ≈ 83%. Both fail simultaneously ≈ 55% probability per round. Dead main-action turns are statistically likely in ~half the rounds after R1. In full-encounter slices, thrall pressure fills these gaps. In solo EV, they create dead air. **DECISION NEEDED:** Does the beholder need a tertiary ranged option (weaker than Disint/VS) for dead-action turns? Candidate: a ranged Eye Ray variant (3d8 force, no save, 90 ft range) as a basic action for dead turns. Not a DB change — DM house rule.

  4. **FI-106 (NEW): Void Eruption first appearance in EV slice fires R4, both PCs down from lair alone.** 2d10=11 force, DC16 Dex half. Both PCs on critically low HP (11 and 6) failed saves — both downed. The beholder's subsequent Disint on Bazgar (0 HP → disintegrated) was overkill. **Feel note:** when the lair action kills the PCs before the boss's main action fires, it's tonally flat. DM should narrate VE descriptively ("the shrine pulses, the void reclaims its domain") so the location — not just the monster — feels like the threat. **Low-risk recommendation:** add a DM callout to beholder-thrulm.md Lair Actions section: *"VE kill-shot feel: if void_eruption alone drops PCs to 0 HP, narrate the kill as the shrine asserting dominance — the beholder is the instrument; the void is the cause."* Mark as DESIGN DECISION — editorial, not bug.

  5. **FI-107 (NEW — DESIGN DECISION): VR + Disint set-up kill pattern not documented in tactics.** After Marwen's R1 turn, beholder spent 2 LA on Void Ray (softened Marwen to 18 HP) then Disint'd her for 39 force. VR was unnecessary — Disint kills Marwen from full 32 HP regardless (39 > 32). The correct play per existing tactics: **Drain Divinity on Marwen after her R1 turn** (3 LA, strips a slot, gains temp HP, preserves Disint kill potential). Current tactics guidance says "burn LA on DD rather than VR when cleric/paladin present" — but this case is: no paladin in party (Sabriel is divine martial with slots, so DD-eligible), Marwen is the caster target. The beholder should have spent all 3 LA on DD (Marwen), not 2 on VR + 1 wasted. **DECISION:** Update tactics to add: *"After a caster's end-of-turn, if Disint is available for the beholder's upcoming action: spend 3 legendary on DD (strip slot + gain temp HP) rather than VR (damage moot if Disint kills anyway). Exception: if Disint ALREADY fired this turn, switch to VR (2 legendary) on the weakest remaining target."*

  6. **FI-108: VS R2 double-fail Wis saves — pattern confirm.** Bazgar d20+2=9, Sabriel d20+3=6. Both fail; 38 psychic each (from 6d10). This confirms the structural pattern: low Wis saves on both melee PCs + DC 16 = frequent double-fails. No action needed. Log for frequency tracking.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 0
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-26T07-20-00.md`

### FI-95 (NEW) / FI-96 (NEW) / FI-97 (NEW) / DD-14/DD-26 (8th cycle confirm) / MQ-47 (NEW): solo-rager-rush 8th-cycle — VICTORY R2; recharge/aggro-mark test objectives structurally unreachable at 52 HP

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 05:16 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 8th cycle. Seed 494381. VICTORY R2 — all three ragers eliminated by back-to-back Fireball (23+30 fire, all three fail both saves). Bazgar downed R2 by Rager-C crit Berserk (5→0 HP). Marwen 22/32, Sabriel 16/44. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded, DD-10 25th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-95 (NEW — feel):** Berserk multiattack dispatch output includes a summed to-hit total across all three attack lines (e.g. "= 39") that has no mechanical meaning — it is the sum of all raw d20 rolls plus all hit bonuses across three independent to-hit checks. DM must read each individual attack line and ignore the total. Same root-cause issue as DD-7 (multiattack combined-damage mislabeling in dnd_roller.py renderer). Outside cron blast radius; flagged for human to fix in the renderer. Low urgency — cosmetic only.

  2. **FI-96 (NEW — structural, 8th-cycle confirm of DD-14/DD-26):** Solo-rager-rush resolved in 2 rounds for the 4th time via double-Fireball (this cycle, 2026-05-24T17:19, 2026-05-23T14:19, 2026-05-23T06:19). In 8 cycles of this slice, Berserk recharge has never been tested (Berserk fires as first use R2, fight ends before any recharge roll). Aggro-mark rider (tested in R1 only, superseded by Berserk in R2+). Taunt-induced movement (bypassed by save-based AoE). **Three of the four stated test objectives for this slice have never been meaningfully exercised.** Immediate fix recommendation (no balance change needed): add a harness setup rule for this slice — "Force Berserk used at the start of R1 (Rager-A Berserks on the approach move — flavor: it charges in a frenzy). R1 recharge roll happens for Rager-A. This exercises the recharge mechanic from the first round." This costs one round of Rager-A damage but enables 3-4 rounds of recharge visibility. **Human decision on whether to implement.**

  3. **FI-97 (NEW — feel):** Aggro-mark rider is structurally subordinate to Berserk. Once Berserk is available (R2+), the rager attacks ALL PCs in reach regardless of mark, so the mark has zero effect on Berserk turns. The mark only shapes targeting during multiattack-only turns (R1 and recharge-fail rounds). In a 2-round fight with 3 ragers, the mechanic had exactly 0 rounds of visible effect. Not a spec bug — the mark is correctly designed to shape multiattack focus. But it is nearly invisible without longer fights. Consider: add a Berserk ordering note — "if the marked attacker is in reach, assign them attack line 1 (first spin target)." This preserves the aggro-mark identity even during Berserk turns.

  4. **DD-14/DD-26 (8th cycle of solo-rager-rush, 4th 2-round Fireball win):** Both design decisions are confirmed again. The recommended fix (raise rager HP to 70) remains pending human sign-off. At 70 HP: two Fireballs (avg 23+30=53 fire on full fail) reduce each rager to 17 HP — still standing, fight continues to R3. R3 gives one recharge roll, enables Madness Endurance stacking, and forces Sabriel's smite economy. This is the minimal change that makes the slice test-complete. **No auto-fix — balance-adjacent.**

  5. **MQ-47 (NEW — clarification needed):** Triple-Berserk R2 scenario: each of the three ragers Berserked on their own turn, all stationary. The Berserk prerequisite is "rager cannot move on this turn." If a PC uses a reaction (e.g., shove, Thunderwave aftermath, forced-movement reaction) between two rager turns in R2, does a rager that has NOT yet acted lose Berserk eligibility for that round? Per MQ-35, involuntary movement voids Berserk for the rager that was pushed. But it should NOT affect siblings who haven't moved. **Recommend adding to the Berserk DB prereq field:** `"Each rager's eligibility is assessed at the start of its own turn, independently of what happened to other ragers."` This is a DB spec clarification, not a balance change. Within cron blast radius — human confirm and the next cycle can run with `combat_action_upsert` update.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 0
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-26T05-16-30.md`

### FI-92 (SIM BUG) / FI-93 (NEW) / FI-94 (NEW) / DD-33 (8th FC confirm) / MQ-46 (NEW harness): Final-confrontation 7th-cycle — TPK R2; VS fires twice; beholder untouched 8th consecutive; initiative-driven shutout

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 04:26 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 7th cycle. Seed 494380. TPK R2 — Bazgar + Marwen down R1 (VS), Sabriel down R2 (VE + R2 VS). Beholder 110/110 HP untouched. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 24th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed. Init: Lair/STB 20 → STA 19 → T4 17 → Beholder 13 → Bazgar 11 → T2/Marwen/T3 8/6/6 → T1 5 → Sabriel 2.

  1. **FI-92 (SIM BUG — harness only, not encounter spec):** First run attempt had Beholder dict missing `"alive": True` key; the alive-check guard `npcs[k].get("alive", False)` treated beholder as dead every turn. Result: false VICTORY R2 (all escorts dead, beholder at 110/110 HP never acted). Corrected in second run by adding `"alive": True` to Beholder init dict. No .md or DB fix needed. Logged so human knows the first run's "VICTORY" was a harness artifact.

  2. **FI-93 (NEW — FEEL): Void Scream fires twice (R1 and R2) — first time in any final-confrontation cycle.** VS recharged on d6=6 in R2 (16.7% probability). R2 VS (35 psychic) killed Sabriel (7 HP after VE). Combined result: Bazgar/Marwen down R1 (VS), Sabriel down R2 (VE + R2 VS). **Effect:** when VS fires twice in R1-2, the encounter resolves in exactly 2 rounds with zero PC counterplay — not even Sabriel's R1 attack pattern runs. The encounter as designed aims for "TPK where death feels earned." A 2-round double-VS wipe feels scripted. **Recommendation (DM note, not spec change):** Add to `beholder-thrulm.md` VS tactics: *"If VS recharged in R2 and only one PC is still standing, consider holding VS until R3 or later — a Round 2 wipe via double-VS removes any narrative tension. Save VS as a finishing move after the party has had at least one action round."* This is entirely optional; RAW the beholder would fire VS when recharged. Human preference call.

  3. **FI-94 (NEW — pattern observation):** Beholder took 0 HP damage for the eighth consecutive final-confrontation cycle. In cycles where Marwen acts before the beholder (higher initiative), she fires Fireball for ~34 HP. In cycles where beholder acts before Marwen (this cycle: beholder init 13 > Marwen init 6), the beholder fires VS first, dropping Marwen before her turn. The difference between "34 HP damage to beholder" and "0 HP damage" is entirely determined by whether Marwen or the beholder wins the initiative. **The encounter's moment-to-moment feel is driven by Marwen's single d20+3 initiative roll more than any party decision.** Not a spec bug, but a structural feel observation. No auto-fix — human note only.

  4. **DD-33 (8th final-confrontation cycle confirm — STILL UNRESOLVED):** STB init 20 and STA init 19 again precede the entire party (Bazgar init 11, Marwen init 6, Sabriel init 2). Pre-PC phase dealt 9+10+10 damage from STB AR + STA multiattack to Bazgar (−23 HP), Marwen (−10), Sabriel (−10). Combined with VS (33 psychic), party was functionally decided before any PC action. Eight cycles, same pattern: shrine-touched initiative dominance renders party tactics moot. **This is the highest-priority unresolved issue in the encounter. Fix options unchanged from prior cycles. Human sign-off required before next FC cycle.**

  5. **MQ-46 (NEW — sim harness, low impact):** Sort key `(-init, 0 if pc else (1 if lair else 2))` places Lair before any NPC at the same initiative. RAW: lair actions fire at "init 20 LOSING ALL TIES" — any combatant with init 20 acts before the lair. This run: Lair fired before STB at init 20. Effect: lair prone on Bazgar resolved before STB AR. Correct order would be: STB AR (fires first, wins tie) → Lair unstable_ground on Bazgar. Total R1 damage to party unchanged. Fix: change sort key so Lair has lowest priority at any given initiative value. Harness-only; no spec change.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 0

### FI-88 (URGENT) / FI-89 / FI-90 / FI-91 / MQ-31 (AUTO-FIXED) / MQ-45: Beholder-escorts-limited 2nd-cycle — TPK R3; grapple+Maw instant-kill structural (2/2 escort cycles); Drain Divinity init-gated; Fireball output variance

- **Context:** 2026-05-26 06:00 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 2nd cycle. Seed 495379. TPK R3 — Bazgar instant-death R2 (grapple+Maw autocrit), Sabriel instant-death R3 (same), Marwen down R1 (VS fail). Beholder at 50/110 HP after party dealt 60 total damage (34 Fireball + 26 Sabriel smite). 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded; DD-10 23rd consecutive). 1 bug auto-fixed (MQ-31).

  1. **FI-88 (URGENT, escalates FI-56, 2nd consecutive beholder-escorts-limited confirm): Grapple+Maw auto-crit is a structural instant-kill on L5 Fighter in both escort cycles.** Cycle 1 (08:18 05-25): Bazgar grappled R1 → Maw autocrit → dead. Cycle 2 (this run): Bazgar grappled R2 → Maw autocrit → dead (63 damage from one multiattack). Sabriel grappled R3 → Maw autocrit → dead (65 damage). The chain is: (1) one tentacle hits a PC, (2) PC fails DC 16 Str save (fails 60% of the time with typical +2–+4 Str mod), (3) Maw on same turn is an auto-crit for ~48 piercing. Total multiattack damage on a grapple: ~63+ in one action. No L5 Fighter/martial survives 63 HP in one hit from 49 HP. **The grapple+autocrit combo is so reliable that it effectively functions as an instant-kill button once the tentacle lands.** DD-11 ruling is urgently needed: should Maw auto-crit require the grapple to persist from a prior turn? This single ruling determines whether the beholder has a reliable "end a PC" action or a melee setup that requires a turn of vulnerability. **Human must decide: (a) same-turn grapple enables same-turn Maw crit (current — very punishing, no counterplay), or (b) grapple must persist from a prior turn (slower, gives prone+Str-check recourse). This is encounter-balance-defining. Do NOT auto-fix.**

  2. **FI-89 (2nd cycle confirm FI-57, NEW angle): Drain Divinity window closed by Marwen's initiative advantage.** In this cycle, Marwen (init 21) acted before beholder (init 20). Beholder's legendary budget (3) was spent: Void Ray (2 actions) at end of Marwen's turn. Only 1 remained for Tentacle at Sabriel's turn. Beholder's own turn refreshed the budget, but then the R2 cycle repeated. The "correct" Drain Divinity window is: beholder budget = 3 at the moment a slot-holder's turn ends. When Marwen goes before the beholder, that window is permanently consumed by Void Ray. This is the scenario the tactics `.md` tries to prevent ("Do NOT split into Void Ray + Tentacle instead") — but the legendary budget is mechanically independent of narrative instruction. **Recommendation: add explicit init-conditional note to beholder tactics: "If a slot-holder PC acts BEFORE beholder in initiative (i.e., budget is at 3 when their turn ends), HOLD the full 3 for Drain Divinity — do not use Void Ray R1. The tempo loss is worth the long-term slot erosion." This is a DM habit note, not a spec change. Low-risk authoring.**

  3. **FI-90 (confirm FI-58, 2nd escort cycle): VS recharge-6 never fires in 3-round escort fight.** Rolled 3, 4 in R2-R3. Cumulative miss across both escort cycles: 4 failed recharge checks. This is the expected distribution (~29% chance of ≥1 recharge in first 2 post-R1 turns). Observation only: in encounters resolving ≤3 rounds, Void Scream is a one-shot R1 weapon only. No fix needed.

  4. **FI-91 (NEW): Beholder Fireball save creates high party-output variance.** When beholder fails DC 15 Fireball save (40% chance), party deals 34 HP to it. When beholder saves, party deals near-zero to it (this cycle: 34 Fireball + 26 Sabriel smite = 60 HP; prior escort cycle: 0+5 = 5 HP). The delta is 55 HP based on a single d20 roll. At these extremes, the beholder might actually be in danger (surviving at 50 HP, party output in smite range). **Design note: in a sustained fight, the 40% Fireball fail is a meaningful probability. If the party could get two rounds of Fireball + smite, the beholder reaches ≤16 HP range (10,000 XP) — not impossible but requires Marwen surviving R1, which VS prevents. The interaction locks: party can only win if Marwen survives VS (requires saving on ~50% chance) AND beholder fails Fireball save (40%). Combined p(favorable R1) ≈ 20%. In 20% of escort-limited encounters, the party can deal 60+ HP and have a realistic fight. Log for human: is 20% chance of a real fight the intended difficulty?**

  5. **MQ-31 (APPLIED): Init-tie note added to beholder-thrulm.md checklist item 7.** Low-risk authoring fix: "Lair actions fire at init 20, LOSING TIES — if beholder also rolled 20, beholder acts first, then lair action fires." Confirmed from RAW 5e MM.

  6. **MQ-45 (sim-script harness): Sabriel attack target hardcoded to T1.** `target_pc = "T1"` instead of `thralls_alive[0]`. In R2-3, Sabriel's attack loop targeted dead T1. She should have engaged T3 (R2) or beholder (R3). Effect: ~10 HP of missed damage to T3 or beholder. Harness-only; no spec change needed.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 1 — MQ-31: init-tie note added to `beholder-thrulm.md` checklist item 7.
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-26T06-00-00.md`

### FI-84/85/86/87 / MQ-44: Tank-wall 2nd-cycle — VICTORY R2; extreme variance; CW/Berserk pairing still never demonstrates

- **Context:** 2026-05-25 17:18 UTC, slice #2 (tank-wall) 2nd cycle. Seed 494369. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 20/49, Marwen 23/32, Sabriel 44/44 (untouched). Init: Marwen 20, Sabriel 18, Bazgar 14, Rager 13, SC 10. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 22nd consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-84 (DD-41 3rd tank-wall confirm): CW 3/3 stranded — initiative-dependent structural gap.** SC init 10 < Rager init 13. Rager charges to melee before SC acts; SC-to-Rager gap grows to ~50 ft — beyond 30 ft CW range. No other ally in range. 3/3 CW uses unspendable for the entire fight. In both today's tank-wall cycles (07:00 and 17:18 UTC), CW fired 0 times. Across all tank-wall cycles on record, CW-on-Rager fires only when SC wins initiative vs Rager (~50% probability). **The Taunt+CW pairing the slice is designed to showcase has never demonstrated together.** Not auto-fixable without repositioning SC closer or extending CW range.

  2. **FI-85 (DD-26 2nd consecutive confirm): Berserk never fires in 2nd tank-wall cycle.** Rager moved R1 → Berserk ineligible R1. R2: took 30 fire (Fireball) → died before acting. Berserk requires surviving to R2 with ≥2 PCs in reach and no movement taken that turn. The burst-fire party prevents this. DD-26 recommendation (raise Rager HP 52→~70) unimplemented. **Human decision needed before next tank-wall cycle.**

  3. **FI-86 (NEW): Extreme fight-length variance — R2 vs R9 — purely from initiative.** 07:00 cycle (SC init 21 → SC acts first, CW fires, Rager acts late): fight lasts R9. 17:18 cycle (all PCs act before any NPC in R2): Fireball + smite erases both NPCs in R2. 7-round delta driven solely by initiative. Tank-wall's design goals (taunt+CW synergy, Berserk burst feel) require the Rager to act early; in "PCs-first" inititiative rolls they are structurally unachievable. **This is the crux of DD-26: raising Rager HP is necessary but not sufficient — the fight also needs the Rager to act before the party front-loads, which is initiative-dependent. Recommend: either (a) give the Rager a +3 Dex modifier (12 Dex) so it more consistently wins initiative, or (b) accept the high variance as a feature of this encounter zone. Both options need human sign-off.**

  4. **FI-87 (DD-24 2nd confirm): Taunted Marwen casts Fireball — Taunt fully bypassed.** Marwen failed DC 12 Cha → taunted. Immediately cast Fireball (DC 14 Dex save, AoE). Taunt's "disadvantage on attack rolls vs non-Rager" does not apply to saving-throw-based spells. The Rager spent its bonus action to zero effect. Rager.md already documents this. No additional fix — confirmed structural limitation of preemptive Taunt design.

  5. **MQ-44 (sim-artifact, not a spec bug): Barrage damage re-roll discrepancy.** Dispatch returned "9 piercing" (canonical). Sim re-rolled `d(3,6)` = 6 independently. Canonical post-R1 HP: Bazgar 20/49, Marwen 23/32. Outcome (VICTORY R2) unchanged. Future Phase B scripts should parse the dispatch output damage value rather than re-rolling.

### FI-78/79 (POSITIVE) / FI-80/81/82/83 / MQ-42 (auto-fixed) / MQ-43 (NEW): Shrine-wedge 2nd-cycle — VICTORY R3; stagger fix confirmed; UF/fire-suppression still invisible; Slow > Fireball in altar zone

- **Context:** 2026-05-25 15:24 UTC, slice #1 (shrine-wedge) 2nd cycle. Seed 494367. VICTORY R3 — Bazgar 17/49, Marwen 32/32 (untouched), Sabriel 33/44. Init: Sabriel 8, Bazgar 6, STD-B 6, Marwen 5, STD-A 3. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 21st consecutive). 1 bug auto-fixed (MQ-42).

  1. **FI-78 (POSITIVE): Stagger rule correctly prevents double-AR R1.** STD-A held AR (lower init 3 < STD-B init 6). Only STD-B fired AR. R1 damage: 19 HP total (Bazgar 8, Sabriel 11). Compare to cycle 1 (double-AR, no stagger): ~35+ HP R1 → TPK. Stagger fix is working.

  2. **FI-79 (POSITIVE): 2nd-cycle VICTORY vs 1st-cycle TPK directly demonstrates stagger fix value.** The only structural change between cycles was enforcing the stagger rule. Result: TPK → VICTORY. Encounter is survivable with correct stagger. **No fix needed — confirms design intent.**

  3. **FI-80 (2nd confirm): UF structurally never fires in shrine-wedge.** STD-A took 37 dmg R1 (UF threshold ≥10 met). Sabriel (init 8) kills STD-A before its R2 turn (init 3). UF requires surviving to the next turn, which burst-heavy parties prevent. *Recommend noting in shrine-touched-derro.md start-of-turn checklist: "UF is most relevant against sustained-damage parties; burst parties will kill the STD before UF fires."* **Not auto-fixing — this is a balance/feel note, not a bug.**

  4. **FI-81: Altar zone fire suppression zero-impact in this cycle.** Marwen's Fireball R2 hit only STD-B (only survivor); STD-B saved → half fire damage regardless. Suppression only matters when fire area hits STDs that FAIL a save. In burst-focus-fire patterns (one STD dead R2), the mechanic never surfaces. This is structural, not a bug. **DM callout: Fireball is substantially better outside the altar zone (doubled on fail); party should be incentivized to pull STDs out of range before casting.**

  5. **MQ-43 (NEW): Slow vs Fireball R1 — DM guidance gap for altar zone.** Slow L3 outperformed Fireball L3 in this cycle because fire suppression + burst focus-fire made Fireball redundant. Slow removed STD-A's actions and OBR reactions for 1+ rounds, preventing ~14 HP of party damage. **Recommend:** add a sidebar to `_overview.md` or shrine-touched-derro.md: *"In the altar zone, control spells (Slow, Web, Hypnotic Pattern) outperform fire spells due to vulnerability suppression. Fireball is a trap in this room."*
