### FI-67/68/69/70/71/72 (NEW) / MQ-39/40 (NEW): Empty-void 2nd-cycle — TPK R4; Disint kills 2 PCs permanently; altitude gate blocks DD; lair monotonous

- **Context:** 2026-05-25 13:16 UTC, slice #7 (empty-void) 2nd-cycle. Seed 494365. TPK R4 — Marwen disintegrated R1 (Disint Ray), Bazgar disintegrated R4 (Disint recharged), Sabriel downed by legendary Void Ray at 9 HP. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 19th consecutive). 0 bugs auto-fixed.

  1. **FI-67 (NEW): Drain Divinity altitude gate — DD's 30 ft range fails when beholder stays at 30–40 ft.** DD is the beholder's most efficient legendary spend (3 actions, removes slots + gains temp HP). But when the beholder hovers at 30–40 ft altitude, any ground-level PC is outside the 30 ft sphere. In R1, DD was blocked all round; in R2, the beholder had to fly + shrine_drift to close, then DD fired once. With no thralls, the beholder must choose between altitude safety and DD access. The current tactics text says "DD on first PC's end-of-turn if within 30 ft" — but doesn't explain HOW to get within 30 ft while at altitude. **Recommend adding a descent-to-fire note to the beholder's tactics section.**

  2. **FI-68 (NEW): Solo beholder leaks 1 legendary per round at range.** Without thralls, the 3-legendary budget is hard to spend cleanly. Void Ray costs 2; Tentacle costs 1 but has 10 ft reach (useless at altitude). In multiple rounds, 1 legendary action went unused. With thralls, compel_thrall (1 action) fills the gap. Without: the budget routinely ends at 1/3 or 0/3 with 1 wasted. This is not a bug, but the DM should know: the beholder fights least efficiently in the empty-void slice.

  3. **FI-69 (NEW, confirms FI-56): AC 19 negates multiattack ~22% of rounds; Maw auto-crit never fires.** Sabriel's AC 19 (heavy + shield) brings each tentacle lash to 40% hit rate. In R3, all three multiattack components missed. The Maw auto-crit (grappled target) never triggered because the tentacles couldn't grapple. This is a confirmed pattern — high-AC divine martial is a hard counter to the beholder's primary melee.

  4. **FI-70 (NEW): Healing hazard + disintegration = no recovery path.** Two PCs were disintegrated; Lay on Hands cannot target a disintegrated body. The healing hazard (spell → necrotic) already removes slot-healing; disintegration removes the target entirely. Sabriel's LoH is the only healing in-combat but it's useless once a PC is annihilated. **DM callout recommended: bold warning before first PC drops.**

  5. **FI-71 (NEW): Negotiation price is structurally incompatible with party mission.** The beholder's only negotiable concession (lower shaft off-limits) is the one thing the party cannot accept. Negotiation delivers lore but offers no real choice. **Recommend adding middle-ground options (divine item sacrifice, temporary truce cost) to Interaction Notes.**

  6. **FI-72 (NEW): Lair action monotonous — only `unstable_ground` fires.** `void_eruption` requires PCs near the altar; `manifest_thralls` requires living thralls. In this slice (no thralls, party at threshold), `unstable_ground` fires every lair action for 4 rounds. The lair action suite feels like a single ability. Note for DM: if the party plays the range game, they never see the shrine's lair variety.

  7. **MQ-40 (NEW, CRITICAL): Two PC permanent deaths from Disintegration Ray in one fight.** Marwen (R1) and Bazgar (R4) were both disintegrated. No L5 resurrection option exists for either. This is mechanically correct for a CR 13 beholder, but is a table-culture question: does the user intend permanent character death to be on the table in Thrulm? Options listed in the run transcript. **Human must decide before this encounter goes to table.**

  8. **MQ-39 (NEW): Disintegration vs Void Ray — death clarity needed at table.** Disint = permanent. Void Ray/Scream/Tentacle = normal downed. The DM needs a visible tracker or a clear verbal signal when Disint fires to distinguish permanent vs temporary death. Suggest: a dedicated "disintegrated" token or a different-colored die on the miniature.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 0
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-25T13-16-44.md`

### FI-65 (NEW) / FI-66 (NEW) / FI-67 (NEW) / DD-18 (6th SC-team confirm) / MQ-38 (NEW): Shardcaller-team 5th-cycle — VICTORY R2; CW 0/9 structural; PTV disadv never consumed; Fireball-first initiative kills 2 SCs before they act; chamber layout ambiguity

- **Context:** 2026-05-25 12:00 UTC, slice #6 (shardcaller-team) 5th-cycle. Seed 494364. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 49/49, Marwen 28/32, Sabriel 44/44. Marwen rolled init 21 (highest); Fireball R1 reduced SC-A and SC-B to 2 HP each; Bazgar killed both before they acted. SC-C sole survivor hit Marwen once (4 piercing, PTV triggered). SC-C killed R2 by Bazgar (6 slashing). 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 18th consecutive). 1 auto-fix (MQ-35 applied to derro-rager.md).

  1. **FI-65 (NEW): CW charges 0/9 — 5th consecutive shardcaller-team structural impossibility.** SC-A (init 15) and SC-B (init 13) died before acting. SC-C was sole survivor with no living SC allies — CW requires a living ally target, which doesn't exist. Every shardcaller-team cycle with Fireball R1 produces this result: 2 of 3 SCs are dead before the SC turn window opens. CW is effectively a dead mechanic in any encounter that resolves in ≤2 rounds. **Do NOT auto-fix. Upstream fix: DD-18 (Fireball terrain constraint or HP buff) is the only resolution.**

  2. **FI-66 (NEW): PTV disadv set once but never consumed — 5th-cycle pattern.** SC-C's Throw 2 hit Marwen → PTV disadv on Marwen's next save. R2: Marwen used Scorching Ray (attack roll) — PTV inapplicable. SC-C dropped before any save-based NPC ability could capitalize on the disadv. The full PTV chain (hit → PTV toggle → SC fires save-based ability at disadv target) requires a fight lasting 3+ rounds with 2+ SCs alive. In R2 fights, PTV never demonstrates. **Do NOT auto-fix. See FI-33 (cycle 4 positive): PTV DID demonstrate correctly when fight lasted 3 rounds and 2 SCs were alive.**

  3. **FI-67 (NEW): Sabriel functionally sidelined in R2 — 5th consecutive last-init occurrence.** Sabriel rolled init 4 (last). R1: she attacked SC-C (1 miss + 1 hit with smite, 12 dmg → SC-C to 6 HP). R2: Bazgar killed SC-C before Sabriel's turn (Bazgar init 18). Zero contribution in R2. This is not a bug — it's the expected outcome of low initiative + fast resolution. However, it's worth tracking: in 5 shardcaller-team cycles, Sabriel has meaningful contribution only in cycles lasting 3+ rounds. **Observation only; do NOT auto-fix.**

  4. **DD-18 (6th shardcaller-team cycle confirm, ~11th overall):** SAME pattern as cycles 1-3 and 5. Marwen init 21 > all SCs → Fireball R1 → 2 SCs dead before acting. Only cycle 4 (Marwen lower init, SCs acted first) broke the pattern. At this volume, DD-18 is no longer a "finding" — it is a structural feature of the slice until addressed. Escalation: 6 shardcaller-team cycles, 5 Fireball-trivializes; ~11 confirmed across all slices total. **Human intervention required.** Options previously logged: terrain constraint (columns enforce 25-ft SC spacing, max 2 per Fireball radius), HP buff (SC HP → ~45 to survive 31 fire without save), or Evasion. No further DD-18 notes until a change is implemented or explicitly noted as accepted.

  5. **MQ-38 (NEW): Chamber layout vs Fireball coverage ambiguity.** Cycle 4 noted "Fireball hits max 2 targets (terrain constraint — columns)." Cycle 5 (this run) applied no such constraint — all 3 SCs were catchable at 60 ft clustered at the back wall. The `_overview.md` and `_playtest-runs/README.md` do not specify SC spacing in the shardcaller-team slice. Without an explicit statement, the DM and sim will reach different conclusions. **Authoring recommendation (low-risk):** Add to shardcaller-team slice description (in the rotation or a slice-scenarios.md): "SCs begin 25 ft apart, each in a column bay. Fireball can catch at most 2 SCs (one 20-ft-radius blast cannot span 50+ ft of spread). A center-of-chamber blast might catch 1 SC + party members — DM should note PC position before Marwen fires." Requires human decision on whether the terrain constraint is intended.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 1 (MQ-35: Berserk involuntary-movement voids eligibility — note added to `derro-rager.md`)
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-25T12-00-00.md`

### FI-62 (NEW) / FI-63 (NEW) / FI-64 (NEW) / MQ-35 (NEW): Solo-rager-rush 7th-cycle — VICTORY R5; R1 pre-turn death; Taunt structurally inert; Berserk all-in-R1; Thunderwave push voids Berserk

- **Context:** 2026-05-25 10:22 UTC, slice #5 (solo-rager-rush) 7th-cycle. Seed 494362. VICTORY R5 — Bazgar 41/49, Marwen 22/32, Sabriel 12/44. R1 dead before acting (init 2); R3 dead R3; R2 dead R5. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 17th consecutive). 1 auto-fix.

  1. **FI-62 (NEW): R1 killed before acting — 7th-cycle last-init elimination.** R1 rolled init 2 (last). Bazgar dealt 19 dmg (R1→33HP), Sabriel smite'd 30 (R1→3HP), Marwen Thunderwave 11 (R1→-8HP) — all before R1's turn. 7th consecutive cycle where the lowest-init rager is eliminated pre-turn by focused nova damage. This is a structural feature of the slice: with Sabriel divine smite + Marwen AoE and 3 PCs vs 3 ragers, whoever goes last at init 2 will not survive to act. Not a fix candidate — encounter design note and symptom of DD-14 (Fireball/nova trivializes slice). Confirm this pattern in encounter notes so the DM knows what to expect.

  2. **FI-63 (NEW): Taunt splitting (FI-31) correctly applied — 0 effective outcomes, 7th-cycle confirm.** R2 taunted Marwen 4 rounds (init higher than Marwen, acts before her). Pass (23), Pass (18), Pass (12=DC12 exactly), Fail (4). On the fail (R4), Marwen used Scorching Ray at R2 (the taunter) — no disadvantage since attacking the taunter. Taunt produced zero mechanical constraint the entire fight. Root causes: (1) Cha +3 wizard beats DC 12 ~65% of the time; (2) rational wizard targets the taunter with attack-roll spells → disadvantage rule doesn't apply. **Log for human:** DD-14's recommended HP bump or terrain constraint would extend the fight; Taunt's DC and targeting need a separate look if Taunt is to matter in wizard-dominated combats. Options: raise DC to 14 (saves at +3 succeed 50%), or change Taunt to specify a debuff that affects saves too.

  3. **FI-64 (NEW): Berserk fires opening round as first action for both R2 and R3 — "all-in-R1" feel.** All ragers start recharged. With 3 PCs in melee reach, both R2 (init 20) and R3 (init 11) fire Berserk on their first turn. The encounter opens with two spinning-axes AoE barrages in rapid succession. Mechanically correct; dramatically the "will Berserk recharge?" tension never materializes in R1. The recharge math (33%/round) is correctly tuned for R2+ (R2: d6=4 fail, R3: d6=1 fail, R2 recharged R3: d6=5). The issue is the guaranteed R1 free-fire makes Berserk feel like a permanent feature rather than an escalating threat. **Design note (do NOT auto-fix):** Consider whether Berserk should start in a "recently used" state (must recharge before R1 use) to force the rager to earn its AoE. Would give Berserk narrative weight ("it's ramping up") vs current "instant spin from round 1." Requires human sign-off.

  4. **MQ-35 (NEW): Thunderwave push should void Berserk eligibility — positional abstraction gap.** Marwen's Thunderwave pushed all ragers 10 ft. R3 (init 11) immediately fired Berserk. At table: R3 was pushed 10 ft away from the party — it needs to move to re-enter reach, which the "rager cannot move on this turn" Berserk constraint forbids. Simulation abstracted positions, allowing an invalid Berserk. **Authoring recommendation (low-risk):** Add to `derro-rager.md` Berserk tactics: *"Cannot Berserk on the same turn the rager was involuntarily pushed/pulled away from melee reach — it would need to move to close, violating the no-movement prerequisite. In that case, move normally and Multiattack instead."* No DB spec change — prereq text in `beholder-thrulm.md` and `.md` context only.

- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 1 (MQ-36: Scorching Ray removed from Taunt's save-based-spell exemption list in `derro-rager.md`; clarifying note added)
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-25T10-22-43.md`

### MQ-34 (CRITICAL) / FI-59 / FI-60 (POSITIVE) / FI-61 (POSITIVE): Final-confrontation 6th-cycle — Sim-artifact TPK R1; correct dispatch shows R1 survival; first DD slot strip; stagger working

- **Context:** 2026-05-25 09:15 UTC, slice #4 (final-confrontation) 6th-cycle. Seed 494361. Sim reported TPK R1 — but this is a sim artifact. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 16th consecutive). Similarly Void Eruption dispatch=5 force; sim applied 14.** Under correct dispatch, the fight runs to R2-3 TPK rather than R1. This single bug has been inflating the severity of all previous final-confrontation cycles — prior R1 TPK reports are partially artifacts. **Priority: HIGH. Fix direction: parse dispatch damage from output text rather than re-rolling. Human infra fix needed. Do NOT auto-fix.**

  2. **FI-59 (NEW — DD-33 urgency recalibrated):** With correct dispatch values, all 3 PCs survive R1 (frightened, low HP) and take their turns: Bazgar Action Surge focuses STA down to 12HP, Sabriel smites STA dead. Party has meaningful counterplay before VS hits. Prior characterization "zero counterplay window" was partly MQ-34 artifact. DD-33 fix (lower ST Dex to +1, or shrine-bound hesitation at init 15) still recommended — one STD fires AR before entire party every cycle — but urgency drops from URGENT to HIGH. Do NOT auto-fix.

  3. **FI-60 (NEW, POSITIVE): First Drain Divinity slot strip across 6 final-confrontation cycles.** Beholder spent legendary 3-action budget on DD after Bazgar's turn. Marwen Cha save: 4 vs DC 16 → FAIL. Marwen loses L3 Fireball slot before she acts. At table: Marwen must use L2 Scorching Ray (single target) instead of L3 Fireball (5 targets) for her R1 action. In a fight lasting 3+ rounds, this compounds — DD working exactly as designed. Positive signal: DD does have teeth in this slice when legendary timing is correct (fire after first PC's turn when budget is full).

  4. **FI-61 (NEW, POSITIVE): Stagger correctly enforced for the first time in final-confrontation simulation.** STB (init 23) fired AR; sim tracked `stb_ar_fired=True` and forced STA (init 17) to Multiattack instead. STA's two strikes missed Marwen (lucky). With correct stagger: only one STD AR per round. Prior cycles had broken stagger (MQ-21). This is the stagger fix working.

### FI-56 (NEW) / FI-57 (NEW) / FI-58 (NEW) / MQ-31/32/33 (NEW): Beholder-escorts-limited 1st-cycle — TPK R3; Grapple+Maw R1 kills tank; Drain Divinity phantom; VS never recharged
- **Context:** 2026-05-25 08:18 UTC, slice #3 (beholder-escorts-limited) 1st-cycle. Seed 494360. TPK R3 — beholder at 105/110 HP. 28/28 Phase A clean (DD-10 15th consecutive). No bugs auto-fixed. Init: Beholder 20 (tie with lair — MQ-31), Marwen 15, Bazgar 12, Sabriel 10.
  1. **FI-56 (NEW) — Grapple + Maw auto-crit one-shots L5 Fighter in Round 1.** Beholder R1 multiattack: TL1 hit Bazgar (15 bludgeon) + failed DC 16 Str save → grappled. Maw auto-crit vs grappled target: 8d8+3 (rolled 54 in sim, avg ~39). Total ~54 damage; Bazgar (49 HP) goes down R1 with zero further agency. The Str save (DC 16 vs +4 = 40% success rate) is the entire decision point — on fail, Fighter is removed from the fight immediately. **Design question: should grapple→auto-crit require the condition to persist from a prior turn (not same-turn), or require grappled+prone as a 2-condition setup? Same-turn grapple+crit removes all Fighter counterplay.** Do NOT auto-fix.
  2. **FI-57 (NEW) — Drain Divinity structurally stranded in 3-round beholder-escorts fight.** Fired once (R2, Sabriel Cha 19 → saved). Fight ended R3. The beholder's primary legendary attrition engine had zero net effect. In the "escorts limited" slice, 3-round TPK is the likely range — Drain Divinity's design requires multiple rounds of slot erosion. Not a bug; context note for slice #4 (final-confrontation) where Drain Divinity may finally show its teeth.
  3. **FI-58 (NEW) — Void Scream (recharge 6) did not fire across 3 rounds.** ~42% cumulative chance did not materialize. Adds to the established pattern (FI-3/35) that Void Scream is structurally unreliable in encounters resolving in ≤5 rounds. Observation only — recharge-6 is intentionally rare.
  4. **MQ-31 (NEW) — Beholder init 20 vs lair-action trigger init 20: RAW says beholder wins ties.** Per 5e MM, lair actions fire on "initiative count 20, losing all ties." Beholder rolled 20 — per RAW the beholder acts first, then the lair action fires. Sim ran lair action first (more punishing). **Authoring fix (low-risk): add note to `beholder-thrulm.md` start-of-turn checklist or `_overview.md`: "Lair actions occur at init 20 LOSING TIES — if beholder also rolled 20, beholder turn resolves first."**
  5. **MQ-32 (NEW) — `thrall-derro/multiattack` DB action type=single_attack with 1 attack.** The `.md` is clear ("single swing, no multiattack"), but the DB action name "multiattack" may mislead a DM consulting the DB. Low priority. Consider renaming DB key to `hand_axe` with "multiattack" as a verb alias only.
  6. **MQ-33 (NEW — sim harness) — Incapacitated condition not enforced.** Marwen's Hypnotic Pattern (L3) incapacitated all 3 thralls R1. Sim allowed thralls to keep acting. With correct enforcement: Marwen survives to R3 (~10 HP); fight extends 1-2 rounds; Sabriel still likely dies to Grapple+Maw combo. TPK outcome unchanged but pacing would differ. Harness-only; no spec change.

### FI-38/39 (NEW): shrine-wedge — UF and DE phantom mechanics; stagger rule callout needed (MQ-28)
- **Context:** 2026-05-25 shrine-wedge 1st cycle. Seed 494358. TPK R3. Double-AR R1 (MQ-28 harness bug — stagger rule checked mid-round instead of start-of-round). 17 total party damage to both STDs.

- **FI-39 (DE phantom):** Driven Escape not triggered. Both STDs stayed ~100% HP. Below-20 threshold unreachable in 3 rounds at party's damage output. DE is intended for edge cases (party chips a STD down before TPK) — probably correct but phantom in standard outcomes.

### MQ-27 (NEW): CW target selection — prefer highest-initiative ally
- **Context:** 2026-05-25 threshold-patrol 5th cycle. SC-X (init 16) gives Call Weakness to DW-A (init 5) in R1. Bazgar (init 14) hits DW-A to 10 HP; Sabriel (init 6) kills DW-A before DW-A acts. 5th consecutive cycle where CW is wasted on an ally who dies before its turn.
- **Root cause:** Current DD-39 fix says "only use CW if a melee ally is alive." Insufficient — the fix doesn't account for initiative ordering. DW-A having init 5 (lowest in the fight) means it is most likely to die before acting when focused by Bazgar+Sabriel.
- **Recommendation:** In `derro-shardcaller.md` tactics, add sub-rule: "When choosing the CW target, prefer the ally with the **highest initiative count** — they are most likely to survive to their turn and benefit from advantage. If two allies are available, never CW the lowest-initiative ally when a higher-initiative ally is available." Authoring-only. Low-risk. Resolves DD-39/MQ-12 structurally.
- **Sub-note:** MQ-23 (harness doesn't apply CW advantage to attack rolls in simulation) continues. Not a spec bug.
- See `_playtest-runs/2026-05-25T05-00-00.md` MQ-27.

### FI-32 (NEW) / FI-33 (NEW POSITIVE) / FI-34 (NEW) / MQ-23 / MQ-24 (NEW): Shardcaller-team 4th cycle — VICTORY R3; PTV fires first time; CW+stagger rule demonstrated; TR 0/4 structural; Fireball NOT used
- **Context:** 2026-05-25 shardcaller-team 4th cycle. Seed 494355. VICTORY R3 — Bazgar 39/49, Marwen 15/32 (LoH triage), Sabriel 44/44 (untouched 4th cycle). 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded; DD-10 10th consecutive).

### DD-14 (6th cycle confirm) / FI-31 (NEW, AUTO-FIXED) / MQ-22 (NEW): Solo-rager-rush 6th cycle — VICTORY R2; triple-Taunt MQ-5 degenerate state; Berserk too-late-again; Fireball trivializes 6th consecutive cycle
- **Context:** 2026-05-24 solo-rager-rush 6th cycle. Seed 494345. VICTORY R2 — Bazgar 27/49, Marwen 19/32, Sabriel 44/44. All three ragers destroyed. 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded; DD-10 9th consecutive).
  1. **DD-14 (6th cycle confirm) — Fireball trivializes solo-rager-rush, all mechanics untested:** Marwen's R1 Fireball dealt 32 fire to all 3 ragers (all failed DC 15 Dex save); 96 total HP removed in one action; ragers entered R2 at 20/52 HP each. Berserk fired on both surviving ragers in R2 (correct tactic), landing 2 hits total (9 + 4 slashing on Marwen). Taunt fired 5 times across R1 (2 fails, 1 success) and R2 (1 fail, 1 success) — zero mechanical effect on any round (DD-36: Fireball immune; FI-31: Scorching Ray attack rolls target ragers = no MQ-5 disadvantage). Madness Endurance applied correctly in R2 for Rager-C (+1 from R1 Fireball damage) but missed by wide margins. All three signature mechanics (Berserk/Taunt/Madness) produced zero combat-outcome impact for the 6th consecutive cycle. DD-14 fix (HP bump or Fireball terrain constraint) is now 6 cycles overdue and the highest-priority solo-rager-rush issue.
  2. **FI-31 (NEW, AUTO-FIXED) — Triple-Taunt MQ-5 degenerate state in rager-only formation:** All three ragers Taunted Marwen simultaneously in R1. Under MQ-5 ruling (already in `.md`): disadvantage only on attacks vs creatures that are NOT the taunting ragers. In a rager-only formation, ALL valid targets are ragers — the triple-Taunt produces zero disadvantage on any possible PC action. Distinct from DD-36 (save-based immunity): this is the attack-roll case where Scorching Ray targets ragers and is also inert. **Auto-fix applied:** Added "Rager-only formation corollary (FI-31)" to Multi-Taunt ruling paragraph in `derro-rager.md` — instructs DM to split Taunt across multiple PCs in rager-only encounters rather than stacking on the same caster.
  3. **MQ-22 (NEW) — Madness Endurance "last turn" timing in same-round initiative:** Bazgar (init 8) hit Rager-A (init 3) in R1 before Rager-A acted. Is Rager-A "hit last turn" when it resolves its R1 swing? Applied ruling: "last turn" = previous round, not earlier in same-round initiative. Madness Endurance did NOT apply to Rager-A's R1 attack (correct). Recommend adding to `.md` checklist: "Madness Endurance triggers at the START of the next round, not mid-round after being hit in the same round." Human confirmation needed.

### DD-33 (5th cycle URGENT) / FI-23 / FI-24 / DD-34 (5th cycle) / DD-49 (NEW) / MQ-19/20/21 (NEW sim bugs): Final-confrontation 5th cycle — TPK R1; zero party counterplay; VS R1 wipe; OBR simultaneous death

- **Context:** 2026-05-24 final-confrontation 5th cycle. Seed 494344. TPK R1 — beholder untouched (110/110 HP) for 5th consecutive final-confrontation cycle. Three AOEs landed before any PC acted: Lair VE (all fail Dex 16) + STB AR (all fail Dex 14) + STA AR (Bazgar/Marwen fail, Sabriel saves). Party HP after pre-PC phase: Bazgar 39%→10, Marwen 12%→4, Sabriel 57%→25. Then Sabriel smited two thralls, Marwen Fireball'd surviving NPCs (31 fire killed 3 thralls + dropped STA/STB to 14 HP each), Bazgar Action Surged into STA — OBR reaction killed Bazgar AND STA simultaneously. Beholder fired VS (43 psychic, all fail) — instant TPK.
  1. **DD-33 (5th cycle — URGENT) — Shrine-touched initiative dominance unresolved:** STB init 25, STA init 20. Both ahead of the entire party + lair action also at init 20 = three AOEs before party acts, every cycle across all 5 runs. This is the SINGLE most-impactful balance issue in the encounter. Pre-PC damage ranged from 43% to 88% of max HP across party members. The party cannot demonstrate any tactics, decision-making, or encounter mastery when they've taken ~70% average damage before acting. **Strong recommendation: implement one of the proposed fixes (lower ST Dex to +3, or add "shrine-bound hesitation: can't act until init count 15 in R1"). Human sign-off required. This fix is 5 cycles overdue.**
  2. **FI-23 (NEW) — R1 TPK with zero counterplay window:** The fight resolved in 1 round. No PC had a meaningful decision to make — the outcome was sealed by shrine-touched initiative rolls. Even if Fireball/smites fire (they did), the beholder's VS trivially ends the fight. The issue is not VS damage (44 avg is appropriate for CR 13) but that the party enters VS range already at <40% HP from pre-PC AOEs. Fix DD-33 first; then re-evaluate whether VS needs adjustment.
  3. **FI-24 (NEW — POSITIVE) — OBR simultaneous death is dramatically satisfying:** Bazgar's greatsword hit STA for 13 damage (STA at 1 HP after Fireball), STA's OBR killed Bazgar, then STA's 1d4 self-psychic (1) finished STA. Both attacker and shrine-touched died in the same reaction chain. Thematically resonant — the shrine consumed the derro that killed a PC. Confirm at-table intent: is simultaneous mutual death by OBR intended and acceptable? If yes, this should be called out as a signature moment in the shrine-touched tactics section.
  4. **DD-34 (5th cycle confirm) — Drain Divinity zero tactical impact in final confrontation:** Sabriel at 30 HP (>15 HP threshold from DD-42 fix = eligible target). Beholder spent all 3 legendary actions on DD. Sabriel saved exactly (11+3=16 = DC 16). Zero effect; beholder had no legendary budget for the rest of the round. VS on beholder's turn then killed everyone. Across 5 cycles, DD has never materially influenced the final confrontation outcome. This is a composition issue (fight ends too fast for DD to compound), not a spec issue.
  5. **DD-49 (NEW) — VS disadvantage blanket application: clarification needed:** Simulation applied disadvantage on VS Wis saves to ALL PCs in the chamber, assuming all within 10 ft of shrine. Actual rule: "Creatures within 10 ft of the shrine have DISADVANTAGE." In the chamber, PCs may be spread across a 60-ft area; not all are within 10 ft of the altar stone. At table, the DM must track PC positions before firing VS. Recommendation: add to beholder.md VS tactics: "Apply disadvantage only to PCs explicitly within 10 ft of the altar stone at the moment VS fires — confirm positions before spending the action."
  6. **MQ-19 (NEW — sim harness):** Lair action fires at top of round in simulation, not interleaved at init count 20. In this run: lair fired before STB (init 25), should fire after STB but before STA. Low impact (same total damage). Fix in next sim revision: insert lair at init 20 in the combatant turn order.
  7. **MQ-20 (NEW — sim harness):** Second Wind used at 0 HP (Bazgar knocked to 0 by OBR during his turn, simulation allowed bonus action Second Wind). At 0 HP you are immediately unconscious — bonus actions are unavailable. Fix: check `hp > 0` before resolving bonus actions.
  8. **MQ-21 (NEW — sim harness):** AOE damage (VE, AR, VS) rolled separately per PC instead of once. In D&D 5e, AOE damage is one roll applied to all targets. Fix: roll AOE damage once; apply uniform value to all targets.
- **Bugs auto-fixed:** none
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-24T16-19-24.md`

### DD-42 (4th cycle confirm) / FI-20 / FI-21 / FI-22 / MQ-17 / MQ-18 (NEW): Beholder-escorts-limited 4th cycle — TPK R4; DD over-priority 3× confirmed; Thrall AC-mismatch; Grapple-crit instant kill
- **Context:** 2026-05-24 beholder-escorts-limited 4th cycle. TPK R4 (Bazgar instant-death R2, Marwen down R2, Sabriel down R3/dead R4). Beholder at 21/110 HP. 28/28 Phase A clean.
  1. **DD-42 (4th cycle confirmation) — Drain Divinity over-priority still unimplemented:** DD fired 3 consecutive legendary-budget refreshes (end of Marwen R1, end of Marwen R2, end of Sabriel R3). Sabriel was at 18 HP in R2 and R3 — below the DD-42 proposed threshold of ≥20 HP. Per DD-42 fix (pending human approval), beholder SHOULD prefer Void Ray (2) + Tentacle (1) in R2+R3. All 3 DD uses succeeded (Sabriel failed all 3 DC 16 Cha saves). Despite correctness of TPK outcome, the over-priority prevents Void Ray from ever firing. **Recommendation (do NOT auto-fix): add HP threshold to Drain Divinity priority rule: "if slot-holder is ≤15 HP, prefer Void Ray over Drain Divinity." Human sign-off required.**
  2. **FI-20 — Compel Thrall targeting priority missing (AUTO-FIXED):** Thralls targeted Sabriel (AC 19) throughout — 12 combined attacks, 2 hits (total 8 piercing damage). +4 to-hit vs AC 19 = 30% hit rate. Should direct thralls to lowest-AC PC (Marwen, AC 15 → 45%). Added targeting note to `beholder-thrulm.md` tactics: direct `compel_thrall` to lowest-AC PC. Low-risk authoring-only.
  3. **FI-21 — VS Frightened rider DM reminder missing (AUTO-FIXED):** VS R1 frightened Bazgar and Marwen (both failed DC 16 Wis). Frightened = disadvantage on attacks vs beholder while visible. Marwen's R2 Scorching Ray should have been at disadvantage (already at 1 HP — wouldn't have mattered, but at table this matters). Added reminder to `beholder-thrulm.md` VS line: call out frightened each subsequent round, especially for Bazgar's melee attacks. Low-risk authoring clarification.
  4. **FI-22 — Thrall compel vs divine martial: 4-cycle near-zero damage (design question):** Across all 4 beholder-escorts-limited cycles, thralls directed at Sabriel (AC 19) have dealt minimal damage. FI-20 fix assumes "target lowest AC = most efficient." Thematic question: does the beholder prefer to harass the healer (strategic) vs the softest target (efficient)? Human preference needed. FI-20 fix applies efficiency assumption; revert if theme-over-efficiency is intended.
  5. **MQ-17 — VS Frightened + shrine_drift invisibility gap:** If beholder passes through an object via shrine_drift, does it break LoS for frightened PCs (removing disadvantage)? Recommend: treat beholder as always visible in shrine chamber unless behind actual stone wall. No authoring change yet.
  6. **MQ-18 — Bazgar instant-death from Multiattack (69 dmg from one action):** Tentacle1 (20) + Tentacle2 (19) + Maw-crit-grappled (30) = 69 damage in one multiattack. Bazgar went from 14 HP → -55 HP; total damage 104 > 2×49 HP = instant death. DD-11 (grapple-crit timing: same-action vs prior-turn) still pending. If prior-turn ruling adopted, Maw would NOT crit R2 and Bazgar might survive to R3. Human ruling needed.
- **Bugs auto-fixed:** 2 (FI-20 compel-thrall targeting, FI-21 frightened rider reminder — both `beholder-thrulm.md`)
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-24T15-18-15.md`

### FI-17 / FI-18 / FI-19 / MQ-15 / MQ-16 (NEW): Tank-wall 5th cycle — Fireball wipes before synergy fires; CW range sim bug confirmed; Rager last-init pattern
- **Context:** 2026-05-24 tank-wall 5th cycle. VICTORY R2 (Bazgar 49/49, Marwen 24/32, Sabriel 44/44 — party nearly untouched). 28/28 Phase A clean (cache pre-seeded).
  1. **FI-17 — Sim harness CW range error (R1 blocked incorrectly):** Harness computed SC-to-Rager distance as ~50 ft using a hardcoded "round_num ≥ 2" gate. Actual R1 distance is ~25 ft (party entry 0 ft, Rager at 30 ft, SC at 55 ft → SC-to-Rager = 25 ft < 30 ft CW range). R1 CW on the Rager is legal and tactically correct per the `.md`. Harness infra fix needed. **The taunt+CW synergy was never tested this cycle because of this error.** No authoring change needed.
  2. **FI-18 — Fireball trivially decides the 2-NPC tank-wall before any synergy fires:** Marwen's R1 Fireball (34 fire; both Rager and SC fail DC 14 save) one-shotted the SC and reduced the Rager to 8/52 HP. Victory in 2 rounds; no NPC landed a meaningful hit. The tank-wall slice cannot test Taunt+CW pairing if Fireball removes the SC in R1. **Design question:** Should the SC be tougher (higher HP or Evasion) to survive one Fireball? Or should the slice add a second Rager as a HP buffer? Human review needed.
  3. **FI-19 — Rager last in initiative → Taunt fires after party acts, every cycle:** Rager init modifier is only +1; it goes last ~50% of the time. When Rager acts last R1, its Taunt fires after all PC turns — Taunt's only purpose is pre-empting future-turn aggression, but PCs already acted. Additionally the Rager multiattack is wasted turn 1 if PCs have already nearly killed it. **Design question:** Should the Rager start combat in melee (within 5 ft of Bazgar) to guarantee R1 presence regardless of initiative order? Human review.
  4. **MQ-15 — Fireball radius vs NPC spacing assumption:** Catching Rager (30 ft from entry) and SC (55 ft from entry) in a single Fireball requires the blast center to be within 20 ft of both, placing it ~42 ft from entry. This requires Marwen to advance 5+ ft into the chamber before casting. Not modeled in sim — fight-start position assumed. Recommend adding explicit spacing notes to the slice 2 terrain description.
  5. **MQ-16 — Rager Taunt at 8/52 HP (confirmed correct):** Rager `.md` says "keep swinging until 0 HP." Taunt + Multiattack is always the correct play regardless of HP. Behavior confirmed correct; no change needed.
- **Bugs auto-fixed:** none
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-24T14-19-47.md`

### FI-15 / FI-16 / MQ-13 / MQ-14 (NEW): Shrine-wedge 4th cycle — UF first exercise, OBR 0/4 hits, stagger harness bug revealed
- **Context:** 2026-05-24 shrine-wedge 4th cycle. VICTORY R3 (Bazgar 10/49, Marwen 20/32, Sabriel 24/44).
  1. **FI-15 — UF exercised for the first time in shrine-wedge!** Both STDs activated UF R2 (Fireball dealt 14 fire each → 10+ threshold met). AR was on cooldown (failed recharge d6=1,2), forcing Multiattack with advantage. STD-B UF hit landed (24 vs AC18 → 9 dmg on Bazgar). Narratively compelling — dying-fury moment at 8 HP. **Positive signal.** DD-40 scenario (UF+available-AR+2-in-cone → choose Multiattack) still not exercised — AR must be available AND only 2 PCs in cone. Structurally rare: Fireball clusters PCs and AR cooldown coincides.
  2. **FI-16 — OBR 0/4 hits vs high-AC targets (+4 to-hit vs AC18/19 = 30-35% hit rate).** OBR fired correctly 4× (DD-23 fix confirmed). Rolls: 11, 10, 9, 9 — all misses vs AC18/19. OBR self-psychic (1d4 always, 2+1+1+2=6 total) outlasted the counter-swing in damage contribution. OBR feels cosmetically threatening but produces no damage vs melee fighters. Against Marwen (AC15) it would land 50%+ — but OBR fires when the shrine-touched is HIT, which happens in Bazgar/Sabriel melee. Consider: raise OBR to-hit to +6 (matching shrine-touched Prof+3 pattern) so it's meaningful vs AC18.
  3. **MQ-13 — Stagger harness simulation bug revealed.** Harness checks `other_ar_avail` AFTER the first STD's turn (when `ar_used=True` already), so the stagger condition never triggers. Prior 3 cycles' "both STDs fire AR R1" results are ALL harness artifacts — the .md stagger rule is correctly authored and would hold at-table. DM would check start-of-round state. Harness infra fix needed: snapshot AR state before initiative loop.
  4. **MQ-14 — OBR once-per-attacker-action vs once-per-hit ambiguity.** .md says "interrupts between attacks if attacker has multiattack" — implies per-hit trigger for multiattack. Scorching Ray (3 bolts) is one spell casting, not multiattack. Applied ruling: OBR fires once per attacker's action. If ruling = per-bolt, OBR would fire 3× from Scorching Ray → much more self-damage and counter-swings. Human sign-off needed.
- **See:** `_playtest-runs/2026-05-24T13-25-04.md`

### FI-14 / MQ-12 (NEW): CW dead-card pattern confirmed 4th cycle; Sabriel untouched 4th cycle
- **Context:** 2026-05-24 threshold-patrol 4th cycle. Two recurring patterns confirmed:
  1. **FI-14 — Sabriel untouched 4th consecutive threshold-patrol run.** DWs always focus Bazgar (closest melee); SC always focuses Marwen (caster priority). Sabriel takes 0 damage in all 4 runs. At table feels odd — the tankiest PC is the safest. Human sign-off needed (changes SC targeting priority).
  2. **MQ-12 — CW fallthrough when DD-39 primary target dies.** DD-39 fix (CW on ally acting next after SC in init) is correct, but in fast-party runs (Sabriel Divine Smite R1 burst), the designated DW target dies before SC acts every cycle. CW 0/3 fires 4th consecutive threshold-patrol run. Recommendation: add a fallthrough note "if primary CW target is dead before SC's turn, hold the charge for next round — never fire CW on an ally who already attacked this round." This round: DW-A (init 3) killed by Sabriel smite before SC-X (init 12). DW-B already acted (init 22). No valid CW target.
